<ol>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Serɨ serɨ Sises tamokori ton ese' asi', kin pe te'sen Tepi' pa pe iyesi'pʉ, Epʉra'an pa pe nɨrɨ kanan iyesi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Epʉra'an esi'pʉ Aisi' kʉipʉnʉ pe, Aisi' esi'pʉ Seko' kʉipʉnʉ pe, Seko' esi'pʉ Isuta mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ iyakon non kʉipʉnʉ pe,</li>
      <li>Isuta esi'pʉ Peres mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Sera pokon kʉipʉnʉ pe, Temarʉ esi'pʉ na'ne' to' san pe. Peres esi'pʉ Esuran kʉipʉnʉ pe, Esuran esi'pʉ Ran kʉipʉnʉ pe,</li>
      <li>Ran esi'pʉ Aminatapu kʉipʉnʉ pe, Aminatapu esi'pʉ Naisan kʉipʉnʉ pe, Naisan esi'pʉ Sarʉman kʉipʉnʉ pe,</li>
      <li>Sarʉman esi'pʉ Powas kʉipʉnʉ pe, Reyapu esi'pʉ na'ne' isan pe, Powas esi'pʉ Ope' kʉipʉnʉ pe, Ru' esi'pʉ na'ne' isan pe, Ope' esi'pʉ Ise'si kʉipʉnʉ pe,</li>
      <li>Ise'si nin si esi'pʉ mɨrɨ Tepi' kin pe te'sen kʉipʉnʉ pe. Tepi' esi'pʉ Saraman kʉipʉnʉ pe, Iuraya no'pʉ rʉ'pʉ esi'pʉ na'ne' isan pe,</li>
      <li>Saraman esi'pʉ Reyopowan kʉipʉnʉ pe, Reyopowan esi'pʉ Apaya kʉipʉnʉ pe, Apaya esi'pʉ Esa kʉipʉnʉ pe,</li>
      <li>Esa esi'pʉ Iseyosapa' kʉipʉnʉ pe, Iseyosapa' esi'pʉ Iseyoran kʉipʉnʉ pe, Iseyoran esi'pʉ Usaya kʉipʉnʉ pe,</li>
      <li>Usaya esi'pʉ Iso'tan kʉipʉnʉ pe, Iso'tan esi'pʉ Eyas kʉipʉnʉ pe, Eyas esi'pʉ Esi'kaya kʉipʉnʉ pe,</li>
      <li>Esi'kaya esi'pʉ Mana'sa kʉipʉnʉ pe, Mana'sa esi'pʉ Eman kʉipʉnʉ pe, Eman esi'pʉ Iso'saya kʉipʉnʉ pe,</li>
      <li>Iso'saya esi'pʉ Ise'konaya mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ iyakon non kʉipʉnʉ pe. To' eyaton non uya Esuwerʉ amʉ' a'sisa' arɨ a'tai'ne Paperan pona.</li>
      <li>Paperan pona Esuwerʉ amʉ' a'sisa' asa' to' eyaton non uya a'tai: Ise'konaya esi'pʉ Siya'tiyerʉ kʉipʉnʉ pe, Siya'tiyerʉ esi'pʉ Userupaperʉ kʉipʉnʉ pe,</li>
      <li>Userupaperʉ esi'pʉ Apaiyutʉ kʉipʉnʉ pe, Apaiyutʉ esi'pʉ Iraiya'kin kʉipʉnʉ pe, Iraiya'kin esi'pʉ Esorʉ kʉipʉnʉ pe,</li>
      <li>Esorʉ esi'pʉ Isato' kʉipʉnʉ pe, Isato' esi'pʉ A'kin kʉipʉnʉ pe, A'kin esi'pʉ Iraiyutʉ kʉipʉnʉ pe,</li>
      <li>Iraiyutʉ esi'pʉ Eriyesarʉ kʉipʉnʉ pe, Eriyesarʉ esi'pʉ Ma'tan kʉipʉnʉ pe, Ma'tan esi'pʉ Seko' kʉipʉnʉ pe,</li>
      <li>Seko' esi'pʉ Isose' kʉipʉnʉ pe, Meri taan'pʉ si. Meri esi'pʉ Sises san pe, Kʉrai tato' san pe si.</li>
      <li>Epʉra'an awonsi'kɨ Tepi', kin pe te'sen pʉ'kʉ pona, 14 kaisa rɨ itamokori ton u'tɨsa' esi'pʉ mɨrɨ. Tepi', kin pe te'sen awonsi'kɨ, to' eyaton non uya Esuwerʉ amʉ' a'sisa' arɨ Paperan pona pʉ'kʉ pona, 14 kaisa rɨ itamokori ton u'tɨsa' esi'pʉ mɨrɨ. To' eyaton non uya Esuwerʉ amʉ' a'sisa' arɨ'pʉ Paperan pona awonsi'kɨ, Kʉrai entu pʉ'kʉ pona, 14 kaisa rɨ itamokori ton u'tɨsa' esi'pʉ mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Serɨ serɨ, Sises Kʉrai entu'pʉ pantomʉ: Isanon pe te'ton kon, Meri, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Isose' pokon usauro'sa' esi'pʉ temari'mato' kon pe, e'tane to' uta'pɨtʉ rawɨrɨ rɨ, tʉumono'tasa' i'tu'pʉ Meri uya, Wakʉ A'kwarʉ winɨ.</li>
      <li>Isose' esi'pʉ ipokena' pe te'sen, mɨrɨpan ekoneka'pʉ ama'ai imari'mato' tʉuya ereutanʉ'to' pe tʉuya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pɨ' isenuminka'pʉ tʉpo, Papa inserʉʉi uyee'pʉ ipiya' iye'ne'pɨtʉ yau, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Isose', Tepi' pa rʉ'pʉ, tenari'nʉnse pʉra Meri anʉnkɨ ɨno'pʉ pe, apʉne pʉra Wakʉ A'kwarʉ winɨ imono'tasa' mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Warawo' pe entunʉ'to' iya oton, imʉre mese'tɨi' Sises tukai', apʉne pʉra tʉtonpa ton pika'tɨto' iya oton pe iyesi pɨ' to' makooi apai,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ e'kupʉ'pʉ pena Papa usaurokʉ'pʉ pu'kena' Aisaya awɨrɨ a'ku'tɨnin pe:</li>
      <li>“A'pɨ'pʉn uri'san umono'tato' oton, mɨrɨpan entuto' oton warawo' pe, mɨrɨpan esa'to' oton to' uya Maniwerʉ tukai' tawon,” ta'pʉ iya, “Papa esi upiyau'nokon” ta e'kwa pe.</li>
      <li>Isose' upakasa' uya nin si, Meri mari'ma'pʉ mɨrɨ, Itepuru inserʉʉi uya tauro'ka'pʉ awɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan uya arɨ'pʉ tiwʉ' ta',</li>
      <li>e'tane iyentu rawɨrɨ a'pɨ'pɨtʉ'pʉ iya pen. Mɨrɨpan mʉre entusa' ese'tɨ'pʉ iya “Sises” tukai'.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Sises entu'pʉ tʉpo Pe'teri'en po Isutiya yau, kin pe Era' esi a'tai, pu'kena' amʉ' uyee'pʉ wʉi enu uyepʉ winɨpai Surusiran pona,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan kon uya, “Nai airɨ mʉre, Esuwerʉ amʉ' kin pe te'ton entusa' nai? Kaiyono' epa'kasa' ene'pʉ ina uya iyentusa' ekamanin. Mɨrɨ pɨ' apurɨpɨ'se'na ina uye'sa',” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ tawon etasa' kin pe te'sen Era' uya a'tai, isewankama'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kaisa rɨ Surusiran pon kon usewankama'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Tanporo Papa ena' use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main pɨ' enupanin nan amʉranʉ'sa' tʉuya a'tai, to' ekama'po'pʉ iya, “Nai yau Kʉrai entuto' oton tasa' pu'kena' amʉ' uya nai?” tukai'.</li>
      <li>“Pe'teri'en po, Isutiya yau,” tukai' to' uya eikʉ'pʉ. “Serɨ tukai' pu'kena' uya imenuka'pʉ esi pena rɨ:</li>
      <li>“‘Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon, Isutiya yawon, Pe'teri'en pata pon kon, Isutiya yawo'nan pata ton tentakai' apata kon yau eke esa' wannɨ e'sepoto' oton, karimeru esa' esi to' esa' pe kasa umunkɨ, Esuwerʉ amʉ' esa' pe te'ton,’ tawon,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ etasa' Era' uya a'tai, tʉmaimu ennoko'pʉ iya pu'kena' amʉ' piya' to' pokon pe ama'ai te'sepoto' kon pe, mɨrɨpan kon winɨ eta'pʉ iya, mɨrɨ a'tai kaiyono' epa'ka'pʉ tukai'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon ennoko'pʉ iya Pe'teri'en pona, “Wakʉ pe mʉre mʉwarinpatʉi'. Eposa' auya'nokon a'tai, upana'tɨi' mɨsi'tʉi', urɨ rɨ nɨrɨ utɨto' pe apurɨpɨ'se'na,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Kin maimu eta tʉuya'nokon tʉpo, to' utɨ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya kaiyono' kanan enkaa'pʉ, tʉnene'pʉ kon nʉ'pʉ wʉi enu uyepʉ winɨ, mɨrɨpan pɨ' to' epori'ma'pʉ. Mɨrɨpan kon rawɨrɨ kaiyono' utɨ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan ereuta'pʉ mʉre pata epoi.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, pu'kena' amʉ' ewomʉ'pʉ ɨutɨ ta'. Mʉre si ensa' tʉuya'nokon a'tai, isan, Meri pokon pe, to' e'sekunka'pʉ apurɨpɨtʉ pe. Mɨrɨ a'tai, timamin kon yen a'koka'pʉ to' uya, mɨrɨpan kon uya irepapɨtʉ'pʉ epe'kena' ton ke: korʉ ke, a'po'nan ikɨtun, pʉrankensens tato' ke mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ karapa, mɨrʉ tato' ke.</li>
      <li>Papa uya to' pana'tɨ'pʉ to' e'ne'pɨtʉ yau, to' enna'po namai' kin pe te'sen Era' piya', mɨrɨpan kon enna'po'pʉ tʉpata kon ya' tʉron nɨ awɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>To' utɨ'pʉ tʉpo, Itepuru inserʉʉi usenpoika'pʉ Isose' piya' iye'ne'pɨtʉ yau, “Isose', e'mʉ'sa'ka', mʉre mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ isan tanʉnse ainʉnkɨ Isi' pona. Kin Era' man iwarinpa pɨ' iwɨto' pe tʉuya,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan e'mʉ'sa'kasa' uya mʉre mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ isan arɨ'pʉ ewarupɨ nau Isi' pona,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan kon uko'mamʉ'pʉ Era' uma'ta pona rɨ. Pena pu'kena' amʉ' nekama'pʉ uta'ku'tɨ'pʉ, “Umu kɨ'ma uya Isi' apai,” tawon.</li>
      <li>Era' uya i'tusa' a'tai pu'kena' amʉ' uya tennakasa', ipan pe isakorota'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya, “Warawo' munkɨ amʉ' Pe'teri'en pon kon itʉ'katɨ' asa'ron wʉipiya airon kon mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ mɨrɨ o'koi'no kon nɨ,” ta'pʉ iya, pu'kena' amʉ' uya ekama'pʉ rʉ'pʉ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, pu'kena' Iseremaya nekama'pʉ uta'ku'tɨ'pʉ:</li>
      <li>“Main useta Rama pata po, tʉuta'kwarʉkai' ukaran nɨ esi eke pe rɨ, Rʉi'serʉ esi ukaran nɨ pɨ' tʉmunkɨ amʉ' wenai, tʉpori'ma i'se pʉra iyesi, to' pʉra iyesi pɨ',” tawon.</li>
      <li>Era' uma'ta'pʉ tʉpo, inserʉ usenpoika'pʉ iye'ne'pɨtʉ yau Isose' piya', Isi' po,</li>
      <li>“E'mʉ'sa'ka', mʉre mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ isan akɨ Esuwerʉ pata pona. Kamoro mʉre wɨnɨ i'se te'san uma'ta'pʉ man,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan e'mʉ'sa'ka'pʉ, mʉre mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ isan arɨ'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan kon utɨ'pʉ Esuwerʉ pata pona.</li>
      <li>E'tane A'keras enasa' tʉkʉipʉnʉ Era' pata'pʉ ya' kin pe Isutiya po eta'pʉ iya. Enari'ke' pe iyesi'pʉ, mɨrɨ ya' ɨtɨpai pʉra. Ipanamasa' esi'pʉ iye'ne'pɨtʉ yau, mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ Kiyarari nono pona.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ ɨko'manse'na Nasare' pona. Pu'kena' ton nekama'pʉ uta'ku'tɨ'pʉ mɨrɨ, “Nasarin tukai' esa'to' oton,” tawon.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Isaan Pa'tes uyee'pʉ. Itekare ekama'pʉ iya Isutiya rɨmono'taai awɨrɨ,</li>
      <li>“Amakooi kon apai era'tɨtɨ', apʉne pʉra Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe a'ko pe man,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Isaan pʉse rɨ pu'kena' Aisaya usaurokʉ'pʉ rʉ'pʉ ipɨ': “Rɨmono' tau ka'pon ukɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨtʉ, ‘Itepuru e'ma ikonekatɨ', to'sa rɨ ite'ma ikonekatɨ',’ tawon,” ta'pʉ rʉ'pʉ ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Isaan pon esi'pʉ kiyamerʉ i'po' konekasa', o' pi'pɨ konekasa' esi'pʉ ipokʉrʉʉi pe iworo'pai pɨ'. Iti'kiyari esi'pʉ kairau amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ teusan e'ku.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' utɨ'pʉ ipiya' Surusiran mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Isutiya apai, tanporo Isotan nono piyawo' nan pata apai'ne.</li>
      <li>Tʉmakooi kon ekama pɨ', mɨrɨpan kon pa'taisima'pʉ iya Isotan tuna tʉu'tɨsen kau.</li>
      <li>E'tane tu'ke Pari'si amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Satu'si amʉ' uyepʉ ene tʉuya a'tai epa'taisiman ku'to' iya airɨ, ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon ɨsɨ ton ɨkʉi munkɨ ton! Ɨnʉ' uya apana'tɨsa' kon ayainʉmʉ kon pa nʉye'ai'ne' ekota'man nɨto' piyapai?</li>
      <li>Epetatɨ' ɨyera'tɨsa' kon amakooi kon apai ekamanin ke.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨmɨrɨ'nokon pe rɨ kɨsenuminkatʉu, ‘Epʉra'an esi ina kʉipʉnʉ pe,’ tukai'. Apana'tɨ uya 'nokon serɨ, serɨ ton tɨ' apai Papa uya Epʉra'an munkɨ oton kon koneka mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Wa'ka e'kamasa' man yʉi amʉ' mi' airɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tanporon yʉi amʉ' tepetasen pen a'tɨto' oton nɨ mɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan eno'ma apo' ya'.</li>
      <li>“Apa'taisima uya 'nokon tuna ke, amakooi kon apai ɨyera'tɨ kon pa. E'tane uye'ma'pʉ pe meruntɨ kuru uyepʉ mɨrɨ uyentaino, isapatooi arɨ uya poken pʉra e'ai'ne'. Apa'taisima iya 'nokon mɨrɨ Wakʉ A'kwarʉ ke mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ apo' ke.</li>
      <li>Sara'sara'pan ti'kiyari pi'pɨ menkato' iya ike esi itemiyatʉ yau, mɨrɨpan uya i'kwato' tʉuya apon akoroka, ta'nasi, wi' amʉranʉkʉ iya itiwʉ' ta', ipi'pɨ rʉ'pʉ po'tɨ iya tʉusenkʉ'sen pen apo' ke,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uyee'pʉ Kiyarari winɨ Isaan piya' Isotan tuna airɨ tʉpa'taisimato' pe iya,</li>
      <li>Isaan esi'pʉ ɨnereutanʉ'pai, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Upa'taisima auya ru'ku i'se e'ai', mɨrɨ pe' e'tane upiya' ɨuye'sa'?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Tɨwɨ mɨrɨ kasa rɨ iku'kɨ, serɨ pe rɨken iye'to' pe. Serɨ winɨ tanporo Papa e'to' i'se rɨ kupʉ mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨ a'tai, Isaan uya ikupʉ'pʉ imaimu awɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Inke pʉra tepa'taisima'pʉ rʉ'pʉ pe, Sises ekanwaka'pʉ tuna kapai. Mɨrɨ a'tai kuru rɨ, ka' uta'koka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya Papa A'kwarʉ u'tɨ ene'pʉ wako'wa kasa, mɨrɨpan uta'si'pʉ ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Main, Epʉn winon uya ta'pʉ, “Umu pʉse rɨ, uni'nʉnkanʉ; ipɨ' epori'mayai',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Iya'kwarʉ uya Sises arɨ'pʉ rɨmono' ta' Makoi uya i'tupɨ'to' pe.</li>
      <li>Tʉuseruma tʉpo tenta'nai' pʉra 40 kaisa rɨ wʉi mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ewarupɨ, mɨrɨpan esi'pʉ ipan pe kuru iwan pe.</li>
      <li>I'tupɨ'nin uyee'pʉ ipiya', mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Papa Mumu pe ɨwesi yau, se ton tɨ' amʉ' pɨ' pʉreti pe enakɨ ka'kɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Iye'menukasa', ‘Ka'pon esi tʉuko'mansen pʉreti pɨ' rɨken pen, e'tane tanporon nɨ main pɨ' Papa mʉta yapai tʉuye'sen,’ tawon,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Makoi uya Sises arɨ'pʉ wakʉ eke pata pona, mɨrɨpan uya Papa ena' Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' ka'tawon inakapu putu po iye'mʉ'sa'kato' pe ikupʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“Papa Mumu pe ɨwesi yau, ata'mo'kakɨ, apʉne pʉra iye'menukasa': “‘Tinserʉʉi ton apiyo'ma iya ɨpɨ', mɨrɨpan kon uya temiyatʉ kon yau ayanʉmʉ tɨ' pona a'ta wɨnɨ auya namai',’ tawon,” ta'pʉ Makoi uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Iye'menukasa' rɨ nɨrɨ, ‘Itepuru, Papa, itese' pɨ' ɨwe'to' kʉsi'tupɨtʉi,’ tasa',” ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Makoi uya kanan arɨ'pʉ ka'tawon wʉ' pona, mɨrɨpan uya tanporo eke ton pata enpoika'pʉ itenu ya', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ wakʉ pe rɨ iye'to'.</li>
      <li>“Tanporo serɨ ton ke ɨrepa uya, urɨ pɨ' te'sekunkai' ɨwɨpʉrema yau,” ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Upiyapai enta, Se'tan! Apʉne pʉra iye'menukasa', ‘Itepuru, Papa, itese' pɨ' ɨwe'to' pɨ' rɨken ɨpʉrema'; Kʉrɨ rɨ rɨken poitorʉ pe e'kɨ,’ tawon,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan piyapai Makoi utɨ'pʉ. Inserʉ amʉ' uyee'pʉ ipika'tɨi'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya Isaan esi pariki'si tau tawon etasa' a'tai, iyenna'po'pʉ Kiyarari pona.</li>
      <li>Ɨko'manse'na itɨ'pʉ Ka'paneyan pona, Nasare' tʉnɨnse. Mɨrɨ pata esi'pʉ mɨrɨ parau ku'pɨri piyau Sepuran mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Na'tari nono airɨ.</li>
      <li>Pu'kena' Aisaya uya ta'pʉ rʉ'pʉ a'ku'tɨ pe:</li>
      <li>“Sepuran mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Na'tari nono pon kon, ka'pon amʉ' Kiyarari e'ma awɨron kon mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tuna Isotan ratoi pon kon, Kiyarari, Esuwerʉ amʉ' pen nono yau te'san.</li>
      <li>Pʉsamoro ka'pon amʉ' ewarupɨ yau tʉuko'mansan uya eke rɨ iweyu ensa' man; uma'tan nɨto' nono yau te'san pona iweyu e'wei'tɨsa' man.”</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ si'kɨrɨ rɨ Sises epiya'tɨ'pʉ itekare ekama pɨ', “Era'tɨtɨ' amakooi kon apai, apʉne pʉra Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe man a'ko pe!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises usarɨ koro'tau parau ku'pɨri Kiyarari piyawɨrɨ, ka'pon ene'pʉ iya, takon ya' te'san, Saiman itese', Pi'ta tato' ipɨ', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Anturu si itakon. Tʉpunwerʉ kon tʉrʉ pɨ' to' esi'pʉ parau ku'pɨri kau, apʉne pʉra moro' amʉ' a'sinin nan pe tesi kon pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Upɨkɨrɨ ɨsi'tɨ', ɨkonekato' kon pe uya ka'pon amʉ' a'sinin nan pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe rɨ, tʉpunwerʉ kon tʉnɨnse to' utɨ'pʉ ipɨkɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ apai tʉutɨi', tʉron kon asa'ron kon ɨsirunan ene'pʉ iya, Isens mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Isaan, Sepiti munkɨ amʉ'. Kanau yau to' esi'pʉ, tʉkʉipʉnʉ kon Sepiti pokon pe tʉpunwerʉ kon konepɨtʉ pɨ'. Sises uya to' kɨ'ma'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Inke pʉra, tʉkanwa kon mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉkʉipʉnʉ kon tʉnɨnse to' utɨ'pʉ ipɨkɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Sises utɨ'pʉ siya rɨ Kiyarari awɨrɨ ka'pon amʉ' enupa pɨ' Esuwerʉ amʉ' usenupato' iwʉ' tau'ne. Wakʉ itekare ekama pɨ' iyesi'pʉ, Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe pɨ'. Paran pokon kon mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ takuru'kena' nan ka'pon amʉ' epi'tɨ pɨ' iyesi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Itekareei utɨ'pʉ siya rɨ Siriya poron pata awɨrɨ'ne rɨ, mɨrɨpan ka'pon amʉ' uya tanporo e'ne' pe te'san nee'pʉ ipiya', ti'tui' pʉra rɨ teparan ke te'san. Tʉron kon eparan esi'pʉ ipan pe kuru te'kʉnkʉnmasen, tʉron kon yau makoi a'kwarʉ esi'pʉ, tʉron kon eparan esi'pʉ yai to' enno'pɨ'nin, tʉron kon ipu'tɨka'pɨ'sa' kon Sises uya tanporo pʉsamoro epi'tɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Eke pe rɨ anpisin Kiyarari awɨron kon, Te'ka'pores, Surusiran, Isutiya pon kon, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Isotan nono ratoi pon kon utɨ'pʉ ipɨkɨrɨ.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Sises uya anpisin pe ka'pon amʉ' ensa' a'tai, iyekainʉmʉ'pʉ i'kʉrʉ pona, mɨrɨpan ereuta'pʉ. Ipoitorʉ ton amʉra'pʉ ipiya',</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan kon enupa pɨ' iye'sara'tɨ'pʉ:</li>
      <li>“Pori' pe entu'ma' na'ne' nan ta'kwarʉ kon yau esi, apʉne pʉra to' iwano' pe Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe esi.</li>
      <li>Pori' pe te'ton kon kamoro tʉuta'kwarʉkai' ukaran nɨ pɨ' na'ne' nan serɨ pe, apʉne pʉra Papa uya pori' pe to' ku'to' oton.</li>
      <li>Pori' pe te'ton kon kamoro mɨ pe te'ku'san pen, apʉne pʉra tanporo rɨ non tʉrʉ Papa uya to' ena'.</li>
      <li>Pori' pe te'ton kon kamoro iwan pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tuna'kiri' ke na'ne' nan ipokena' i'se, apʉne pʉra to' rɨ a'wetato' oton.</li>
      <li>Pori' pe te'ton kon kamoro ɨsentu'kena' ton, apʉne pʉra Papa usentu'mato' oton to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Pori' pe te'ton kon kamoro wakʉ pe tewan kon yau nekonekayai'ne' nan, apʉne pʉra to' uya Papa ento' oton.</li>
      <li>Pori' pe te'ton kon kamoro ɨsɨ pe te'san i'nɨ'pankanin nan, apʉne pʉra Papa munkɨ amʉ' pe to' e'to' oton.</li>
      <li>Pori' pe te'ton kon kamoro ɨsɨ pe rɨ, ipan pe rɨ tʉkota'masan wakʉ kupʉ to' uya wenai, to' iwano' pe Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe esi.</li>
      <li>“Pori' pe ɨwesi kon mɨrɨ ka'pon amʉ' uya asapema kon a'tai, iwenai pʉra ɨkota'ma'nokon a'tai mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ to' usaurokʉ ɨri pe rɨ ɨpɨ'nokon a'tai urɨ uriya'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ' ipan pe pori' pe kuru e'tɨ', apʉne pʉra eke rɨ ɨyepe'pʉ kon esi pɨ' Epʉn po, apʉne pʉra mɨrɨ kasa rɨ arawɨron kon pu'kena' amʉ' kota'mapɨtʉ'pʉ to' uya mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“Non waiyori pe rɨ ɨwesi kon, e'tane ine'ne' pe pʉra waiyo enasa' yau, nai kasa ine'ne' pe kanan iye'to' pe ikupʉ? Wakʉ pe pʉra rɨ iyesi mɨrɨ, eno'mato' pe rɨ iyesi ka'pon amʉ' uya iwasa'pɨ'to' pe tʉusarɨ kon a'tai.</li>
      <li>“Serɨ non weyu pe rɨ ɨwesi kon. Wʉ' pon pata e'so'namʉ pʉra iyesi mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe pʉra ka'pon amʉ' uya raan'pu po'tɨsa' nonka pʉra iyesi mɨrɨ pʉsau o'koi'. E'tane ru'ku, to' uya inonka iyapon pona, mɨrɨpan uya tanporon kon nɨ wei'tɨ ɨutɨ tau.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa, tɨwɨ ɨweyu pe na'ne' ne'wei'tɨi ka'pon amʉ' uya ento' pe. Mɨrɨ a'tai, wakʉ ɨnkupʉnʉ ento' pe to' uya, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Papa, ɨkʉipʉnʉ, Epʉn pon apurɨpɨ'to' pe to' uya nɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“Pu'kena' amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Mosi' nekama'pʉ Main eno'mai' uye'sa' tukai' kʉsi'tutʉu. Eno'mase'na uye'sa' pen e'tane a'ku'tɨi' ru'ku uye'sa'.</li>
      <li>I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; Epʉn mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ non e'weuka pʉ'kʉ pona, ɨ'rɨ rɨ mo'ka pʉra iyesi Papa Maimu yapai. Aiko pe rɨ na'ne' pen nʉwarai'ka'pʉ esi moro rɨ Main pe tanporon nɨ uta'ku'tɨ pʉ'kʉ pona.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' rɨ aiko pe rʉ'kwɨ na'ne' Main tonpa i'kwɨ'nin mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉron kon enupanin mɨrɨ rɨ marɨ ku'to' pe to' uya e'to' oton aiko pe Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe yau; e'tane ɨnʉ' rɨ Main kupʉ pɨ' na'ne' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipɨ' enupanin pe na'ne' e'to' oton eke pe kuru Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe yau.</li>
      <li>Ta uya ɨpɨ'nokon, wakʉ rɨken ku'to' auya'nokon pe iyesi Pari'si amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main pɨ' enupanin nan entai; mɨrɨ kupʉ auya pʉra iyesi a'tai, Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe ya' ɨyepa'kato' oton kon parɨ pen nɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Miyarɨ rɨ usenupan nɨto' ekama'pʉ Sises uya; “Eta'pʉ auya'nokon pena rɨ ka'pon amʉ' pɨ' ta'pʉ, ‘Ɨtonpa kʉ'wɨnɨi,’ tawon, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ, ‘Ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉtonpa wɨnin nʉ'pʉ kota'mato' oton,’ tawon,</li>
      <li>e'tane ta uya ɨpɨ'nokon, ɨnʉ' rɨ sakoro' pe na'ne' tʉtonpa pɨ' kota'mato' oton Papa uya. Takapʉ uya kanan, ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉtonpa esa'nin ‘Ra'ka,’ tukai' esi Esuwerʉ amʉ' Konsʉrʉʉi ton nʉkota'ma ton pe, e'tane ɨnʉ' uya, ‘Ɨmɨrɨ, iya'kwarʉ pʉn!’ tasa' a'tai tʉtonpa pɨ', ɨsɨ rɨ apo' e'ma tau iyesi mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', ɨuse'mato' Papa ena' esi a'tai, moro ɨyenu yau ɨri pe ɨtonpa e'ku'to' ɨpɨ' tʉku'se itɨkɨ ɨtonpa e'ku'to' ɨri pe ɨpɨ' konekai'.</li>
      <li>Papa ena' use'man nɨto' apon piyau ɨntʉrʉnʉ tʉnonkai', wapiya ɨtonpa a'kɨrɨ ekoneka ta, ɨyenna'po pa ɨntʉrʉnʉ tʉse'na.</li>
      <li>“Oko pe pʉra ɨyeyaton ko'tʉ ta' ayayai'ne' a'kɨrɨ ekonekaka'kɨ ipokon pe rɨ marɨ ɨwesi koro'tau, ɨkota'mato' ya' ɨtʉrʉ iya wapiya, eseru aimenkanin uya ɨtʉrʉ pʉresiman ena', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨyeno'ma to' uya pariki'si ta'.</li>
      <li>I'napairon nɨ ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; ɨyepa'kato' oton pen nɨ tanporo ɨne'manʉ kon i'ma'ka auya'nokon pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ.</li>
      <li>“Eta'pʉ auya'nokon; ‘Tʉtaan'pʉ kenan kʉsekumankai,’ tawon.</li>
      <li>E'tane ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; ɨnʉ' uya rɨ uri'san ensa' a'tai ekumai' pe, iyekumaka'sa' rɨ mɨrɨ uri'san a'kɨrɨ tewan yau.</li>
      <li>Enwo'ne' winon ɨyenu uya ɨye'makoima emapu'tɨ pe iyesi yau, imo'kakɨ eno'ma pa; wakʉ iwa pe rɨ iyesi tikin nɨ ɨpun tonpa'kasa' auya a'tai, tanporo ɨpun eno'ma ekota'man nɨto' ya' entai.</li>
      <li>Enwo'ne' winon ɨyemiyatʉ uya ɨye'makoima emapu'tɨ pe iyesi yau, a'tɨkɨ eno'ma pa; wakʉ iwa pe iyesi mɨrɨ tikin nɨ ɨpun tonpa'kasa' auya a'tai, tanporo ɨpun eno'ma ekota'man nɨto' ya' entai,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>“Tasa' iya kanan, ‘Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ tʉno'pʉ nonka a'tai, tɨwɨ nʉkaretai'tɨi kuru rɨ iye'nonka karetaai ke,’</li>
      <li>e'tane ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉno'pʉ nonkayai'ne', iyekumasa' pen nɨ e'tane uya tekumasen pe iyesi emapu'tɨ mɨrɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨnʉ' rɨ inonkasa' rʉ'pʉ mari'mayai'ne', ekuma pe iyesi mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“Eta'pʉ auya'nokon pena rɨ kanan ka'pon amʉ' pɨ' ta'pʉ, ‘Ausauro'sa' rʉ'pʉ ipɨ', iku'to' pe auya kʉ'pʉremekʉi, e'tane Papa ya' ausauro'sa' rʉ'pʉ awɨrɨ rɨ e'kɨ.’</li>
      <li>E'tane ekama uya ɨpɨ'; ɨ'rɨ rɨ kʉkai ɨnku'ton pen nɨ pɨ', Epʉn nɨ kʉsesakʉi---Papa apon mɨrɨ,</li>
      <li>non nɨ kʉsesakʉi---Papa pʉta apon mɨrɨ; Surusiran nɨ kʉsesakʉi---eke kin pata'se' mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ a'pai rɨ kʉsesakʉi, apʉne pʉra tikin nɨ rɨ a'pai i'po' aimu'naka auya pʉra iyesi mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ i'kʉrʉntanʉkʉ auya pʉra rɨ iyesi.</li>
      <li>Ewai' ta auya a'tai, ewai' ka'kɨ; kane ta auya a'tai, kane ka'kɨ rɨ nɨrɨ. Tʉron nɨ pe ausaurokʉ a'tai mɨrɨ esi Makoi winon pe.</li>
      <li>“Eta'pʉ auya'nokon nɨ, ‘En epe'pʉ pe en nɨ esi; ɨ epe'pʉ pe ɨ rɨ esi,’ tawon.</li>
      <li>E'tane ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; ɨri pe ɨku'nin nʉ'pʉ pɨ' kɨse'mai. Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ ɨwɨnɨ yau enwo'ne' winon ɨye'peta pɨ', iratoi rʉ'pʉ rɨ marɨ ira'tɨkɨ iwinɨkʉi'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨnʉ' uya rɨ ayarɨ pe iyesi yau ko'tʉ ta' ɨ'rɨ wenai rɨ, mɨrɨpan uya ɨpon mo'ka pe iyesi yau itepe'pʉ pe, tɨwɨ ipʉro'pon pokon pe ɨpon mo'kai.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ ta'kwarʉkai' ayarɨ ta'kɨrɨ a'tai 1 mayirʉ, enta 2 mayirʉ e'to' airɨ.</li>
      <li>Ɨyekama'poyai'ne'nokon irepatɨ', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kera'tɨi ɨnʉ' rɨ ɨyekama'ponin ɨiwano' pɨ' piyapai.</li>
      <li>“Eta'pʉ auya'nokon; ‘Ɨtonpa i'nʉnkakɨ, ɨyeyaton ewaruma'tɨi'ma.’</li>
      <li>E'tane ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; ɨyeyaton kon nɨ i'nʉnkatɨ', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨpʉrematɨ' ɨkota'manin kon pona,</li>
      <li>Epʉn pon ɨkʉipʉnʉ kon munkɨ amʉ' pe ɨwesi kon pa. Ɨri ton nɨ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ wakʉ ton nɨ weyu pe wʉi enu enuku emapu'tɨnin. Ipokena' ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipokena' ton pen nɨ pona tuna ennoko iya.</li>
      <li>Ɨi'nʉnkanin kon nɨken i'nʉnka auya'nokon yau, ɨ'rɨ ken si ɨyepe'pʉ kon eporo auya'nokon mɨrɨ? Mɨrɨ pe' kupʉ pʉrata amʉranʉ'nin nan uya pʉra nai?</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨtonpa ton nɨken nɨ pɨ' miyarɨ ta auya'nokon yau, ɨ'rɨ ken si kupʉ auya'nokon tʉron kon entai? Mɨrɨ pe' kupʉ Papa apurɨnin nan pen uya pʉra nai?</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', wakʉ pe e'tɨ', ɨkʉipʉnʉ kon, Epʉn pon esi wakʉ pe kasa.”</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Sises e'sara'tɨkaa'pʉ kanan tʉpoitorʉ ton enupa pɨ'. Ta'pʉ iya, “Ti'tui' e'tɨ', wakʉ ɨnkupʉnʉ kon yau, wakʉ pe e'nɨto' pɨ' ka'pon amʉ' uya ɨyento' pe tukai'. Mɨrɨ ku'sa' auya a'tai, ɨyepe'pʉ eporo auya pʉra rɨ iyesi mɨrɨ ɨkʉipʉnʉ, Epʉn pon winɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pɨ' entu'manin nan repa auya'nokon a'tai, eke pe kʉsekamai, wakʉ pe te'ku'san uya ikupʉ kasa Esuwerʉ amʉ' usenupato' iwʉ' tau, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ asanta tawɨrɨ rɨ, tapurɨto' kon pe ka'pon amʉ' uya tukai'. I'napairon nɨ ekama uya serɨ ɨpɨ'nokon, to' uya tepe'pʉ kon epoka'sa' rɨ mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane entu'manin nan repa auya a'tai, tɨwɨ akamisi winon ɨyemiyatʉ kʉsi'tunin ɨyenwo'netʉ winon ɨyemiyatʉ nʉkupʉnʉ,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨ pɨ' ɨnkupʉnʉ e'to' pe nesii ama'ai, ɨkʉipʉnʉ, ama'ai ɨnkupʉnʉ ennin nʉ'pʉ uya ɨye'mato' pe.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨwɨpʉrema kon a'tai, wakʉ pe te'ku'san kasa ke'tʉu. Ɨpʉremapaino kon te'mʉ'sa'kai' Esuwerʉ amʉ' usenupato' iwʉ' tau mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ asanta ka'taporo rɨ, tento' kon pe ka'pon amʉ' uya. I'napairon nɨ ekama uya serɨ ɨpɨ'nokon, to' uya tepe'pʉ kon epoka'sa' rɨ mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane ɨwɨpʉrema a'tai, ɨiwʉ' pʉ'kʉ ta' ewonkɨ, ɨmʉra'taai a'kokɨ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨwɨpʉrema pa tʉusensen pen nɨ ɨkʉipʉnʉ pɨ'. Mɨrɨ a'tai, ɨkʉipʉnʉ, ama'ai ɨnkupʉnʉ ennin uya ɨye'mato' pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ amaimu rɨ marɨ tʉna'popɨ'se kɨpʉremai, Papa i'tunin nan pen kasa tʉmaimu kon useta pe tekamai', apʉne pʉra tu'kan nɨ esakʉ tʉuya'nokon pɨ'.</li>
      <li>To' kasa ke'tʉu, ɨkʉipʉnʉ uya rɨ i'tuka'sa' i'se ɨwe'to' tekama'po auya wapiya rɨ.</li>
      <li>“Se kasa nin si ɨwɨpʉremato' kon esi mɨrɨ: “‘Ina Kʉipʉnʉ Epʉn pon, tʉnamasen pe ɨyese' nesii.</li>
      <li>Ina esa' pe ɨwe'to' nʉyepʉi, serɨ non po ɨyeseru ne'kupʉi Epʉn po iyesi na'ne' kasa.</li>
      <li>Ina irepakɨ serɨ pe wʉi kaisa rɨ te'sen ina i'kiyari ke.</li>
      <li>Ina nʉko'manʉkʉnʉ ɨri pɨ' ɨsentu'makɨ, ina usentu'masa' ɨri ko'manʉ'nin nan pɨ' na'ne' kasa.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ina kʉsarɨi i'tupɨ'nɨto' ya', e'tane ɨri pe te'sen piyapai ina imo'kakɨ.’</li>
      <li>“Apʉne pʉra ka'pon amʉ' uya ɨri pe ɨku'sa' a'tai, to' pɨ' ɨusentu'ma yau, ɨkʉipʉnʉ, Epʉn pon nɨ nɨrɨ usentu'ma mɨrɨ ɨpɨ'.</li>
      <li>E'tane ɨri pe ɨku'nin nan nʉ'pʉ kon pɨ' ɨusentu'ma kon pʉra iyesi yau, ɨkʉipʉnʉ rɨ nɨrɨ usentu'ma pʉra iyesi ɨpɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Ɨuseruma a'tai tenta'nai' pʉra, pokoi pe ɨyemʉ' kʉ'kupʉi wakʉ pe te'ku'san e'to' kasa, temʉ' rɨ to' ena ka'pon amʉ' uya rɨ nin tento' kon pe, ka'pon amʉ' uya rɨ nin tapurɨto' kon pe. I'napairon nɨ ekama uya ɨpɨ', to' uya tepe'pʉ kon epoka'sa' rɨ mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane ɨuseruma a'tai tenta'nai' pʉra, ɨsenpatauka', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ekarapaima'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, ka'pon uya ɨto'ka'nʉkʉ pʉra iyesi mɨrɨ ɨuseruma tenta'nai' pʉra tukai', e'tane ɨkʉipʉnʉ, tʉusensen pen nɨ uya i'tu, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨkʉipʉnʉ, ama'ai te'ku'sen ennin nʉ'pʉ uya rɨ ɨye'mato' pe.</li>
      <li>“Ɨimamin kʉsamʉranʉkʉi serɨ non po, ene amʉ' uya ima'tanʉ'to' yau rɨ, ikaranto' yau rɨ, ama' amʉ' e'to' ama' pe yau rɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane Epʉn po ɨimamin kon amʉranʉ'tɨ', ene amʉ' uya ima'tanʉ'to' pen pata'se' yau, ikaranto' pen yau, ama' amʉ' e'to' ama' pe pata pen nɨ yau.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra ɨimamin kon e'to' airɨ, mɨrɨ yau ɨyewan kon nɨ nɨrɨ esi.</li>
      <li>“En esi pun raan'puui pe rɨ. Wakʉ pe ɨyenu esi yau, tanporo ɨpun esi a'kwa pe.</li>
      <li>E'tane, wakʉ pe pʉra ɨyenu esi a'tai, ewarupɨ pe rɨ ɨpun esi. Iweyu pʉra ɨpun esi yau, ipan pe rɨ ewarupɨ pe iyesi mɨrɨ!</li>
      <li>“Ɨnʉ' rɨ e'tʉrawasoma pʉra iyesi asa'ron kon tepuru ton apiyo' pe. Tikin nan ewaruma'tɨ iya, isakon i'nʉnka iya; tikin nan pɨ' ita'si, isakon sanoma iya pʉra. Asa'rɨ rɨ marɨ Papa mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ pʉrata apiyo' pe ɨwesi pʉra iyesi.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', ekama uya serɨ ɨpɨ'nokon, ɨuko'manto' kon pɨ' rɨ kɨsewankamatʉu, ɨi'kiyari kon pɨ' rɨ mɨrɨ pe pʉra ɨuku kon pɨ' rɨ, mɨrɨ pe pʉra ɨpun kon pɨ' rɨ, ɨ'rɨ esi upon pe tukai'. Ɨuko'manto' pe' esi pen mɨrɨ kiyari entai? Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨpun kon pe' esi pen pon entai?</li>
      <li>Apʉne toron amʉ' entɨ' ka'tawon kon. Ti'kiyari kon pɨnnin nan pen nɨ, anʉnnin nan pen nɨ, mɨrɨ pe pʉra amʉranʉ'nin nan pen nɨ, e'tane rɨ ɨkʉipʉnʉ kon, Epʉn pon uya to' ewekʉ. Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon ken pe' si esi pen i'nʉnkena' pe to' entai?</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ tʉuko'manto' ɨnka miyarɨ parɨ ipɨ' tʉusewankamai'?</li>
      <li>“Ɨ'rɨ pɨ' pon pɨ' ɨusewankama kon? Apʉne entɨ' pata ipʉrʉ esi wakʉ pe rɨ iya'ta tʉpata'se' yau, te'tʉrawasomasen pen mɨrɨ pe pʉra ɨ'pɨ'nin pen.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ rɨ e'tane ekama uya serɨ ɨpɨ'nokon; Saraman, imaminkena' epontɨsa' pʉra iyesi'pʉ mɨrɨ ton kasa.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa si Papa uya wana' rɨ pontɨ pe iyesi yau wana' serɨ pe na'ne' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ awanapairɨ eno'ma apo' ya', mɨrɨ na'ne' entai pe' ɨpontɨ iya 'nokon pen mɨ? Aiko sɨ, aiko pe rʉ'kwɨ rɨ apurɨto' auya'nokon esi!</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pɨ' kɨsewankamatʉu, ‘Ɨ'rɨ kuru ɨ'to' pe?’ mɨrɨ pe pʉra, ‘Ɨ'rɨ kuru ensito' pe?’ mɨrɨ pe pʉra, ‘Ɨ'rɨ kuru e'to' pe upon kon pe?’ tukai'.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra Papa i'tunin nan pen e'to' ipɨkɨrɨ ton serɨ, mɨrɨpan ɨkʉipʉnʉ kon, Epʉn pon uya i'tu serɨ ton i'se ɨwesi kon.</li>
      <li>E'tane ru'ku, wapiya kuru esa' wannɨ pe iye'to' iwarinpatɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipokena' pe iye'to', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tanporo serɨ ton nɨ nin si e'tʉrʉ mɨrɨ ɨyena'nokon nɨ nɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Awanapairo' pɨ' kɨsewankamai, tʉponaron nɨ mɨrɨ awanapairo' pɨ' usewankaman; wʉi kaisa rɨ iponaro' rɨ usewankaman nɨto' esi,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>“Ka'pon amʉ' eseru kʉsaimenkatʉu, ɨyeseru kon nɨ nɨrɨ aimenka kʉse'nin.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra ka'pon amʉ' eseru maimenkayatʉi'ne' kasa rɨ marɨ ɨyeseru kon aimenka mɨrɨ. I'tuto' auya'nokon yai pe rɨ ɨnkupʉ'pʉ yai rɨ ɨyena'nokon i'tu mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“Ɨ'rɨ pe iyesi pɨ' aiko rʉ'kwɨ rɨ paranka punu'pɨ ɨnenpai ɨwesi ɨtonpa enu yawon, eke rɨ paranka e'tane ɨyenu yau?</li>
      <li>Nai kasa ɨtonpa pɨ', ‘Apʉne amuru simo'kai' ɨyenu apai,’ ta auya inke rɨ moro paranka e'tane ɨyenu yau?</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon wakʉ pe te'ku'san, wapiya kuru ɨyenu apai paranka imo'kaka'kɨ, mɨrɨ a'tai wakʉ pe ene auya ɨtonpa enu apai amuru mo'ka pa,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Wakʉ pe te'sen kʉ'tʉtʉu pero amʉ' ena'; mokon pun ton ɨiwano' kon kʉseno'matʉu peiruku amʉ' ena', to' uya iwasa'kapɨtʉ esi mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ to' era'tɨ esi akarapɨ'se'na.</li>
      <li>“Ekama'potɨ'; mɨrɨ a'tai, ɨyena'nokon nɨ iye'tʉrʉ. Iwarinpatɨ'; mɨrɨ a'tai, eporo auya'nokon. Mʉra'ta iwɨpɨ'tɨ', mɨrɨpan uta'kokato' pe ɨyena'nokon.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra tanporon kon ekama'po pɨ' na'ne' nan uya eporo; kʉrɨ rɨ iwarinpa pɨ' na'ne' uya rɨ eporo, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kʉrɨ rɨ iwɨpɨtʉ pɨ' na'ne' ena' rɨ mʉra'ta uta'koka.</li>
      <li>Nai kʉrɨ warai uya tʉmu uya pʉreti ekama'po yau irepa tɨ' ke?</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe pʉra, moro' ekama'po iya yau, irepa ɨkʉi ke?</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon nin si ɨri ton uya i'tu yau wakʉ ton e'repan nɨto' ke ɨmunkɨ kon amʉ' repa auya'nokon, mɨrɨ entai kuru ɨkʉipʉnʉ kon, Epʉn pon uya wakʉ ton e'repan nɨto' tʉrʉ kamoro ekama'ponin nan ena'.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pɨ', tanporon yau rɨ iku'tɨ' tʉron kon pɨ', ikupʉ to' uya i'se me'ai'ne' ɨpɨ'nokon. Serɨ uya Main mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pu'kena' amʉ' rɨ nʉmenuka'pʉ amʉranʉkʉ mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“Ewontɨ' aiko rʉ'kwɨ mʉra'ta awɨrɨ, apʉne pʉra eke mʉra'ta mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ eke asanta esi uma'tan nɨto' ya' utɨn e'ma pe, mɨrɨpan tu'kan kon nɨ ka'pon amʉ' ewomʉ iyawɨrɨ,</li>
      <li>e'tane aiko rʉ'kwɨ mʉra'ta mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ aiko rʉ'kwɨ asanta esi wakʉ uko'man nɨto' ya' utɨn e'ma pe, e'tane tu'kan kon pen nɨ utɨto' iyawɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Miyarɨ rɨ Sises esi'pʉ to' enupa pɨ', mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ, “Akono amʉ' pe te'san entɨ'; to' uyepʉ karimeru kasa, e'tane ɨsɨ ton, ene amʉ' kasa to' esi.</li>
      <li>To' i'tu auya'nokon mɨrɨ to' eperu winɨ. Tikʉ kenan apai pe' kʉre' pʉipɨ'nin nan ka'pon amʉ', mɨrɨ pe pʉra pi' rɨ ɨmɨ'nɨ'ta apai? (Kane.)</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ, wakʉ yʉi epeta wakʉ pe rɨ, ɨri yʉi epeta ɨri pe rɨ.</li>
      <li>Wakʉ yʉi epeta pʉra iyesi ɨri pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨri yʉi epeta pʉra iyesi mɨrɨ wakʉ pe.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' uya tʉusepetasen pen yʉi a'tɨ eno'mato' pe tʉuya'nokon apo' ya'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa to' eperu winɨ to' i'tu auya'nokon,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Tanporon kon ka'pon amʉ', ‘Uyepuru, uyepuru!’ tawon nan upɨ' epa'kato' oton pen nɨ Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe pata'se' ya', e'tane kʉrɨ rɨken ukʉipʉnʉ, Epʉn pon e'to' i'se ku'nin.</li>
      <li>Iweyu e'seposa' a'tai, tu'kan kon nɨ ka'pon amʉ' uya tato' oton upɨ', ‘Uyepuru, uyepuru, pu'kena' pe pe' ina usaurokʉ pʉn ɨyese' yau, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨyese' yau pe' ɨri a'kwarʉ ton enpa'kapɨtʉ'pʉ ina uya pʉn, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ eke Papa tʉrawasooi ku'pɨtʉ pʉn pe' ina uya?’</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, tʉwapu'tɨi' pʉra to' pɨ' ekamato' uya oton, ‘Ɨi'tusa' uya 'nokon pʉra man. Entantɨ' upiyapai, ɨmɨrɨ'nokon ɨri ku'nin nan!’” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', tanporon kon serɨ ton umaimu ton eta pɨ' na'ne' nan mɨrɨpan kupʉ pɨ' na'ne' nan esi mɨrɨ ta'kwarʉ kenan ka'pon kasa tɨ' po tiwʉ' amɨnin.</li>
      <li>Tuna uyee'pʉ, tuna apɨrʉ ton u'ma'pʉ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ a'setun uyee'pʉ e'se'ne' pe ɨutɨ tʉwɨse, e'tane ita'mo'ka'pʉ pen nɨ, apʉne pʉra tɨ' po iyapon esi pɨ'.</li>
      <li>E'tane tanporon kon serɨ ton umaimu ton eta pɨ' na'ne' nan mɨrɨpan kupʉ to' uya pʉra na'ne' nan esi mɨrɨ iya'kwarʉ pʉn ka'pon kasa tiwʉ' amɨnin wɨ'sɨ' po.</li>
      <li>Tuna uyee'pʉ, tuna apɨrʉ ton u'ma'pʉ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ a'setun uyee'pʉ e'se'ne' pe ɨutɨ tʉwɨse, mɨrɨpan uta'mo'ka uya eke pe pata a'merunpa'pʉ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ ton pɨ' Sises usaurokʉ e'nonkasa' a'tai, anpisin ton nɨ ka'pon amʉ' usewansiuka'pʉ enupan nɨto' iya pɨ',</li>
      <li>apʉne pʉra enupan iya pɨ' tʉmeruntɨrʉ kenan pe kuru rɨ, Main pɨ' enupanin nan kasa pʉra.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Wʉ' ponsi'kɨ Sises u'tɨsa' a'tai, anpisin ton nɨ ka'pon amʉ' uya e'ma'pʉka'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Erekʉ'pan ka'pon uyee'pʉ ipiya', mɨrɨpan e'sekunka'pʉ irau. Mɨrɨpan uya, “Uyepuru, ɨnku'pai ɨwesi yau, wakʉ pe rɨ ukupʉ auya,” ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Temiyatʉ ɨnka'pʉ Sises uya, mɨrɨpan uya a'pɨtʉ'pʉ, “Ɨnku'pai rɨ e'ai', wakʉ pe e'kɨ!” ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'. Inke pʉra rɨ, tʉwereei apai iyekoneka'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya, “Ɨnʉ' pɨ' rɨ kʉsekamai,” ta'pʉ, “e'tane enta ɨsenpoikata use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin ena', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨntʉrʉnʉ pe te'sen Mosi' uya tasa' na'ne' awɨrɨ mʉtʉrʉi'. Mɨrɨ uya rɨ nin si ɨusepi'tɨsa' ekama mɨrɨ to' pɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises epa'kasa' a'tai, Ka'paneyan pona, soisa amʉ' epuru uyee'pʉ ipiya' tʉpika'tɨto' pe iya ekama'pose'na.</li>
      <li>“Uyepuru, upoitorʉ man ipan pe e'ne' pe iyesi, ipu'tɨka'sa' te'kwe' tau rɨ iyesi, pata po,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Miyarɨ rɨ utɨ mɨrɨ epi'tɨi',” ta'pʉ Sises uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Soisa amʉ' epuru uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Uyepuru, uiwʉ' ta' ɨuyepʉ pokena' pen nɨ urɨ. Amaimu rɨken itʉkɨ; mɨrɨ a'tai, upoitorʉ usepi'tɨto' pe.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra urɨ kʉrɨ rɨ tepuru kenan, soisa amʉ' esa' uwo'noro te'san. Pʉse pɨ', ‘Enta,’ ta uya a'tai, itɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kʉrɨ pɨ', ‘Ɨsi'kɨ,’ ta uya a'tai, iyepʉ. Upoitorʉ pɨ', ‘Se iku'kɨ,’ ta uya a'tai, ikupʉ iya,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya serɨ etasa' a'tai, isewansiuka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ tʉpɨkɨrɨ te'san ka'pon amʉ' pɨ', “I'napairon ekama uya serɨ ɨpɨ'nokon, ɨnʉ' rɨ eposa' uya pʉra rɨ man Esuwerʉ po eke rɨ serɨ waraino apurɨto' esa'.</li>
      <li>Ta uya ɨpɨ'nokon, tu'kan kon nɨ ka'pon amʉ' uye'to' oton pata wʉi enu uyepʉ, wʉi enu utɨ winɨ'ne, mɨrɨpan kon ereutato' oton enta'nan pɨ' Epʉra'an, Aisi' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Seko' pokon pe Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe yau.</li>
      <li>E'tane esa' wannɨ pe e'nɨto' yau te'ton kon tasa' kon nʉ'san eno'mato' iya oton ewarupɨ ya', ukaran nɨto' oton, ɨ e'kɨtɨtɨi'mato' oton ya',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan soisa amʉ' epuru pɨ' Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Enna'po', anapurɨnʉ awɨrɨ rɨ ɨpoitorʉ usepi'tɨ mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨ a'tai rɨ, ipoitorʉ usepi'tɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Sises utɨ'pʉ Pi'ta iwʉ' ta'. Mɨrɨ yau, Pi'ta ewo'pʉ ene'pʉ iya te'kwe' tau e'kɨɨi'man pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya itemiyatʉ pɨ' a'pɨtʉ'pʉ. Mɨrɨ a'tai rɨ, iye'kɨɨi'mato' ereuta'pʉ, mɨrɨpan e'mʉ'sa'ka'pʉ to' mʉta'napase'na.</li>
      <li>Pata uko'mansa' a'tai, ka'pon amʉ' uya tu'kan kon nɨ ka'pon amʉ' makoi a'kwarʉ yen ton pe te'san nee'pʉ Sises piya'. Se kasa rɨ tʉusauro'se makoi a'kwarʉ ton ennoko'pʉ iya, tanporo rɨ takuru'kena' nan epi'tɨ'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ ton kupʉ'pʉ iya pena pu'kena' Aisaya nekama'pʉ rʉ'pʉ a'ku'tɨ pe: “Ɨ'sɨ'mʉra e'nɨto' mo'ka'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan uya uyeparan kon arɨ'pʉ,” tawon.</li>
      <li>Sises uya anpisin ensa' a'tai tʉwoi, tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ', “Parau ku'pɨri ratoi pona e'kwɨrɨ'nɨpai'nokon,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan Main pɨ' enupanin uyee'pʉ ipiya', “Uyepuru, siya rɨ mʉtɨyai'ne' ya' rɨ aya'kɨrɨ utɨ serɨ,” tase'na ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Maikan amʉ' kamoro tenkena' nan, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ toron amʉ' kanan esi tʉpon ke, e'tane Ka'pon, Papa winon esi mɨrɨ ti'pai nonkato' iya yau pʉn nɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Tʉron nɨ kanan ka'pon Sises poitorʉ pe e'paino uya, “Uyepuru, apʉne ken si, wapiya ukʉipʉnʉ siu'na'tɨka'tai',” ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>E'tane Sises uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Tɨwɨ tʉ'koro'tau'nokon te'sen eri'sa' u'na'tɨi to'; uya'kɨrɨ ru'ku utɨnpai,” ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises ekanwa'tɨ'pʉ kanau ya', mɨrɨpan a'kɨrɨ ipoitorʉ ton utɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ koro'tau, ite'kwanau pʉra rɨ pana' pe, ɨsɨ pe rɨ a'setun uyee'pʉ parau ku'pɨri ka', mɨrɨpan uya eke pe rɨ sipa'sipa kupʉ'pʉ tuna pʉro'po. Eke pe sipa'sipa esi uya to' kanwa paru'tɨ esi'pʉ, e'tane rɨ Sises esi'pʉ e'nʉn nɨ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Ipoitorʉ ton utɨ'pʉ ipiya' enpakase'na, ta'pʉ to' uya ipɨ', “Ina epuru! Ina ipika'tɨkɨ! Ina aputan pɨ' man!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon, aiko rʉ'kwɨ apurɨto' iya to' ton, ɨ'rɨ pɨ' ɨyetʉipɨtʉ kon?” ta'pʉ iya. Iye'mʉ'sa'ka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya a'setun mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ sipa'sipa eseremekʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan e'nɨ'pamʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Kamoro si ka'pon amʉ' usewansiuka'pʉ mɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan kon usekama'popɨtʉ'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ pan si pʉse rɨ ka'pon? A'setun mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ sipa'sipa rɨ e'to' imaimu awɨrɨ!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipoitorʉ ton uya si parau ku'pɨri Kiyarari nʉ'kwɨrɨ'nʉ'sa' a'tai, ka'pon amʉ' Katara nono po tʉuko'mansan, asa'ron kon makoi a'kwarʉ yen ton pe te'san uyee'pʉ uruwai' apai to' winɨkʉi'. Ɨsɨ ton nɨ, ɨnʉ' utɨ pokena' pen nɨ mɨrɨ awɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon ukɨ'pɨ'nʉmʉ'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ pe ina ku'se'na ɨuye'sa', Papa Mumu? Iweyu rawɨrɨ rɨ pe' ina kota'mai' ɨuye'sa'?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Ɨnnɨ kuru pʉra rɨ to' piyapai tu'kan kon nɨ peiruku amʉ' esi'pʉ enta'nan pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Makoi a'kwarʉ yen ton uya Sises ekama'po'pʉ ipan pe, “Ina ken si ennoko auya a'tai pʉsamo ka'pon amʉ' apai, apʉne ken si ina enno'kɨ kamo tu'kan kon peiruku amʉ' ya',” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Entantɨ' si,” ta'pʉ Sises uya to' pɨ'. To' epa'ka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon utɨ'pʉ peiruku amʉ' ya' ewonse'na. Tanporo rɨ si kamoro peiruku amʉ' eka'tumʉ'pʉ mɨrɨ parau ku'pɨri ka' tepitoren awɨrɨ rɨ, mɨrɨpan kon aputapɨtʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau, to' mainanpa pɨ' te'san eka'tumʉ'pʉ pata pona, mɨrɨpan kon uya tanporo iye'ku'sa' rʉ'pʉ ekama'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' pɨ'. To' uya rɨ nɨrɨ kamo makoi a'kwarʉ yen ton pe te'san ka'pon amʉ' pɨ' iye'ku'sa' rʉ'pʉ ekama'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan tanporo rɨ mɨrɨ pata yau te'san ka'pon amʉ' utɨ'pʉ Sises ense'na. To' uya Sises ensa' a'tai, tʉnono kon apai iyenna'poto' pe ipan pe to' uya auro'ka'pʉ.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Sises mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipoitorʉ ton ekanwa'tɨ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon ɨ'kwɨrɨtʉ'pʉ. To' uyee'pʉ tʉpata'se' kon ya'.</li>
      <li>Tʉron kon ka'pon amʉ' uya ipu'tɨka'sa' nee'pʉ Sises piya'. Sises uya pʉsamoro ka'pon amʉ' napurɨnʉ ene'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ipu'tɨka'sa' pɨ', “Utonpa, kenari'nʉmʉi, amakooi pɨ' usentu'masa' man,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ etasa' Main pɨ' enupanin nan tonpa ton uya a'tai, “Pʉse rɨ ka'pon usaurokʉ Papa sapema pe rɨ,” ta'pʉ to' uya tewan kon yau.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' usenuminkato' i'tu'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨto' pe ɨri pe rɨ ɨusenuminka kon ɨyewan kon yau?</li>
      <li>Nai esi sa'man pe pʉra: ‘Amakooi pɨ' usentu'ma,’ ta; mɨrɨ pe pʉra, ‘E'mʉ'sa'ka', asakɨ,’ ta katɨ ipu'tɨka'sa' pɨ'?</li>
      <li>I'tu kon pa, Ka'pon, Papa winon piyau meruntɨ esi serɨ non po makoi pɨ' usentu'man nɨto',” ta'pʉ iya. Sises uya ta'pʉ ipu'tɨka'sa' ka'pon pɨ', “E'mʉ'sa'kakɨ, ayapon anʉnkɨ, enna'pokɨ si apata'se' ya',” ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Pʉse rɨ ka'pon ena'pʉ wakʉ pe, mɨrɨpan e'mʉ'sa'kasa', enna'po'pʉ tʉpata'se' ya'.</li>
      <li>Serɨ ensa' tʉuya'nokon a'tai, ipan pe rɨ ka'pon amʉ' enari'nʉmʉ'pʉ. To' uya si Papa apurɨpɨtʉ'pʉ eke rɨ serɨ meruntɨ tʉsa' iya pɨ' ka'pon amʉ' ena'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya si mɨrɨ pata nɨmɨ a'tai, ka'pon ereutasa' ene'pʉ iya pʉrata amʉranʉ'nin pe e'nɨ iwʉ' tau, Ma'siu itese'. Sises uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Ɨsi'kɨ upoitorʉ pe, Ma'siu,” ta'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨpan e'mʉ'sa'ka'pʉ, iya'kɨrɨ itɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Sises enta'na koro'tau Ma'siu iwʉ' tau, tu'kan kon nɨ pʉrata amʉranʉ'nin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉmakooikena' nan uyee'pʉ ipokon pe enta'nase'na, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipoitorʉ ton pokon pe rɨ nɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai si, Pari'si amʉ' uya serɨ ensa' a'tai, ta'pʉ to' uya Sises poitorʉ ton pɨ', “Ɨ'rɨto' pe ɨti'saai kon enta'na pʉrata amʉranʉ'nin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉmakooikena' nan pokon pe rɨ?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' eta'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon pɨ' ta'pʉ iya, “Atu' ka'pon esi pen mɨrɨ ta'ta i'se e'tane, takuru'kenan esi i'se.</li>
      <li>Ɨsenupatantɨ', ɨ'rɨ ta iya e'kwa pe serɨ esi tukai': ‘Ka'pon amʉ' i'se esi ɨsentu'kena' pe, o' ke tʉuse'masan i'se esi pen,’ tawon. Uye'sa' serɨ ipokena' ton ka'pon amʉ' kɨ'mai' pen, e'tane uye'sa' serɨ tʉmakooikena' nan kɨ'mase'na,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ tʉpo, Isaan poitorʉ ton uyee'pʉ Sises piya'. To' uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Ɨ'rɨ pe iyesi pɨ' ina mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pari'si amʉ' useruma tenta'nai' pʉra, e'tane ɨpoitorʉ ton useruma pʉra iyesi?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' eikʉ'pʉ, “Nai kasa warawo' temari'masen nʉkɨ'ma'san esi tʉuta'kwarʉkai' ukaran nɨ pɨ' tʉpiyau'nokon nɨ iye'tane? Iweyu rɨ e'seporo mɨrɨ temari'masen utanʉnto' oton to' piyapai, mɨrɨ a'tai nin si to' useruma mɨrɨ tenta'nai' pʉra,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya rɨ ta'pʉ, “Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ pon pooi'pɨ pona pon atʉ punu'pɨ a'si'tɨ pʉra rɨ iyesi mɨrɨ; emenna' pon punu'pɨ uya ipooi'pɨ pon karaka mɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan uya eke pe iteuta kupʉ mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ, ka'pon amʉ' uya emenna' waain entɨ pʉra iyesi mɨrɨ ipooi'pɨ iten ya'. Mɨrɨ ku'sa' to' uya a'tai, emenna' waain uya penaro' rʉ'pʉ iten toi'kwa rɨ mɨrɨ; mɨrɨ tʉpo, asa'rɨ rɨ marɨ waain mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ iten uma'tasa' rɨ mɨrɨ. Ka'pon amʉ' uya emenna' waain entɨto' pe iyesi emenna' iten ya'. Mɨrɨ a'tai, asa'rɨ rɨ marɨ wakʉ pe iyesi mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ rɨ ta Sises uya koro'tau, Esuwerʉ amʉ' epuru uyee'pʉ ipiya'. Iye'sekunka'pʉ Sises rakʉi', mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Uyensi uma'tasa' man serɨ pe rɨ, e'tane uya'kɨrɨ ɨsi'kɨ uiwʉ' ta' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ a'pɨ'tanʉ'kɨ ito'panto' pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises e'mʉ'sa'ka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ iya'kɨrɨ. Ipoitorʉ ton nɨ nɨrɨ utɨ'pʉ iya'kɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai rɨ, uri'san, mʉn ennoko pɨ' te'sen uyee'pʉ ipɨkɨrɨ, ipon e'pi a'pɨ'se'na. Mɨrɨ pɨ' iko'mansa' esi'pʉ 12 kaisa rɨ wʉipiya.</li>
      <li>Tewan yau rʉ'kwɨ rɨ, “Sises pon nɨ a'pɨ'sa' uya yau, usepi'tɨ rɨ mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises era'tɨ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ene'pʉ. Ta'pʉ iya ipɨ', “Kɨsewankamai, ma'non. Papa uya ɨyepi'tɨsa' mɨrɨ, apʉne pʉra apurɨ auya ke,” ta'pʉ Sises uya ipɨ'. Mɨrɨ a'tai rɨ, uri'san usepi'tɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises ewomʉ'pʉ Esuwerʉ amʉ' epuru iwʉ' ta'. Mɨrɨ yau, ka'pon amʉ', sarakuwa turunpa pɨ' te'san mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉron kon ukaran nɨ pɨ' te'san ene tʉuya a'tai,</li>
      <li>ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “Entantɨ', iyeri'sa' pen mɨrɨ; iye'nʉnsa' rɨ nin mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya. E'tane to' uta'kɨrɨ'pʉ ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Pʉroroi pona to' enpa'ka tʉpo, ɨutɨ ta' iyewomʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya uri'san anʉmʉ'pʉ itemiyatʉ pɨ', mɨrɨpan uto'pamʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan ekareei utɨ'pʉ siya rɨ mɨrɨ nono kaisarɨ rɨ.</li>
      <li>Sises uya si mɨrɨ pata nɨmɨ koro'tau, asa'ron kon tenku'na' nan uya e'ma'pʉka'pʉ. To' ukɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨtʉ'pʉ ipɨ', “Ɨmɨrɨ, Tepi' pa rʉ'pʉ, ina pɨ' ɨsentu'ma'!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai si ɨutɨ ta' Sises ewonka'sa' koro'tau, to' uyee'pʉ ipiya'. To' ekama'po'pʉ iya, “Mapurɨyatʉu pe' ɨyepi'tɨ uya 'nokon tukai'?” ta'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨpan kon uya si ta'pʉ, “Ewai', Uyepuru, ina uya rɨ ayapurɨ,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ tʉpo, Sises uya to' enu a'pɨtʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ, “Ɨsepi'tɨtɨ' si, apurɨ auya'nokon ke,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ennin nan pe si to' ena'pʉ. Mɨrɨ tʉpo, Sises uya ta'pʉ ipan pe to' pɨ', “Ɨnʉ' rɨ kʉ'pana'tɨtʉu serɨ pɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane rɨ to' utɨ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya serɨ si itekareei ekama'pʉ siya rɨ mɨrɨ nono kaisarɨ rɨ.</li>
      <li>To' utɨka'tane rɨ, ka'pon amʉ' uya makoi yen, tʉusauro'sen pen ka'pon nee'pʉ Sises piya'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan enpa'kasa' iya a'tai, isaurokʉ'pʉ. Ipan pe rɨ ka'pon amʉ' usewansiuka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya ta'pʉ, “Serɨ waraino e'kupʉ ensa' pʉra rɨ iyesi wapiya Esuwerʉ po!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>E'tane Pari'si amʉ' uya ta'pʉ, “Makoi amʉ' epuru winɨ makoi amʉ' enpa'kapɨtʉ iya,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises utɨpɨtʉ'pʉ tanporon eke iwa ton pata yau'ne, mɨrɨpan uya ka'pon amʉ' enupa'pʉ Esuwerʉ amʉ' usenupato' iwʉ' tau'ne. Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe ekareei ekama'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan uya tanporo ka'pon amʉ' epi'tɨpɨtʉ'pʉ ti'tui' pʉra paran pɨ' takuru'ke te'san.</li>
      <li>Tu'kan kon ka'pon amʉ' ensa' tʉuya a'tai, to' pɨ' isentu'ma'pʉ, apʉne pʉra ipan pe rɨ usewankaman pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tiwano' kon pe to' epika'tɨ poken pʉra rɨ to' esi pɨ'. To' esi'pʉ karimeru amʉ' ipa'simanin pʉnon kon kasa.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ', “Eke pe rɨ umɨ yau kiyari akʉ'pʉsa' tanʉnsen man e'tane, tu'ke pʉra tʉrawaso amʉ' amʉranʉ'nin nan esi.</li>
      <li>Umɨ esa' ekama'potɨ', ka'pon amʉ' enno'to' pe iya kiyari akʉ'pʉsa' anʉmʉ amʉranʉ'nin nan pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>12 kaisaron kon tʉpoitorʉ ton kɨ'ma'pʉ iya tʉpiya', mɨrɨpan kon repa'pʉ iya ɨri a'kwarʉ pa'kato' meruntɨrʉ ke, ti'tui' pʉra rɨ paran ton pɨ' takuru'ke'ne te'san nɨrɨ epi'tɨpɨ'nin nan pe.</li>
      <li>Pʉsamoro na'ne' 12 kaisaron kon enno'sa' kon ese' ton: wapiya Saiman (Pi'ta tukai' tesa'sen), iyakon Anturu; Isens, Sepiti mu, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ iyakon Isaan;</li>
      <li>Piri', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pa'taramiu; Tamas, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Ma'siu, Roman kopʉnaai ena' use'man nɨto' amʉranʉ'nin; Isens (Arʉ'piyas mu), mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Tatiyas;</li>
      <li>Saiman, Usera' tukai' tesa'sen; mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Isutas Eskariya', eparankanin pe iyesi'pʉ na'ne'.</li>
      <li>Pʉsamoro 12 kaisaron kon tʉpoitorʉ ton ennoko'pʉ iya to' tauro'kai' se kasa: “Esuwerʉ amʉ' ton pen nɨ ka'pon amʉ' piya' kʉtɨtʉu, mɨrɨ pe pʉra kepa'katʉu Sameriya pata ton ya' rɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane Esuwerʉ amʉ' piya' entantɨ', karimeru utano'masa' waraino kon piya'.</li>
      <li>Ɨutɨ kon pe rɨ, serɨ itekare mekamatʉi': ‘A'ko pe Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe man,’ tukai'.</li>
      <li>Takuru'kenan kon ka'pon amʉ' mepi'tɨtʉi', iyeri'sa' kon nɨrɨ ka'pon amʉ' mi'mʉ'sa'kapɨ'tʉi'. Ere' pɨ' te'san mepi'tɨtʉi', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨri a'kwarʉ ton menpa'kapɨ'tʉi'. Te'mai' pʉra eposa' auya'nokon kasa rɨ, te'mai' pʉra mʉtʉtʉi'.</li>
      <li>Korʉ, sirʉpa, ka'pa rɨ kʉsatʉu ɨpokʉrʉʉi kon yau;</li>
      <li>paiki, sapato, teke'sen, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tu'ke ipona ɨpon kon kʉsatʉu aya'kɨrɨ'nokon, apʉne pʉra tʉrawaso amʉ' pe ɨwesi kon, mɨrɨ epe'pʉ rɨ eporo auya'nokon,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Eke iwa pata ya' ɨutɨ kon a'tai, wakʉ pe tiwʉ' kon ta' ɨyereutanʉ'nin kon mɨnentʉi'. Itiwʉ' tau me'tʉi' inɨmɨ auya'nokon pona rɨ.</li>
      <li>To' iwʉ' ta' ɨyewomʉ kon a'tai, ‘Miyarɨ,’ mʉkatʉi'.</li>
      <li>To' uya ɨyereutanʉkʉ kon a'tai, tɨwɨ ‘Miyarɨ,’ ta'pʉ auya'nokon nɨ ne'nonkai to' pona. Mɨrɨ kupʉ to' uya pʉra iyesi a'tai ɨpɨ'nokon, mʉna'potʉi' to' piyapai.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ wakʉ pe ɨyereutanʉkʉ kon pʉra iyesi yau, mɨrɨ pe pʉra amaimu kon eta to' uya pʉra iyesi yau, a'ta kon mʉtɨutɨpɨ'tʉi' mɨrɨ pata nɨmɨ auya'nokon a'tai.</li>
      <li>I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, Satan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Komora uya imoronka poken parɨ iye'to' oton eseru aimenka weyu a'tai mɨrɨ pata uya imoronka entai iye'tane,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises esi'pʉ miyarɨ rɨ 12 kaisaron kon tʉpoitorʉ ton auro'ka pɨ'. Ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “Ɨyennoko uya 'nokon serɨ ɨri ton ka'pon amʉ' koro'ta', karimeru ennoko kasa ɨsɨ ton, ene amʉ' koro'tau. Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', emepoke' pe me'tʉi' ɨkʉi kasa, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨsɨ pe pʉra wako'wa kasa me'tʉi'.</li>
      <li>Tenu ke nɨrɨ me'tʉi' ka'pon amʉ' pɨ'; to' uya ɨtʉto' oton kon mɨrɨ pata epuru ton ena'. To' uya nɨrɨ ayari'po'pɨ'to' oton kon mɨrɨ tʉusenupato' kon iwʉ' tau'ne.</li>
      <li>To' uya ayato' oton kon mɨrɨ kopʉna mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kin amʉ' piya' urɨ wenai, urɨ ekama kon pa Esuwerʉ amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' pen pɨ'.</li>
      <li>E'tane kɨsewankamatʉu to' uya aya'sisa' kon a'tai, ɨ'rɨ ta uya, nai kasa ta uya tukai'. Mɨrɨ a'tai, amaimu'tɨ uya 'nokon mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon pe ausaurokʉ kon pen mɨrɨ, e'tane ɨkʉipʉnʉ kon A'kwarʉ usauro'to' oton mɨrɨ ayawɨrɨ'nokon.</li>
      <li>“Eri'nɨto' ya' tʉrui eparankato' oton iyakon uya, ikʉipʉnʉ uya nɨrɨ tʉmʉre; mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ, mʉre amʉ' enato' oton tʉsan kon amʉ' ewa'noma pɨ' to' eri'to' ya' to' tʉrʉ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Urɨ wenai tu'kan kon ka'pon amʉ' uya ɨyewaruma'tɨto' oton kon, e'tane kʉrɨ rɨ pana' pe ne'mʉ'sa'kayai'ne' iu'matʉ pona rɨ epika'tɨto' oton mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>To' uya pata yau ɨkota'ma kon a'tai, tʉron nɨ pata ya' mapʉrʉntʉi'. I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, Esuwerʉ amʉ' pata ton awɨrɨ ɨutɨto' kon i'ma'kasa' auya'nokon pʉra iye'tane Ka'pon, Papa winon uye'to' oton,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya rɨ ta'pʉ, “Tʉusenupasen esi pʉra iyesi tʉti'saai entai, mɨrɨ pe pʉra ipoitorʉ pe te'sen tesa' entai.</li>
      <li>Tʉusenupasen e'to' pe iyesi tʉti'saai kasa, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipoitorʉ kanan tesa' kasa rɨ. Ɨutɨ esa' pe te'sen esakʉ pe iyesi yau Pirɨsipupʉ tukai', mɨrɨ entai kuru rɨ si to' uya itiwʉ' tawon kon esakʉ!</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pɨ', to' pɨ' kenari'nʉntʉu. Ɨ'rɨ pʉra rɨ iyesi mɨrɨ iwapu'tɨsa' te'nɨponkasen pen, mɨrɨ pe pʉra onansa' i'tu pʉra te'sen.</li>
      <li>Ewarupɨ yau kanpana'tɨyatʉi'ne' ekamatɨ' wʉi nai; apana kon ya' ɨyetarerumʉ'pʉ kon ekamatɨ' ɨutɨ nakapu ponsi'kɨ.</li>
      <li>Ɨpun kon wɨnin nan pɨ' kenari'nʉntʉu, aya'kwarʉ kon wɨnin nan pen nɨ pɨ'. E'tane ru'ku, kʉrɨ pɨ' enari'nʉntɨ', asa'rɨ rɨ marɨ ɨpun mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ aya'kwarʉ wɨnin pɨ' ekota'man nɨto' yau.</li>
      <li>Asa'ron kon pe' toron amʉ' tekʉrʉpo'pomasan pen tikin nan pʉrata punu'pɨ kaisa rɨ? E'tane tikin nan nɨ to' tonpa uta'mo'ka pen mɨrɨ non pona ɨkʉipʉnʉ wanmʉra.</li>
      <li>A'pai i'po' tu'kanoro esi tanporo i'tusa' pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ wenai, kenari'nʉntʉu, i'nʉnkena' ton ɨmɨrɨ'nokon, tu'kan kon toron amʉ' entaino kon.</li>
      <li>“Ɨnʉ' rɨ uyekamayai'ne', ‘I'nai rɨ iyesi tukai',’ ka'pon amʉ' rau, urɨ uya rɨ nɨrɨ ekama, ‘I'nai rɨ iyesi tukai',’ ukʉipʉnʉ, Epʉn pon rau.</li>
      <li>E'tane ɨnʉ' rɨ, unonkayai'ne' ka'pon amʉ' rau, urɨ uya rɨ nɨrɨ inonka mɨrɨ ukʉipʉnʉ, Epʉn pon rau.</li>
      <li>“Serɨ non pona tʉusewankamai' pʉra e'nɨto' ne'sa' uya tukai' ke'tʉu,” ta'pʉ Sises uya. “Tʉusewankamai' pʉra e'nɨto' ne'se'na uye'sa' pen, e'tane supara ne'sa' uya.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra uye'sa' rɨ tasa': “‘warawo' era'tɨto' pe tʉkʉipʉnʉ ewa'noma pɨ', uri'san tʉsan ewa'noma pɨ', ipa'se tewo'pʉ ewa'noma pɨ'— ka'pon eyaton pe itiwʉ' tawon kon nɨ enato' oton,’” tawon.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Ɨnʉ' rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ tʉkʉipʉnʉ, tʉsan i'nʉnkanin urɨ i'nʉnka tʉuya entai esi mɨrɨ upoitorʉ ye' pe pʉra rɨ. Ɨnʉ' rɨ kʉrɨ tʉmu, mɨrɨ pe pʉra tensi i'nʉnkanin urɨ i'nʉnka tʉuya entai esi mɨrɨ upoitorʉ ye' pe pʉra rɨ,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉkurusukuui tanʉnse upɨkɨrɨ ɨtɨpai pʉra na'ne' esi uiwano' pe pʉra.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' rɨ kʉrɨ tʉuko'manto' eporo pɨ' na'ne' uya tʉuko'manto' nonka rɨ mɨrɨ. Ɨnʉ' rɨ kʉrɨ tʉuko'manto' nonkanin nʉ'pʉ uwenai uya tʉuko'manto' epoto' oton mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ miyarɨ rɨ, “Kʉrɨ ayanʉnyai'ne' uya uyanʉmʉ rɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kʉrɨ uyanʉnyai'ne' uya kʉrɨ uyenno'nin nʉ'pʉ anʉmʉ.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' uya Papa Maimu anin ereutanʉ'sa' a'tai, Papa Maimu anin pe iyesi pɨ' uya itepe'pʉ tonpa eporo mɨrɨ tepe'pʉ eporo iya a'tai. Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ ipokena' ka'pon ereutanʉ'sa' a'tai, ipokena' pe iyesi pɨ', kʉrɨ rɨ uya rɨ ipokena' ka'pon epe'pʉ tonpa eporo mɨrɨ tepe'pʉ eporo iya a'tai.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨnʉ' uya pʉsamoro sepa' nan nʉ'kwɨ rɨ o'pa yau komi' tuna ke rʉ'kwɨ rɨ, apʉne pʉra upoitorʉ pe to' esi pɨ', i'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, tepe'pʉ nonka iya pen kuru rɨ mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>12 kaisaron kon tʉpoitorʉ ton auro'ka tʉpo, Sises utɨ'pʉ mɨrɨ pata apai itekare ekamai' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon amʉ' enupai' Kiyarari po'nan pata ton yau.</li>
      <li>Isaan Pa'tes uya etasa' a'tai pariki'si tawonsi'kɨ Kʉrai nʉkupʉnʉ, tʉpoitorʉ ton ennoko'pʉ iya</li>
      <li>ekama'popɨ'se'na, “Ɨmɨrɨ pe' kʉrɨ rɨ tʉuye'ton ta'pʉ rʉ'pʉ ipɨ', tʉron nɨ rɨ katɨ uyepʉ enupɨkɨrɨ ina e'to' nai?” tukai'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' eikʉ'pʉ, “Enna'potɨ', ɨneta'pʉ kon mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨnene'pʉ kon ekamatantɨ' Isaan pɨ';</li>
      <li>tenku'na' nan enasa' man ennin nan pe; ise'mesa' kon enasa' man tʉusasan pe; erekʉ'pa' nan usepi'tɨsa' man; etanin nan pen enasa' man etanin pe; eke' amʉ' e'mʉ'sa'kasa' man, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ wakʉ itekare usekamasa' man entu'manin nan pana ya'.</li>
      <li>Pori' pe ka'pon esi mɨrɨ tʉuta'mo'kasen pen unkupʉnʉ uriya',” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Isaan poitorʉ ton enna'po koro'tau, Sises epiya'tɨ'pʉ anpisin auro'ka pɨ' Isaan pɨ', “Ɨ'rɨ ense'na ɨutɨ'pʉ kon rɨmono' ta'? Wana' rɨ ari'ma a'setun uya ense'na?</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe pʉra iyesi yau, ɨ'rɨ ken ense'na ɨutɨ'pʉ kon? Wakʉ pe katɨ ka'pon epontɨpɨ'sa' ense'na? Kane. Kamoro rupɨ ton nin esi mɨrɨ epe'kena' ton ipon ton esi kin iwʉ' tawon kon.</li>
      <li>Ɨ'rɨ kuru ken ense'na ɨutɨ'pʉ kon? Pu'kena' katɨ? Ewai' apana'tɨ uya 'nokon, pu'kena' entaino rɨ.</li>
      <li>Pʉse rɨ sa'ne si kʉrɨ rɨ ko iye'menukasa' itekare usauro'sa' rʉ'pʉ ipɨ': “‘Umaimu ekamanin ennoko uya mɨrɨ arawɨrɨ, ɨye'ma konekanin pe awapiya,’ ta'pʉ rʉ'pʉ ipɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, kamo uri'sami'si amʉ' nentunʉkʉ'san koro'tau pʉra iyesi mɨrɨ eke Isaan Pa'tes entaino; mɨrɨ e'tane, kʉrɨ aiko pe te'sen Epʉn po esa' wannɨ pe e'nɨto' yawon esi eke pe Isaan entai.</li>
      <li>Isaan Pa'tes weyu rʉ'pʉ si'kɨrɨ serɨ pʉ'kʉ pona, Epʉn po esa' wannɨ pe e'nɨto' uta'tu'man pɨ' man meruntɨ pe, mɨrɨpan a'si pɨ' meruntɨ ton ka'pon amʉ' man.</li>
      <li>Tanporon kon nɨ pu'kena' amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main usenupan nɨto' ipɨ' uya Papa Maimu ekama'pʉ, Isaan Pa'tes uyepʉ pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ.</li>
      <li>Serɨ si to' maimu anapurɨpai ɨwesi kon yau, Isaan nɨ si kʉrɨ rɨ Iraisa uyepʉ tasa' rʉ'pʉ ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Kʉrɨ rɨ tʉpana ke na'ne' tɨwɨ netai,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya kanan takaa'pʉ, “Ɨnʉ' yan kasa to' esi tukai' serɨ a'taino kon ekama uya? Mʉre amʉ' ereutapɨ'sa' kʉrʉpo'po pata'se' yau na'ne' tʉukɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨ'san tʉron kon pɨ' kasa to' esi:</li>
      <li>“‘Sarakuwa turunpa'pʉ ina uya, e'tane aumanʉnsa' kon pʉra iyesi. Eke' eremu pɨ' ina userenka'pʉ, e'tane tʉuta'kwarʉkai' aukaransa' kon pʉra iyesi,’ tawon nan kasa.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra Isaan uyee'pʉ iyenta'na mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨ'rɨ ensi iya pʉra, mɨrɨpan pɨ', ‘Makoi esi iyau,’ ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon, Papa winon uyee'pʉ tenta'nasen nɨ waain ensinin nɨ, mɨrɨpan pɨ', ‘Eke pe tenta'nasen, te'taripasen,’ ta'pʉ ipɨ'. ‘Pʉrata amʉranʉ'nin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉmakooikena' nan nɨ tonpa pe iyesi,’ ta'pʉ to' uya. E'tane Papa pu'ketʉ usi'tu mɨrɨ i'napai rɨ inkupʉnʉ pɨkɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises usaurokʉ'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' pata yau to' eno'ma pe, eke Papa tʉrawasooi kupʉ'pʉ tʉuya yau'ne, apʉne pʉra tʉmakooi kon apai to' era'tɨ kasa pʉra.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsɨ sɨ, Korasin pon kon! Ɨsɨ sɨ, Pe'saita pon kon! Ɨ'koro'tau'nokon ne'ku'ai'ne' eke Papa tʉrawasooi e'ku'sa' pe iyesi yau Taya mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Saitan pon kon koro'tau, pena rɨ to' era'tɨ'pʉ nesii'no tʉmakooi kon apai. To' epontɨpɨ'sa' esi'pʉ nesii'no isa'ka'si ya', urumɨrʉ'pʉ yau to' nesii'no.</li>
      <li>E'tane apana'tɨ uya 'nokon Taya mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Saitan pon kon uya parɨ imoronkato' oton eseru aimenka weyu e'seposa' a'tai ɨmɨrɨ'nokon entai.</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon, Ka'paneyan pon kon, autanʉnto' oton kon pe' ka'takʉi'? Kane! I'na' auta'mo'kato' oton kon mɨrɨ ta'mu kenan pen nɨ ya'. Ɨ'koro'tau'nokon ne'ku'ai'ne' eke Papa tʉrawasooi e'ku'sa' pe iyesi yau Satan po, moro rɨ mɨrɨ pata nesii'no serɨ pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane pʉra rɨ ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, Satan pon kon uya parɨ imoronkato' oton eseru aimenka weyu e'seposa' a'tai ɨmɨrɨ'nokon entai,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Kanyapurɨpɨ'ai', Papai, Epʉn mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ non Epuru, apʉne pʉra serɨ ton onansa' auya pɨ' pu'kena' ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ isenupasa' kon piyapai, mɨrɨpan enpoikasa' auya pɨ' aiko ton mʉre amʉ' ena'.</li>
      <li>Ewai' Papai, serɨ ku'sa' auya i'se ɨwe'to' awɨrɨ pori' pe ɨku'nin pe iyesi pɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Tʉwɨpʉrema tʉpo, ka'pon amʉ' auro'ka pɨ' iye'sara'tɨ'pʉ. “Tanporon nɨ esi ukʉipʉnʉ nʉnonka'pʉ pe uyena'. Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ imu i'tu pʉra iyesi, e'tane ikʉipʉnʉ uya rɨken i'tu. Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ ikʉipʉnʉ i'tu pʉra iyesi, e'tane imu uya rɨken i'tu mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kamo nɨrɨ imu na'ne' e'to' ɨnenpoikapai itena' ton,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsi'tɨ' ɨmɨrɨ'nokon iseta'kasa' kon, e'tape'ne' esa' pe te'san, ɨumoronkapʉ kon pa ɨku'to' kon pe uya.</li>
      <li>Uwari'sarʉ apon anʉntɨ' ɨpona'nokon, ɨusenupa kon pa upɨ', ɨsɨ pen nɨ urɨ, mɨ pe te'ku'sen pen nɨ uyewan yau, aya'kwarʉ kon umoronka'to' eporo kon pa.</li>
      <li>Wakʉ rɨ mɨrɨ uwari'sarʉ apon, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ uwari'sarʉ esi asi'ono pe,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises utɨ'pʉ a'nai' e'kwa nawɨrɨ Sapa' a'tai. Ipoitorʉ ton esi'pʉ iwan pe, mɨrɨpan kon e'sara'tɨ'pʉ a'nai' e'suruupɨ'sa' i'kwɨ'pɨtʉ pɨ', mɨrɨpan kon uya ɨku'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Pari'si amʉ' uya serɨ e'kupʉ ensa' a'tai, Sises pɨ' ta'pʉ to' uya, “Apʉne enkɨ, ɨpoitorʉ ton uya Main uya tʉku'sen pen Sapa' a'tai tasa' rʉ'pʉ kupʉ,” ta'pʉ to' uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' eikʉ'pʉ, “Kin Tepi' nʉkupʉ'pʉ pe' etasa' auya'nokon pʉra nai, tʉpoitorʉ ton pokon pe iwan pe tesi kon a'tai?</li>
      <li>Iyewomʉ'pʉ Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' ta' tʉtonpa ton pokon pe mɨrɨpan kon uya ipʉremasa' pʉreti ɨku'pʉ, to' nʉkupʉnʉ tasa' pen nɨ Main uya e'tane. Papa ena' use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan yu pe rɨken te'sen ɨku'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ rɨken pe pʉra, ene auya'nokon pʉra pe' iyesi Main yau Papa ena' use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan uya Papa iwʉ' tau Sapa' a'tai Main i'kwɨtʉ'pʉ te'tʉrawasoma kon winɨ, e'tane wakʉ pe rɨ to' esi?</li>
      <li>“Ɨpɨ'nokon ekama uya serɨ; moro rɨ iyesi serɨ yau eke pe te'sen Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' entaino.</li>
      <li>I'tusa' auya'nokon pe iyesi yau ɨ'rɨ ta e'kwa pe serɨ main esi tukai', ‘Ɨsentu'kena' pe ɨwesi kon i'se esi, o' ke ɨuse'ma kon i'se esi pen,’ tawon, wakʉ ton nɨ eno'masa' auya'nokon nesii'no pen.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra Ka'pon, Papa winon esi Sapa' Epuru pe rɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ apai tʉutɨi', itɨ'pʉ Esuwerʉ amʉ' usenupato' iwʉ' ta'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau, itemiyatʉ aipʉtasa' amʉrasa' ka'pon esi'pʉ. Sises eseru'tɨto' pe tʉuya'nokon, mɨrɨ yawon kon ka'pon amʉ' uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Main awɨrɨ pe' e'nɨ pe iyesi mɨrɨ, Sapa' a'tai ka'pon epi'tɨsa' a'tai?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “Karimeru esa' pe ɨwesi kon yau mɨrɨpan uta'mo'ka yau akasa' ya' Sapa' a'tai, ta'sii' pe' anʉmʉ auya'nokon pen?</li>
      <li>Ka'pon esi i'nʉnkena' pe karimeru entai. Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', Sapa' a'tai ka'pon pika'tɨsa' esi Main awɨrɨ e'nɨ pe rɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan a'tai, “Ɨyemiyatʉ ɨnka',” ta'pʉ Sises uya ka'pon pɨ', mɨrɨpan uya temiyatʉ ɨnka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan enna'po'pʉ tesi'pʉ ya', itemiyatʉ ratoi kasa rɨ marɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane si Pari'si amʉ' epa'kasa' utɨ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon ekoneka'pʉ iwɨto' tʉuya'nokon pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya Pari'si amʉ' ekonekasa' i'tusa' a'tai, itɨ'pʉ mɨrɨ pata apai. Tu'kan kon ka'pon amʉ' utɨ'pʉ ipɨkɨrɨ, mɨrɨ yau to' koro'tau takuru'kena' nan esi'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon epi'tɨpɨtʉ'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>To' panama'pʉ iya tʉron kon pɨ' kʉrɨ rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ ta to' uya namai' tʉpɨ'.</li>
      <li>Serɨ kupʉ'pʉ iya pu'kena' Aisaya yai Papa usaurokʉ'pʉ uta'ku'tɨto' pe:</li>
      <li>“Upoitorʉ pe, unanʉmʉ'pʉ pʉse rɨ. Ipan pe uni'nʉnkanʉ, mɨrɨpan pɨ' epori'ma. Uya'kwarʉ ennoko uya mɨrɨ ipona, mɨrɨpan uya wakʉ pe e'nɨ eseru ekamato' oton tanporon kon ka'pon amʉ' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan usauro'to' oton ama'ai; eke pe asanta tau isauro'to' oton pen.</li>
      <li>Iye'sekeukasa' wana' i'kwɨtʉ iya pen, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ usenkʉ'nɨ poken te'sen apo' enkʉ'nʉkʉ iya pen, wakʉ ena itentai pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ.</li>
      <li>Itese' yau tanporon kon ka'pon amʉ' uya te'ku'to' kon tʉto' oton,” tawon.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau, tʉron kon ka'pon amʉ' uya makoi yen ka'pon nee'pʉ Sises piya'. Kʉrɨ rɨ ka'pon esi'pʉ tenku'nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉusauro'sen pen. Mɨrɨpan epi'tɨ'pʉ Sises uya makoi a'kwarʉ tenpa'kai', mɨrɨpan enasa' esi'pʉ tʉusauro'sen pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ennin pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, ka'pon amʉ' usewansiuka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya, “Tepi' pa rʉ'pʉ pe pe' iyesi serɨ, itenupɨkɨrɨ e'nɨto' Me'saya?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>E'tane Pari'si amʉ' uya serɨ etasa' tʉuya'nokon a'tai, “Pirɨsipupʉ, makoi amʉ' epuru uya tʉpika'tɨi' makoi amʉ' enpa'kapɨtʉ pʉse rɨ uya mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' usenuminkato' i'tusa' esi'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Tanporo esa' wannɨ pe te'san epantakapɨ'sa' a'tai ɨsewa'nomai' tiwano' kon pe rɨ, to' uma'ta mɨrɨ; pata mɨrɨ pe pʉra ɨsiwʉ' tawon kon ka'pon amʉ' epantakapɨ'sa' a'tai ɨsewa'nomai' tiwano' kon pe rɨ uko'mamʉ pen nɨ mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa si iyesi Se'tan uya Se'tan nɨrɨ enpa'kasa' a'tai, tiwano' pe rɨ iyepantakasa' pe iyesi ɨsewa'nomai'; mɨrɨ kasa iyesi a'tai, nai kasa ken Se'tan e'to' itesa' pe uko'mamʉ?</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ makoi amʉ' enpa'ka uya pe iyesi yau Pirɨsipupʉ ke, ɨnʉ' ke ken ɨpoitorʉ kon to' enpa'kanin nan? To' nin si esi mɨrɨ ɨyeseru kon aimenkanin nan pe.</li>
      <li>E'tane makoi amʉ' enpa'ka uya pe iyesi yau Papa A'kwarʉ ke, Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe nin si uye'sa' mɨrɨ ɨpona'nokon.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pe pʉra kanan, nai kasa ɨnʉ' rɨ ewomʉ pana'pan iwʉ' ta' itapuruui ton ase'na? Wapiya auronpɨ'sa' a'tai rɨ nin iye'kupʉ. Mɨrɨ a'tai nin itimamin arɨ iya itiwʉ' tapai.</li>
      <li>“Kʉrɨ rɨ ka'pon utonpa pe pʉra na'ne' esi mɨrɨ uyeyaton pe; kʉrɨ rɨ amʉranʉkʉ iya pʉra na'ne' uya'kɨrɨ uya, ita'nʉkʉ mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, tanporon nɨ makoi mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Papa sapema pe isauro'sa' kon ka'pon amʉ' pɨ' rɨ usentu'man, e'tane Iya'kwarʉ sapema pe isauro'sa' kon pɨ' usentu'man pen nɨ.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' rɨ Ka'pon, Papa winon pɨ' ewa'noma pe isauro'sa' rʉ'pʉ pɨ' usentu'man, e'tane ewa'noma pe Wakʉ A'kwarʉ pɨ' isauro'sa' rʉ'pʉ pɨ' usentu'man pen nɨ, serɨ a'tai'ne mɨrɨ pe pʉra serɨ entawon a'tai'ne rɨ.</li>
      <li>“Wakʉ pe yʉi iku'kɨ; mɨrɨ a'tai, wakʉ pe iteperu esi mɨrɨ. Mɨrɨ pe pʉra, ɨri pe yʉi iku'kɨ; mɨrɨ a'tai, ɨri pe rɨ iteperu esi mɨrɨ, apʉne pʉra yʉi usi'tu mɨrɨ iteperu winɨ.</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon ɨkʉi munkɨ ton! Nai kasa ɨmɨrɨ'nokon ɨri pe te'san usaurokʉ wakʉ pe? Apʉne pʉra ɨyewan kon epe'tɨsa' apaino kuru enpa'ka auya'nokon mɨrɨ anta kon yai.</li>
      <li>Wakʉ ka'pon uya wakʉ ton enpa'ka mɨrɨ wakʉ usentɨsa' tʉyau, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨri ka'pon uya ɨri enpa'ka mɨrɨ ɨri usentɨsa' tʉyau.</li>
      <li>Serɨ ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, Papa uya ka'pon amʉ' aimenkato' oton tanporon nɨ tʉusenuminkai' pʉra rɨ to' usauro'sa' rʉ'pʉ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Wakʉ amaimu kon winɨ ayanʉnto' oton kon, ɨri amaimu kon winɨ ɨyeno'mato' oton kon,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Pari'si amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main pɨ' enupanin nan uya ta'pʉ Sises pɨ', “Ti'sa, eke Papa tʉrawasooi ɨi'tuto' ipɨkɨrɨ kupʉ auya ɨnenpai ina man,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>To' maimu eikʉ'pʉ iya, “Ɨri ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ iyemari'masa' ekumankanin nan ka'pon amʉ' uya eke Papa tʉrawasooi i'tuto' tʉuya'nokon ipɨkɨrɨ ekama'po. Ikupʉ uya pen e'tane Isona, pu'kena' pɨ' i'tuto' ipɨ' rʉ'pʉ rɨken kupʉ uya.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra Isona esi'pʉ osorʉwau wʉi mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ osorʉwau ewarupɨ nɨrɨ eke moro' ewan yau. Mɨrɨ na'ne' kasa, Ka'pon, Papa winon uko'manto' oton osorʉwau wʉi mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ osorʉwau ewarupɨ non ewan yau.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' Ninipa pon kon e'mʉ'sa'kato' oton eseru aimenka weyu a'tai serɨ a'taino kon pokon pe to' eno'ma pe; apʉne pʉra to' era'tɨ'pʉ tʉmakooi kon apai Isona uya itekare ekama pɨ'. Serɨ pe eke Isona entaino man serɨ yau.</li>
      <li>Kwin, wʉi enu uye'to' kamisi winon e'mʉ'sa'kato' oton eseru aimenka weyu a'tai serɨ a'taino kon pokon pe to' eno'ma pe; apʉne pʉra iye'sa' wenai non u'matʉ apai Saraman pu'ketʉ etase'na. Serɨ pe eke Saraman entaino man serɨ yau,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>“Makoi a'kwarʉ epa'kasa' a'tai ka'pon apai, itɨ mɨrɨ tʉ'kenan pata ya'. Tereutato' yau warinpa pɨ', mɨrɨpan eporo iya pʉra iyesi.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, ‘Enna'po serɨ ɨutɨ unnɨmɨ'pʉ ta',’ ta iya. Iye'sa' a'tai, eporo iya itawon pʉra, wakʉ pe akorokasa' pe mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ikonekasa' pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, itɨ 7 kaisaron kon a'kwarʉ ton ɨri ton kuru tentaino kon nepʉ iya ta'kɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan kon ewomʉ, to' uko'mamʉ mɨrɨ yau. Mɨrɨ a'tai, pʉse rɨ ka'pon esi mɨrɨ ɨri pe kuru wapiya tesi'pʉ entai. Mɨrɨ na'ne' kasa, ɨmɨrɨ'nokon ɨri pe nʉko'manyai'ne' nan serɨ a'taino kon e'to' oton,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Anpisin auro'ka pɨ' Sises esi koro'tau rɨ marɨ, isan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ iyakon non e'soto'pɨ'sa' esi'pʉ pʉroroi po. Iya'kɨrɨ asauro'pai to' esi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon uya ipana'tɨ'pʉ, “Asan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ayakon non e'soto'pɨ'sa' man pʉroroi po. Ayauro'kapai to' esi,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Eikʉ'pʉ iya, “Ɨnʉ' si usan? Ɨnʉ' yan si uyakon non?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Tʉpoitorʉ ton enusimai'ma ta'pʉ iya, “Pʉsamo nin usanon mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ uyakon non.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra ɨnʉ' rɨ ukʉipʉnʉ, Epʉn pon e'to' i'se ku'nin esi mɨrɨ, uyakon pe, uparusi pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ usan pe,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mɨrɨ wʉi a'tai si, Sises epa'ka'pʉ ɨutɨ tapai, mɨrɨpan utɨsa' ereuta'pʉ parau ku'pɨri e'pi po.</li>
      <li>Tu'ke kuru rɨ anpisin pe ka'pon amʉ' esi pɨ' tʉwoi, kanau ya' tekanwa'tɨi' iyereuta'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' e'tane a'mun po.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, tu'kan pɨ' rɨ to' auro'ka'pʉ iya panton yai. “Umɨ pɨ' te'sen utɨ'pʉ kiyari ye' pɨnse'na tʉpa'karakai'.</li>
      <li>Ipa'karaka iya koro'tau, tʉron nɨ ton uta'pokʉ'pʉ asanta ta'. Toron amʉ' uyee'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya ɨku'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Tʉron nɨ uta'pokʉ'pʉ tɨ' pe te'sen ya' eke pe pʉra te'sen non ya'. Iya'ta'pʉ inke pʉra, apʉne pʉra i'nau pʉra non esi ke.</li>
      <li>E'tane wʉi enu enu'sa' a'tai, a'ne' pe ipuru'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan aipʉta'pʉ apʉne pʉra imi' utɨpɨ'sa' pʉra iyesi wenai.</li>
      <li>Tʉron nɨ ton uta'pokʉ'pʉ tikʉkenan nʉ'ta', mɨrɨpan ɨmɨ'nɨ'ta a'ta uya ɨwɨtanʉkʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ e'tane rɨ, tʉron nɨ ton uta'pokʉ'pʉ wakʉ non ya', mɨrɨpan epeta'pʉ 100 kaisarɨ rɨ, 60 mɨrɨ pe pʉra 30 kaisarɨ rɨ ite'kwa ipɨmɨ'pʉ entai rɨ.</li>
      <li>Kʉrɨ rɨ tʉpana ke na'ne' tɨwɨ netai,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Ipoitorʉ ton uyee'pʉ ipiya' ekama'pose'na, “Ɨ'rɨ pe iyesi pɨ' ka'pon amʉ' auro'ka auya panton yai?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>To' eikʉ'pʉ iya, “Ɨnʉ' ni'tunʉ pen nɨ ama'aino Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe i'tu kon pa ɨyena'nokon itʉsa', e'tane to' ena' itʉsa' pʉra iyesi.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' rɨ itesa' pe te'sen repa mɨrɨ miyarɨ rɨ, mɨrɨpan e'to' pe eke pe itesa' pe. Ɨnʉ' rɨ ɨ'rɨ esa' pen nɨ enapai imo'ka mɨrɨ itenawon nʉ'kwɨ rɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pɨ' to' auro'ka uya mɨrɨ panton yai: “Ennin pe rɨ to' e'tane, to' uya ene pʉra iyesi pɨ'; etanin pe rɨ to' e'tane, to' uya eta mɨrɨ pe pʉra ito'ka'nʉkʉ pʉra iyesi pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Pu'kena' Aisaya nekama'pʉ uta'ku'tɨsa' to' pɨ': “‘Eta pɨ' rɨ ɨwe'to' oton e'tane, ito'ka'nʉkʉ auya pʉra iye'to' oton; ene pɨ' rɨ miyarɨ rɨ ɨwe'to' oton e'tane, ento' auya oton pen.</li>
      <li>Pʉsamoro ka'pon amʉ' ewan enasa' sa'man pe; to' uya eta pʉra rɨ iyesi tʉpana kon ke, tenu kon a'kopɨ'sa' to' uya, tenu kon ke to' uya ene nesii'no, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉpana kon ke to' netai'no, tewan kon ke to' nʉto'ka'nʉkʉi'no, to' nera'tɨi'no, mɨrɨpan kon sepi'tɨi'no,’ tawon.</li>
      <li>E'tane wakʉ pe ɨyenu kon esi mɨrɨ, apʉne pʉra ene iya pɨ', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ apana kon eta iya pɨ'.</li>
      <li>I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, tu'kan kon nɨ pu'kena' amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipokena' ton ka'pon amʉ' esi'pʉ menyatʉi'ne' ɨnenpai e'tane, to' uya ene'pʉ pen; mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ metayatʉi'ne' ɨnetapai e'tane, to' uya eta'pʉ pen,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>“Etatɨ' ɨ'rɨ ta e'kwa pe tʉpa'karakai' te'pɨnsen pantomʉ esi tukai':</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ itekare eta a'tai Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe pɨ', e'tane ito'ka'nʉkʉ iya pʉra iyesi, Makoi uyepʉ itewan ya' ipa'karakasa' mo'kase'na. Serɨ esi ite' ipa'karakasa' asanta ta'.</li>
      <li>Kʉrɨ rɨ ite' uta'po'sa' na'ne' tɨ' pona kasa esi ka'pon Main etanin nʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya inke pʉra anʉmʉ'pʉ pori' pe esii'ma.</li>
      <li>E'tane imi' pʉra iyesi wenai, inke pʉra kuru itano'ma. Manenpanin mɨrɨ pe pʉra kota'manin uye'sa' a'tai Main wenai, inke pʉra kuru ita'mo'ka.</li>
      <li>Kʉrɨ rɨ ite' ita'po'sa' rʉ'pʉ tikʉkenan nʉ'ta' esi mɨrɨ ka'pon Main etanin nʉ'pʉ, e'tane tʉusewankamasen wakʉ pe ɨko'manpai tesi pɨ', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ imaminke' pe te'to' pɨ' tʉusenku'tɨsen. Mɨrɨ uya ɨwɨtanʉkʉ, tepetasen pe pʉra ikupʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane kʉrɨ rɨ ite' ita'po'sa' rʉ'pʉ wakʉ non ya' esi ka'pon Main etanin mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ito'ka'nʉ'nin nɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan epeta 100 kaisa rɨ'ne rɨ, 60 kaisa rɨ'ne rɨ, mɨrɨ pe pʉra 30 kaisa rɨ'ne rɨ ite'kwa ipa'karakasa' rʉ'pʉ entai,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya tʉron nɨ panton ekama'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' pɨ', “Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe esi ka'pon tʉpa'karakai' wakʉ kiyari ye' pɨnnin nʉ'pʉ tʉmainarʉ yau kasa.</li>
      <li>Ewarupɨ nau, kʉrɨ rɨ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipoitorʉ ton e'nʉnsa' e'tane, iteyaton uyee'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya wana' e' pɨmɨ'pʉ mɨrɨ rɨ umɨ yau, mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Emennʉ'pʉ rɨ, kiyari ye' a'ta'pʉ epetan pɨ' iye'sara'tɨ'pʉ e'tane, ipoitorʉ ton uya wana' e' a'tasa' ene'pʉ kiyari ye' koro'tau.</li>
      <li>Ipoitorʉ ton utɨ'pʉ tepuru kon piya', mɨrɨpan kon uya, ‘Ina epuru, wakʉ sa'ne kiyari ye' pɨntai ina ko, ina apiyontɨ'pʉ auya awɨrɨ rɨ, e'tane nai awon wana' e' a'tasa'?’ ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“To' epuru uya nin si, ‘Uyeyaton uya rɨ ipɨnsa' pe iyesi mɨrɨ,’ ta'pʉ to' pɨ'. “‘Wana' ken pe' nai' ina utɨ i'se me'an?’ ta'pʉ ipoitorʉ ton uya.</li>
      <li>“E'tane, ‘Kane, wana' na auya'nokon koro'tau, iya'tai pʉra kiyari ye' kanan na auya'nokon esi,’ ta'pʉ to' epuru uya to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>‘Tɨwɨ asa'rɨ rɨ nʉsemo'kai iteperu akʉ'pʉsa' anʉmʉ weyu e'seporo pona rɨ. Mɨrɨ a'tai, anʉnnin nan apiyontɨto' pe uya, wapiya kuru wana' nato' pe to' uya, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ to' uya auronpɨ'to' pe iyepo'tɨpɨ'to' pe, mɨrɨ tʉpo nin si to' uya a'nai' i'kwɨ'pɨ'to' pe, mɨrɨpan amʉranʉ'to' pe to' uya ui'kiyari iwʉ' ta',’ ta'pʉ itepuru uya tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ',” ta'pʉ Sises uya anpisin ka'pon amʉ' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Tʉron nɨ panton ekama'pʉ Sises uya ka'pon amʉ' pɨ', “Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe esi kiyari ye' mosta' itese' ena'pɨ, ka'pon nʉpɨmɨnʉ tʉmainarʉ yau kasa.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ ena'pɨ esi aiko ton kuru tʉron nɨ ena'pɨ pokon pe i'tu a'tai, e'tane eke pe isemo'ka tʉron kon umɨ yau te'sen kiyari ye' entai, mɨrɨpan usemo'ka eke yʉi pe, toron amʉ' rɨ esi ipanta po'ne,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉron nɨ kanan panton ekama'pʉ Sises uya, “Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe esi pʉrowa a'sarutanʉ'nin kasa, uri'san nanʉmʉnʉ, mɨrɨpan uya pʉrowa pokon pe eke pe iki'ma, tanporo ipun yau iyena pʉ'kʉ pona,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya tanporo serɨ ton ekama'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' anpisin ton pɨ' panton yai; ɨ'rɨ ke rɨ panton yai pʉra to' auro'ka iya pʉra iye'pɨtʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Serɨ kupʉ'pʉ iya, pena rɨ Papa nekama'pʉ pu'kena' yai uta'ku'tɨto' pe: “Panton yai ka'pon amʉ' auro'kato' uya oton, non ekoneka a'tai rɨ iye'so'nansa' rʉ'pʉ ekamato' uya oton,” tawon.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya anpisin ka'pon amʉ' nɨmɨ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ itau te'to' ɨutɨ ta'. Ipoitorʉ ton utɨ'pʉ iya'kɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan kon uya, “Apʉne, ɨ'rɨ ta e'kwa pe wana' umɨ yawon esi tukai' ekama',” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' eikʉ'pʉ, “Kʉrɨ wakʉ itena'pɨ pɨnnin nʉ'pʉ tʉpa'karakai' esi Ka'pon, Papa winon.</li>
      <li>Umɨ esi ka'pon amʉ' serɨ non po te'san, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ wakʉ kiyari ye' esi esa' wannɨ pe e'nɨ munkɨ amʉ'; wana' esi Makoi munkɨ amʉ' ekamanin pe,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ eyaton, wana' pɨnnin nʉ'pʉ esi Makoi. Kiyari akʉ'pʉsa' anʉmʉ esi non weyu u'ma'sa' a'taino, kiyari anʉnnin nan esi inserʉ amʉ'.</li>
      <li>“Wana' na mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipo'tɨ kasa, mɨrɨ kasa si iye'to' oton pata weyu u'ma'sa' a'tai.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon, Papa winon uya tinserʉʉi ton enno'to' oton serɨ non pona, mɨrɨpan kon uya ɨri ku'nin nʉ'san mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉtonpa kon e'makoima emapu'tɨnin nʉ'san amʉranʉ'to' oton Papa pata'se' yapai,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan kon eno'mato' to' uya oton apo' ya'. Mɨrɨ yau, to' ukaranto' oton, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉyɨ kon kɨtɨtɨi'mato' oton to' uya.</li>
      <li>E'tane ipokena' ton e'wei'tɨto' oton wʉi enu kasa tʉkʉipʉnʉ kon e'to' esa' wannɨ pe yau. Kʉrɨ rɨ tʉpana ke na'ne' tɨwɨ netai,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Miyarɨ rɨ ka'pon amʉ' enupa'pʉ Sises uya, “Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe esi i'nʉnkena' mamin umɨ yau onansa' te'sen kasa. Mɨrɨpan eposa' ka'pon uya a'tai, iu'na'tɨkapʉ iya kanan, mɨrɨpan esi pori' pe, mɨrɨpan uya tanporo timamin kʉrʉpo'poma, mɨrɨpan epe'pʉ ke mɨrɨ non e'ma iya.</li>
      <li>“Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe esi epe'kena' mokon pun tʉne'manʉ ton warinpa kʉrʉpo'po pokon uya na'ne' kasa.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan eposa' tʉuya a'tai, itɨ tanporo timamin kʉrʉpo'pomai', mɨrɨpan epe'pʉ pʉrata ke mɨrɨ mokon pun e'mato' pe tʉuya.</li>
      <li>“Se kasa kanan Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe esi punwe esi na'ne' kasa ka'pon amʉ' nʉtʉrʉnʉ parau ku'pɨri ka', mɨrɨpan kon uya ɨ'si'tau rɨ moro' amʉ' a'si.</li>
      <li>Punwe epe'tɨsa' a'tai, to' uya ipi'sikʉ makʉi'. Tereutai', tansan pe te'san menkato' pe tʉuya'nokon pa'siki'ti ya', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tansan pen ma'kɨrɨi'ma.</li>
      <li>Serɨ kasa si iye'to' oton pata weyu u'ma'sa' a'tai. Inserʉ amʉ' uye'to' oton, mɨrɨpan kon uya ɨri ton ka'pon amʉ' menkato' oton ipokena' ton piyapai,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan kon uya ɨri ton ka'pon amʉ' eno'mato' oton apo' ya'. To' ukaranto' oton, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉyɨ kon kɨtɨtɨi'mato' oton to' uya mɨrɨ yau,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Usaurokʉine' ipɨ' pe' mʉto'ka'nʉ'tʉu?” ta'pʉ Sises uya tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ'. Mɨrɨ pɨ', “Ewai', ina uya ito'ka'nʉ'sa' man,” ta'pʉ ipoitorʉ ton uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pɨ' ta'pʉ iya, “Tanporon kon Main pɨ' enupanin usenupasa' Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe pɨ' esi mɨrɨ, ka'pon tiwʉ' tawon emenna' ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ penaro' ton timamin enpa'kapɨ'nin kasa,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Panton amʉ' i'ma'kasa' tʉuya a'tai, Sises utama'pʉ mɨrɨ apai.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ tʉpata'se' ya'. Ka'pon amʉ' enupa pɨ' iye'sara'tɨ'pʉ to' usenupato' iwʉ' tau. Mɨrɨpan kon usewansiuka'pʉ. “Nai yau si tʉpu'ketʉ eporo'pʉ iya tʉusauro'to' pe mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉpana'pano eke Papa tʉrawasooi ku'nin pe te'to' pe?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Kiya'pinta mu pen pe' pʉse rɨ? Meri pen pe' isan ese', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Isens, Isose', Saiman, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Isutas pokon pe' yakon non pen?</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tanporo pʉra pe' iparusi ton nai upiyau'nokon? Nai yau ken si serɨ ton epopɨtʉ'pʉ iya?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon ɨkɨnʉmʉ'pʉ ipɨ', e'tane Sises uya to' maimu eikʉ'pʉ, “Ipata'se' yau rɨken mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ itonpa ton uya pu'kena' nama pʉra iyesi,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Tu'ke eke Papa tʉrawasooi kupʉ Sises uya pʉra iyesi'pʉ mɨrɨ yau, apʉne pʉra apurɨto' to' uya pʉra iyesi pɨ'.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, kopʉna Era' uya ka'pon amʉ' nekamanʉ eta'pʉ mɨrɨ kupʉ Sises uya tukai'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' tʉpiyawon kon pɨ', “Isaan Pa'tes kʉrɨ rɨ. Iye'mʉ'sa'kasa' terikʉ'pʉ apai; mɨrɨ wenai, eke Papa tʉrawasooi kupʉ iya mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Era' uya Isaan a'sisa' mɨrɨpan auronpɨ'sa' tʉsa' pariki'si ta' esi'pʉ, Eratiyas, Piri' takon no'pʉ wenai,</li>
      <li>apʉne pʉra Isaan uya ta esi'pʉ ipɨ': “Main awɨrɨ ɨwesi pe pʉra iyesi kʉrɨ rɨ anʉnsa' auya na'ne',” ta.</li>
      <li>Era' esi'pʉ Isaan ɨnwɨpai, e'tane iyenari'nʉmʉ'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' pɨ', apʉne pʉra Isaan i'tu to' uya pɨ' pu'kena' pe.</li>
      <li>Era' uya tentu'pʉ weyu rʉ'pʉ kupʉ esi'pʉ iyenta'nato' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Eratiyas mʉre umanumʉ'pʉ to' iwano' pe. Serɨ uya Era' kupʉ'pʉ ipan pe rɨ pori' pe,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ, “Ɨ'rɨ rɨ ekama'po auya a'tai, ɨrepa uya kuru rɨ mɨrɨ,” tukai' isaurokʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Isan uya imaimu'tɨ'pʉ mɨrɨ ekama'pokɨ tukai', mɨrɨpan uya, “Isaan Pa'tes i'pai rʉ'pʉ ke urepakɨ serɨ yau parapi po,” ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Kin upokoita'pʉ tʉusaurokʉ'pʉ pɨ' ipan pe, e'tane ikupʉ uya kuru mɨrɨ tasa' tʉuya rʉ'pʉ pɨ' enta'nai' tʉnkɨ'ma'san pana yai rɨ ikupʉ iya rɨ esi'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya tʉsoisaai amʉ' apiyo'ma'pʉ inesakʉ'pʉ ku'to' pe to' uya,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan kon uya Isaan i'pairʉka'pʉ pariki'si tau.</li>
      <li>I'pai rʉ'pʉ nee'pʉ to' uya parapi po, mɨrɨpan kon uya itʉrʉ'pʉ uri'san ena', mɨrɨpan arɨ'pʉ iya tʉsan ena'.</li>
      <li>Isaan poitorʉ rʉ'san uyee'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya itekepu arɨ'pʉ iu'na'tɨto' pe tʉuya'nokon, mɨrɨpan kon utɨ'pʉ Sises pana'tɨi'.</li>
      <li>Iye'ku'sa' rʉ'pʉ etasa' tʉuya a'tai, Sises ekanwa'tɨ'pʉ kanau ya', mɨrɨpan kon utɨ'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton pokon pe tʉ'kena'pɨ ya'. Tu'kan kon nɨ ka'pon amʉ' uya serɨ eta'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon utɨ'pʉ tʉ'ta kon po Sises pɨkɨrɨ pata ton apai'ne.</li>
      <li>Sises ekanwakasa' uya tu'ke anpisin pe ka'pon amʉ' ensa' a'tai, ipan pe rɨ to' pɨ' isentu'ma'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya rɨ to' koro'tau takuru'ke'ne te'san epi'tɨpɨtʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Ko'mamʉ pe rɨ iyenaka'tane, ipoitorʉ ton uyee'pʉ ipiya', mɨrɨpan kon uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Ɨnnon sa'ne serɨ pata ko, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ pata kanan uko'manka'sa'. Ka'pon amʉ' ipana'tɨ' tiwano' kon pe ti'kiyari kon epose'na to' utɨto' pe eke iwa ton pata pona'ne,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “To' kʉsenno'tʉu. To' a're'tɨtɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Ina piyau 5 kaisaron nɨken itekiino pʉreti mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ asa'ron kon nʉ'kwɨ moro' amʉ' esi,” ta'pʉ to' uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Pʉreti mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ moro' amʉ' ine'tɨ' uyena',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' pɨ', “Ereutapɨ'tɨ' wana' pona'ne,” ta'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨ tʉpo, 5 kaisaron itekiino pʉreti mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ moro' amʉ' anʉmʉ'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan uya tenu anʉmʉ'pʉ ka' winɨkʉi', mɨrɨpan uya pʉreti, moro' amʉ' i'kwɨ'pɨtʉi'ma tenki ta'pʉ Papa pɨ'. Mɨrɨ tʉpo, itʉrʉ'pʉ iya tʉpoitorʉ ton ena', mɨrɨpan ekamʉ'pʉ to' uya ka'pon amʉ' ena'.</li>
      <li>Tanporon kon nɨ ka'pon amʉ' enta'na'pʉ ta'wetapɨ'se, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipoitorʉ ton uya kiyari punu'pɨ e'nonkasa' ke 12 kaisaron pa'siki'ti arʉ'tɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau si 5,000 e'to' airɨ warawoti'si amʉ' tu'kanoro esi'pʉ. Uri'sami'si amʉ', mʉre amʉ' nɨrɨ esi'pʉ mɨrɨ yau to' pokon pe pʉra to' i'tusa'.</li>
      <li>Inke pʉra tʉpoitorʉ ton ekanwa'tɨto' pe kanau ya' ikuu'pʉ Sises uya, to' utɨto' pe tʉrawɨrɨ iratoi pona, anpisin enno'tane tʉuya.</li>
      <li>To' ennoko tʉpo, Sises utɨ'pʉ wʉ' pona tikin sarɨ ɨpʉremase'na Papa pɨ'. Pata uko'mansa' a'tai, tikin sarɨ rɨ mɨrɨ yau iyesi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>E'tane ipoitorʉ ton e'to' yau kanau esi'pʉ ɨnnɨ rɨ ite'pi piyapai. Eke pe rɨ sipa'sipa esi'pʉ kanau rɨ tʉwɨpɨ'se, apʉne pʉra a'setun uyee'pʉ ɨsɨ pe to' winɨkʉi'.</li>
      <li>Awanakʉi' kuru, pata emakʉ wapiya, Sises epa'ka'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton piya'. Parau ku'pɨri po itɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Parau ku'pɨri po iyepʉ ene tʉuya'nokon a'tai, ipan pe rɨ to' etʉipɨtʉ'pʉ. “A'kwarʉ'pʉ rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ!” tukai' to' ukɨ'pɨ'nʉmʉ'pʉ tetʉipɨtʉ kon pe.</li>
      <li>Sises uya inke pʉra rɨ to' pɨ' ta'pʉ, “Meruntɨ pe e'tɨ'! Urɨ rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ! Ketʉipɨ'tʉu!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Pi'ta uya ta'pʉ, “Uyepuru, ɨmɨrɨ pe iyesi yau, ukɨ'makɨ ɨpiya' utɨto' pe tuna pʉro'po!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya, “Ɨsi'kɨ si upiya'!” ta'pʉ ipɨ'. Mɨrɨ pɨ' Pi'ta ekanwaka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ tuna pʉro'po Sises piya'.</li>
      <li>E'tane mɨrɨ a'tai, Pi'ta uya eke rɨ sipa'sipa, a'setun nɨrɨ ene'pʉ. Mɨrɨ pɨ' iyenari'nʉmʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan e'sara'tɨ'pʉ e'sʉnkan pɨ' tuna ka', mɨrɨpan ukɨ'pɨ'nʉmʉ'pʉ, “Uyepuru, upika'tɨ'!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, inke pʉra rɨ Sises uya temiyatʉ ɨnka'pʉ a'sise'na, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ Pi'ta pɨ', “Aiko pe kuru anapurɨnʉ man! Ɨ'rɨ pe iyesi pɨ' ikasima'pʉ auya?” ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Kanau ya' to' ekanwa'tɨsa' a'tai rɨ, a'setun ereuta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Kamoro nin si kanau yawon kon uya apurɨpɨtʉ'pʉ mɨrɨ, “I'napairɨ rɨ Papa Mumu pe ɨwesi,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>To' ɨ'kwɨrɨ'sa' a'tai, to' e'te'ka'pʉ Kenesare' airɨ.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' mɨrɨ yau te'san uya Sises to'ka'nʉ'sa' a'tai, to' uya si tʉmaimu kon enno'pɨtʉ'pʉ a'ko pa'nan ka'pon amʉ' ena', mɨrɨpan kon uya si tanporo takuru'kena' nan nee'pʉ Sises piya'.</li>
