      <li>Ipan pe Sises pawana'tɨ'pʉ to' uya, “Tɨwɨ takuru'kena' nan ka'pon amʉ' ɨpon e'pi a'pɨ'pɨtʉi,” ta'pʉ to' uya, mɨrɨpan tanporo kon a'pɨ'pɨ'nin nʉ'san usepi'tɨpɨtʉ'pʉ.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Pari'si amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main pɨ' enupanin nan tonpa ton utɨ'pʉ Sises piya' Surusiran poi, mɨrɨpan kon uya,</li>
      <li>“Ɨ'rɨ pe iyesi pɨ' ɨpoitorʉ ton uya ina epuru ton eseru rʉ'pʉ i'kwɨtʉ? Temiyatʉ kon korʉka to' uya pʉra iyesi tenta'na kon rawɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ to' uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' maimu eikʉ'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ pe ken iyesi pɨ' Papa Maimu i'kwɨtʉ auya'nokon, ɨyeseru kon awɨrɨ ɨwesii'ma'nokon?</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra Papa uya, ‘Asanon kon inamatɨ',’ tasa', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ, ‘Ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉsanon pa'nʉ'nin wɨto' pe kuru rɨ iyesi,’ tasa'.</li>
      <li>E'tane ta auya'nokon, ka'pon uya rɨ tʉkʉipʉnʉ pɨ' mɨrɨ pe pʉra tʉsan pɨ', ‘Ɨpika'tɨto' pe ɨneporonʉ uwinɨ tʉsa' man Papa ena',’ ta yau,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨ ke tʉkʉipʉnʉ namato' iya pʉra iyesi. Mɨrɨ kasa si ipʉra Papa maimu kupʉ auya'nokon ɨyeseru kon pɨkɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon wakʉ pe te'ku'san! I'napai rɨ kuru rɨ Aisaya usaurokʉ'pʉ man ɨpɨ'nokon:</li>
      <li>“‘Pʉsamoro uya unama tʉnta kon ke rɨ, e'tane ɨnnɨ rɨ to' ewan esi upiyapai.</li>
      <li>To' ɨpʉrema upɨ', ɨ'rɨ epoton kon kasa rɨ, to' usenupato' esi ka'pon amʉ' uya rɨken to' enupa'pʉ ipɨ' to' e'to' yawɨrɨ pe,’ tawon,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Anpisin ton kɨ'ma'pʉ Sises uya tʉpiya', mɨrɨpan uya, “Umaimu etatɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ito'ka'nʉ'tɨ'.</li>
      <li>Ɨ'rɨ rɨ ka'pon mʉta ya' nʉtɨyai'ne' uya wakʉ pe pʉra ka'pon kupʉ pen; e'tane ka'pon mʉta yai nepa'kayai'ne' uya kuru wakʉ pe pʉra ka'pon kupʉ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises poitorʉ ton uyee'pʉ ipiya', mɨrɨpan kon uya, “Mi'tuyan pe' serɨ pe kuru masaurokʉine' uya Pari'si amʉ' ɨkɨnʉnpa'pʉ?” ta'pʉ to' uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>To' eikʉ'pʉ iya, “Tanporon nɨ ite' tʉnpɨmɨ'pʉ pen kuru'kato' oton ukʉipʉnʉ Epʉn po na'ne' uya.</li>
      <li>Tɨwɨ kamoro itepuru ton nesii, itenu pʉra to' esi mɨrɨ. Tenku'nan uya tenku'nan arɨ a'tai, asa'rɨ rɨ to' uta'mo'ka mɨrɨ akasa' ya',” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Pi'ta uya Sises ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ ta e'kwa pe serɨ panton esi?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya, “Ito'ka'nʉ'nin nan pe pʉra rɨ marɨ pe' ɨwesi kon mɨrɨ?” ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“Ene auya'nokon pʉra pe' iyesi ɨ'rɨ rɨ mʉta ya' newonyai'ne' utɨ ewan ya', mɨrɨpan epa'ka pun apai?</li>
      <li>E'tane ɨri main ka'pon mʉta yai nepa'kayai'ne' uyepʉ itewan yapai. Serɨ ton uya ka'pon kupʉ mɨrɨ ɨri pe.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra ka'pon ewan yapai ɨri pɨ' isenuminkato' uyepʉ; e'wɨn, tʉron kon no'pʉ a'kɨrɨ te'sen pe, tʉnmari'ma'pʉ pen nɨ a'kɨrɨ tekumasen pe, ama' e' pe rɨ, kasi ye' pe rɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨri pe tʉron kon pɨ' tʉusauro'sen pe.</li>
      <li>Serɨ ton uya ka'pon kupʉ mɨrɨ ɨri pe, temiyatʉ tʉkorʉkai' pʉra iyenta'na uya pen,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pata tʉnɨnse, Sises utɨ'pʉ Kiyarari ponsi'kɨ Taya mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Saitan itese' ton nono ya'ne.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yawon, uri'san, Esuwerʉ pe pʉra te'sen uyee'pʉ ɨkɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨtʉi'ma Sises piya', “Uyepuru, kin Tepi' pa rʉ'pʉ, upɨ' ɨsentu'ma'! Makoi a'kwarʉ yen pe umʉre esi ekota'man pɨ' man ipan pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane Sises uya imaimu eikʉ pʉra iyesi pɨ', ipoitorʉ ton uyee'pʉ ipiya' mɨrɨpan kon uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Enno'kɨ, apʉne pʉra ɨkɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨtʉi'ma uye'ma'pʉkapɨtʉ kon pɨ' man,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya nin si eikʉ'pʉ mɨrɨ, “Papa uya uyenno'sa' serɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' piya' rɨken, itano'masa' kon karimeru amʉ' kasa te'san piya',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Uri'san uyee'pʉ Sises piya', mɨrɨpan e'sekunka'pʉ ipiyau, mɨrɨpan uya, “Uyepuru, upika'tɨ'!” ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Eikʉ'pʉ iya, “Ipoken pʉra iyesi mʉre amʉ' yu pʉreti eno'ma to' ikʉn non pero amʉ' ena',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Ewai', Epuru, e'tane tesa' i'kiyari punu'pɨ uta'po'sa' tepʉrʉ poi pɨ' rɨ tʉuta're'tɨsan kamoro pero amʉ',” ta'pʉ uri'san uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan pɨ', “Eke pe kuru apurɨto' auya man! Tɨwɨ si ɨnekama'po'pʉ ne'kupʉi,” ta'pʉ Sises uya ipɨ', mɨrɨpan mʉre ena'pʉ wakʉ pe mɨrɨ a'tai rɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ tʉpo, Sises uya mɨrɨ pata nɨmɨ'pʉ; parau ku'pɨri Kiyarari e'pi poro itɨ'pʉ. Wʉ' pona iyenuku'pʉ, mɨrɨpan ereuta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau, anpisin pe ka'pon amʉ' uyee'pʉ ipiya', mɨrɨpan kon uya tʉusasan pen mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tenku'na' nan nee'pʉ ta'kɨrɨ'nokon; tʉron kon nee'pʉ to' uya ise'mepɨ'sa' kon mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉusauro'san pen, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉron kon nɨ e'ne' pe te'san, mɨrɨpan kon nonkapɨtʉ'pʉ to' uya Sises piya', mɨrɨpan uya tanporo rɨ to' epi'tɨpɨtʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' usewansiuka'pʉ, tʉusauro'san pen ka'pon amʉ' usaurokʉ tetase, tʉron kon ipu'tɨka'sa' kon usepi'tɨsa' tense, tʉusasan pen usarɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tenku'na' nan enasa' ennin pe tense. Mɨrɨ tense Papa apurɨpɨtʉ'pʉ to' uya Esuwerʉ amʉ' ɨpʉremato' ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya tʉpoitorʉ ton kɨ'ma'pʉ tʉpiya', mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ, “Pʉsamoro ka'pon amʉ' pɨ' usentu'mayai', apʉne pʉra osorʉwau wʉi upiyau'nokon to' uko'mansa', mɨrɨpan kon enta'nato' ipɨ' pʉra iyesi to' ɨnenno'pai pʉra esi iwan pe, yai to' utɨ esi tʉutɨ kon koro'tau,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pɨ' ipoitorʉ ton uya, “Nai yau rɨ eke pe pʉreti eporo ina uya pʉsamoro ka'pon amʉ' a're'tɨto' ike serɨ ɨnnon nɨ pata yau?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ kaisa rɨ pʉreti nai ɨpiyau'nokon?” tukai'. Mɨrɨ pɨ', “7 pe rɨken mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tu'kan kon pen aiko ton moro' amʉ',” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Anpisin auro'ka'pʉ iya to' ereutato' pe non pona.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya 7 kaisaron pʉreti mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tu'kan kon pen moro' amʉ' anʉmʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya tenki ta'pʉ tʉuya rʉ'pʉ pe i'kwɨ'pɨtʉ'pʉ. Tʉpoitorʉ ton ena' itʉpɨtʉ'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan kon uya ka'pon amʉ' ena' ekamʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Tanporo to' enta'na'pʉ ta'wetapɨ'se. Mɨrɨ tʉpo, ipʉ'kʉ rʉ'san e'nonkasa' amʉranʉkʉ'pʉ ipoitorʉ ton uya, 7 kaisaron pa'siki'ti tʉpe'ke'ne.</li>
      <li>Kamoro iyenta'nasa' kon tu'kanoro esi'pʉ 4,000 kaisa rɨ, uri'sami'si amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ mʉre amʉ' pokon ti'tui' pʉra.</li>
      <li>Anpisin ka'pon amʉ' ennoko tʉpo, Sises ekanwa'tɨ'pʉ kanau ya' tʉpoitorʉ ton pokon pe, mɨrɨpan kon utɨ'pʉ Makatan itese' pʉ'kʉ pona.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Pari'si amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Satu'si amʉ' uyee'pʉ Sises piya' i'tupɨ'se'na ti'tuto' ipɨkɨrɨ Epʉn poino ku'to' pe iya.</li>
      <li>Entakanoma'pʉ iya, “Ko'mamʉ pe kuru pata enasa' a'tai, ‘Tuna uyepʉ pen mɨrɨ, apʉne pʉra isuweyu pe ka' man,’ ta auya'nokon,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ awanakʉi', ‘Serɨ pe tuna pokon pe a'setun pe pata esi mɨrɨ, apʉne pʉra isuweyu pe ka' esi mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ewarupɨ pe,’ ta auya'nokon. Ka' winɨ rɨ ɨ'rɨ rɨ enpoikanin pe ɨwesi kon, e'tane si pata weyu i'tuto' ipɨ' enpoika auya'nokon pʉra iyesi.</li>
      <li>Ɨri ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ iyemari'masa' ekumankanin nan ka'pon amʉ' esi eke Papa tʉrawasooi i'tuto' tʉuya'nokon ipɨkɨrɨ kupʉ uya i'se. Ikupʉ uya pen, e'tane Isona pɨ' i'tuto' ipɨ' rʉ'pʉ na'ne' rɨken kupʉ uya,” ta'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨpan kon tʉnɨnse Sises utɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Parau ku'pɨri ratoi pona to' ɨ'kwɨrɨ'sa' a'tai, pʉreti arɨ to' uya pʉra ipoitorʉ ton upu'tɨkaa'pʉ esi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“Ti'tui' e'tɨ',” ta'pʉ Sises uya to' pɨ', “te'mainanpai' e'tɨ' Pari'si amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Satu'si amʉ' uya pʉrowa a'sarutanʉ'to' ike namai',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>To' usaurokʉ'pʉ tiwano' kon pe, “Apʉne pʉra pʉreti ne'sa' kasa pʉra isaurokʉ mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>To' usauro'to' i'tu tʉuya pɨ', Sises uya to' ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon aiko rʉ'kwɨ apurɨto' iya ton! Ɨ'rɨ pɨ' ausaurokʉ kon pʉreti pʉra ɨwesi kon pɨ'?</li>
      <li>Ito'ka'nʉkʉ auya'nokon pʉra rɨ marɨ pe' iyesi? Ɨyenu kon yau pe' ikupʉ auya'nokon pʉra iyesi 5 kaisaron pʉreti 5,000 kaisaron kon iwano' rʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ pa'siki'ti ton pe'tɨpɨtʉ'pʉ auya'nokon?</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe pʉra, 7 kaisaron pʉreti 4,000 kaisaron kon iwano', ɨ'rɨ kaisa rɨ pa'siki'ti mamʉranʉ'ta'tʉi?</li>
      <li>Nai pe ito'ka'nʉkʉ auya'nokon pʉra iyesi pʉreti pɨ' ayauro'ka uya 'nokon pen tukai'? E'tane Pari'si amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Satu'si amʉ' uya pʉreti a'sarutanʉ'to' namai' ɨye'mainanpa kon pa,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, to' uya ito'ka'nʉkʉ'pʉ pʉrowa a'sarutanʉ'nin itisu pen nɨ pɨ' kenʉ' Sises usaurokʉ'pʉ tukai', e'tane Pari'si amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Satu'si amʉ' uya enupan nɨto' pɨ' kenʉ' tukai'.</li>
      <li>Sises mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipoitorʉ ton uya Sisariya Piri'pai nono eposa' a'tai, tʉpoitorʉ ton ekama'po'pʉ iya, “Ɨnʉ' pe Ka'pon, Papa winon esi tukai' ka'pon amʉ' nʉsauro'an?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>To' uya entakanoma'pʉ, “Tʉron kon uya Isaan Pa'tes ta ɨpɨ'; tʉron kon uya kanan pu'kena' Iraisa ta; tʉron kon uya rɨ marɨ Iseremaya mɨrɨ pe pʉra tʉron kon pu'kena' amʉ' tonpa ton ta ɨpɨ',” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“E'tane si, ɨmɨrɨ'nokon, ɨnʉ' pe ken si esi mʉkayatʉu?” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Saiman Pi'ta uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Ɨmɨrɨ kʉrɨ rɨ Kʉrai, nurɨne te'sen Papa Mumu,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Pori' rɨ ɨmɨrɨ, Saiman, Isona mu, i'napairon serɨ uye'sa' ka'pon amʉ' winɨ pen e'tane tʉmɨrɨ pe Papa uya ekamasa' ɨpɨ'.</li>
      <li>Ekama uya serɨ, Pi'ta pe ɨyese' esi, Tɨ' ta e'kwa pe. Uso'sii nin si amɨ uya, ɨmɨrɨ tɨ' po, iyeri'sa' kon utɨto' ya' pata mʉra'taai enato' oton pen itentai.</li>
      <li>Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe yau kii ke ɨrepa uya; serɨ non po ɨ'rɨ rɨ auronsa' auya a'tai, Papa uya kanan auromʉ mɨrɨ Epʉn po; mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ serɨ non po ɨ'rɨ rɨ eukasa' auya iyesi a'tai, Papa uya kanan euka mɨrɨ Epʉn po,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya tʉpoitorʉ ton panama'pʉ ɨnʉ' rɨ pana'tɨ to' uya namai' Kʉrai pe iyesi, tukai'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ si'kɨrɨ, Sises uya tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ' ekama'pʉ Surusiran pona tʉutɨto' oton nɨ, mɨrɨ yau tu'kan yau rɨ itepuru ton uya, Papa ena' use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main pɨ' enupanin nan uya rɨ tʉkota'mato' oton, mɨrɨpan kon uya tʉwɨto' oton, mɨrɨpan te'mʉ'sa'kato' oton itosorʉwano wʉi a'tai tʉuko'manton pe ekama'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Pi'ta uya Sises arɨ'pʉ, ɨnnɨ kuru pʉra rɨ tʉron kon ipoitorʉ ton piyapai esereme'se'na. “Mɨrɨ kasa kasaurokʉi! Serɨ kʉse'ku'nin ɨpɨ', uyepuru!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises era'tɨ'pʉ Pi'ta winɨkʉi', mɨrɨpan uya, “Atamakɨ, Se'tan!” ta'pʉ. “Uye'ma tau uwa'kʉ'pɨ'nin tɨ' pe me'ai'; ka'pon usenuminkato' kasa ɨusenuminka, Papa usenuminkato' kasa pʉra,” ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ' ta'pʉ, “Ɨnʉ' rɨ upoitorʉ pe e'pai na'ne', tɨwɨ teseru nonkai mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tekota'mato' kurusu' anʉmʉi, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ upɨkɨrɨ tʉuye'to' pe.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra ɨnʉ' rɨ serɨ yau tʉuko'manto' ɨnnonkapai pʉra na'ne' uya epoto' oton pen nɨ, e'tane ɨnʉ' rɨ serɨ yau tʉuko'manto' nonkanin uya, urɨ wenai, epoto' oton.</li>
      <li>Ɨ'rɨ wakʉ esi ka'pon pɨ' serɨ po tanporon nɨ eposa' iya yau ta'kwarʉ nonkai'ma? Mɨrɨ pe pʉra, ɨ'rɨ tʉrʉ iya ta'kwarʉ entakano' pe?</li>
      <li>Apana'tɨ uya 'nokon serɨ; Ka'pon, Papa winon uye'to' oton tʉkʉipʉnʉ meruntɨrʉ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ itinserʉʉi ton pokon pe. Mɨrɨ a'tai, to' epe'pʉ ke ka'pon amʉ' e'mato' iya oton to' nʉkupʉ'pʉ pɨkɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>I'napairon kuru ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, serɨ yau iye'soto'pɨ'sa' na'ne' nan tonpa ton eri'to' oton pen Ka'pon, Papa winon uyepʉ esa' wannɨ pe te'to' yau ene tʉuya'nokon rawɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>6 kaisa rɨ wʉi tʉpo, Sises uya Pi'ta, Isens, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ iyakon Isaan pokon nɨken arɨ'pʉ ta'kɨrɨ wʉ' nakapu pona.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau, tʉron nɨ pe iyena'pʉ, itemʉ' e'wei'tɨ'pʉ wʉi enu kasa, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipon ena'pʉ aimu'ne, enkena' pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai kuru si mɨrɨ yau, Mosi' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Iraisa usenpoika'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya Sises auro'ka esi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Pi'ta uya ta'pʉ Sises pɨ', “Uyepuru! Wakʉ rɨ pan pe serɨ yau ina man! I'se ɨwesi yau, osorʉwau ɨiwʉ' kon amɨ uya mɨrɨ; tikin nɨ ɨiwano' pe, Mosi' iwano' pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Iraisa iwano' pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Pi'ta usaurokʉ koro'tau, enkena' kapuru' uya to' nɨpontɨ'pʉ. Main kapuru' yawon uya ta'pʉ, “Umu pʉse rɨ, Uni'nʉnkanʉ, ipɨ' pori' pe e'ai' ipan pe; imaimu etatɨ'!” tawon.</li>
      <li>Ipoitorʉ ton uya serɨ main etasa' a'tai, to' etʉipɨtʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uta'mo'ka'pʉ non pona itemʉ'.</li>
      <li>E'tane Sises uyee'pʉ to' a'pɨ'se'na, “E'mʉ'sa'katɨ',” ta'pʉ iya, “Ketʉipɨ'tʉu,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Tenu kon anʉnsa' to' uya a'tai, ɨnʉ' ene'pʉ to' uya pen nɨ, Sises rɨken ene'pʉ to' uya tikin sarɨ.</li>
      <li>Wʉ' ponsi'kɨ ɨu'tɨi'ma rɨ, Sises uya to' panama'pʉ, “Ɨnʉ' pɨ' rɨ ɨnene'pʉ kon kʉsekamatʉu, Ka'pon, Papa winon eri'sa' e'mʉ'sa'kasa' pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ipoitorʉ ton uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ pe ken si iyesi pɨ' Main pɨ' enupanin nan uya Iraisa kuru uye'to' oton wapiya ta?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' entakanoma'pʉ, “I'napairɨ rɨ Iraisa uye'to' oton ta to' uya, tanporon nɨ konekai' iyesi'pʉ ya'.</li>
      <li>E'tane nin si ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, Iraisa uye'kaa'pʉ, mɨrɨpan i'tu to' uya pʉra rɨ iyesi'pʉ, e'tane i'se te'to' kon awɨrɨ ɨri eseru kupʉ'pʉ to' uya ipɨ'. Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ Ka'pon, Papa winon ekota'mato' oton to' enau,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Iraisa pɨ' Sises usaurokʉ a'tai, Isaan Pa'tes pɨ' isaurokʉ tukai' ipoitorʉ ton uya i'tu'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Anpisin ton koro'ta' to' uye'sa' a'tai, ka'pon uyee'pʉ Sises piya', mɨrɨpan e'sekunka'pʉ ipiyau.</li>
      <li>Ta'pʉ iya Sises pɨ', “Uyepuru, umu pɨ' ɨsentu'makɨ. Yai itɨpɨtʉ, ipan pe iyekota'ma. Apo' ya', tuna ka' rɨ ita'mo'kapɨ'pɨtʉ.</li>
      <li>Ɨpoitorʉ ton piya' inee'pʉ uya, e'tane to' uya epi'tɨ poken pʉra iyesi'pʉ,” ta'pʉ iya Sises pɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Ɨri sɨ! Ɨri ton nɨ, apurɨnin nan pen nɨ serɨ a'taino kon! Ɨ'rɨ pʉ'kʉ pona useta'ka pʉra uko'mamʉ ɨpiyau'nokon? Ɨ'rɨ pʉ'kʉ pona aya'kɨrɨ'nokon esi? Ine'tɨ' upiya'!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya makoi a'kwarʉ eseremekʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan epa'ka'pʉ warawo' mʉre apai. Mɨrɨ a'tai rɨ, isepi'tɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises piya' ipoitorʉ ton uyee'pʉ ama'ai, mɨrɨpan kon uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ pe iyesi pɨ' ina uya enpa'ka pʉra iyesi?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' eikʉ'pʉ, “Apʉne pʉra aiko pe rʉ'kwɨ apurɨto' auya'nokon esi. I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; aiko rʉ'kwɨ mosta' ena'pɨ kasa apurɨto' auya'nokon esi yau, wʉ' pɨ', ‘Atamakɨ mairɨ!’ tasa' auya'nokon a'tai, itama rɨ. Ɨ'rɨ rɨ kupʉ auya'nokon a'tai, sa'man pe pʉra rɨ iyesi ɨpona'nokon.</li>
      <li>E'tane serɨ rupɨ epa'ka pʉra iyesi ɨpʉreman mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ useruman tʉuta're'tɨi' pʉra uya rɨken enpa'ka,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Tanporo to' amʉrasa' a'tai Kiyarari pona, Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Ka'pon, Papa winon eparankato' oton ka'pon amʉ' ena'.</li>
      <li>To' uya iwɨto' oton, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ itosorʉwano wʉi a'tai iye'mʉ'sa'kato' oton tʉuko'manto' ya',” ta'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan poitorʉ ton upokoita'pʉ ipan pe.</li>
      <li>Sises mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipoitorʉ ton uya Ka'paneyan pata eposa' a'tai, Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' ta' te'masen amʉranʉ'nin nan uyee'pʉ Pi'ta piya', mɨrɨpan kon uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨti'saai kon pe' Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' ta' tʉuse'masen?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Pi'ta uya to' eikʉ'pʉ, “Ewai', e'manin kʉrɨ rɨ,” ta'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨpan Pi'ta utɨ'pʉ ɨutɨ ta'. Sises usaurokʉ'pʉ wapiya kuru, mɨrɨpan uya Pi'ta ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ tukai' mɨsenuminkayan Saiman? Ɨnʉ' yan rupɨ winɨpai kin amʉ' uya pʉrata amʉranʉ'to' pe iyesi? Patawon amʉ' mɨrɨ pe pʉra ka'kʉran amʉ' winɨpai katɨ?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Pi'ta uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Ka'kʉran amʉ' winɨ,” ta'pʉ iya. “Patawon amʉ' use'mato' pe pʉra iyesi,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>“E'tane pʉsamoro ka'pon amʉ' ɨnɨkɨntanʉ'pai pʉra e'nɨ. Mɨrɨ pɨ', konoi' pɨ' enta parau ku'pɨri ka', mɨrɨpan wapiya kuru anma'pʉ moro' inta nau pʉrata pun eporo auya mɨrɨ, asakɨrɨ'ne wʉi e'tʉrawasoman nɨsa' epe'pʉ airon nɨ, mɨrɨpan ke e'mase'na mɨtɨi' uiwano' pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨiwano' pe nɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises poitorʉ ton uyee'pʉ ekama'poi', “Ɨnʉ' kuru si e'to' oton eke pe Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe yau?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya mʉre rʉ'kwɨ kɨ'ma'pʉ, mɨrɨpan soto'ka'pʉ iya to' koro'tau,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ, “I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; ɨusensima kon a'tai rɨken mʉre amʉ' pe tenai', ɨyepa'ka kon Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe ya'.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' rɨ esi mɨ pe te'ku'sen pe pʉra mʉre na'ne' kasa esi mɨrɨ eke pe Papa pona.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ, ɨnʉ' uya rɨ aiko rʉ'kwɨ mʉre pʉse rɨ warai ereutanʉkʉ a'tai, uyese' yau, uyereutanʉkʉ iya pe rɨ iyesi.</li>
      <li>“E'tane ɨnʉ' uya rɨ pʉsamoro uyapurɨnin nan aiko ton nʉ'kwɨ tonpa e'makoima emapu'tɨsa' yau, wakʉ iwa pe rɨ iyesi kʉrɨ rɨ ka'pon i'mʉ pɨ' eke a'nai' e'pato' ike tɨ' ewa'tɨsa' a'tai, mɨrɨpan eno'mato' pe parau ka' iyaputato' pe.</li>
      <li>Ɨsɨ sɨ, ka'pon amʉ' non pon kon, apʉne pʉra ka'pon amʉ' umakoita emapu'tɨ to' uya pɨ'. Mɨrɨ warai ton nɨ e'ku'to' pe iyesi e'tane, ɨsɨ yau kʉrɨ man iye'kupʉ emapu'tɨnin.</li>
      <li>Ɨyemiyatʉ mɨrɨ pe pʉra a'ta uya ɨye'makoima emapu'tɨ pe iyesi yau, a'tɨkɨ eno'ma pa; wakʉ iwa pe iyesi itemiyatʉ pʉra mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ i'ta pʉra esii'ma tɨwɨrɨ rɨ ɨuko'manto' ya' ɨyepa'ka a'tai, tanporo ɨpun eno'ma apo', tɨwɨro' rɨ ya' entai.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨyenu uya ɨye'makoima emapu'tɨ pe iyesi yau, imo'ka' eno'ma pa; wakʉ iwa pe iyesi tikin nɨ itenu esii'ma tɨwɨrɨ rɨ ɨuko'manto' ya' ɨyepa'ka a'tai, asa'rɨ itenu apo', iya'mu pʉn ya' ɨyeno'ma entai,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Miyarɨ rɨ Sises esi'pʉ usauro'nɨ pɨ', “Pʉsamoro aiko ton nʉ'kwɨ kʉsenpɨ'tʉu. Ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, to' inserʉʉi ton esi ukʉipʉnʉ emʉ' ennin nan pe tɨwɨrɨ rɨ Epʉn po.</li>
      <li>Serɨ ta uya ɨpɨ'nokon apʉne pʉra Ka'pon, Papa winon uye'sa' itano'masa' kon pika'tɨi'.</li>
      <li>Ɨ'rɨ tukai' mɨsenuminkayan? Ka'pon esi yau 100 kaisaron kon karimeru amʉ' esa' pe, mɨrɨpan kon tonpa utano'masa' yau, 99 pan kon pe' karimeru amʉ' nɨmɨ iya pen wʉ' po itano'masa' rʉ'pʉ warinpase'na tʉutɨto' pe?</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan eposa' tʉuya yau, i'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; pori' pe kuru iyesi tikin nan itano'masa' rʉ'pʉ karimeru pɨ' 99 pan kon itano'masa' kon pen karimeru amʉ' pɨ' pori' pe tesi entai.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ na'ne' kasa, ɨkʉipʉnʉ, Epʉn pon esi pʉsamoro aiko ton nʉ'kwɨ uyapurɨnin nan utano'ma i'se pʉra,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Miyarɨ rɨ Sises esi'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton auro'ka pɨ', mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ, “Ɨri pe ɨtonpa uya ɨku'sa' yau, ɨri inkupʉ'pʉ ekama ta ipɨ', asa'ken esii'ma. Amaimu etasa' iya yau, mɨrɨ nin si ɨtonpa pe ina'posa' auya.</li>
      <li>E'tane amaimu eta iya pʉra iyesi yau, tikin nɨ mɨrɨ pe pʉra asa'rɨ rɨ ka'pon amʉ' akɨ aya'kɨrɨ auro'kaka'se'na. Pʉsamoro asa'ron kon ka'pon amʉ' esi, ‘auro'ka pɨ' ɨpika'tɨnin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨri pe ɨwe'sa' esi i'napai rɨ tawon nan pe ipɨ'.’</li>
      <li>E'tane to' ɨnetapai pʉra kanan iyesi yau, ekamatɨ' so'si tawon kon pɨ', e'tane ɨnetapai pʉra kanan iyesi yau, inonkatɨ' Papa apurɨnin pen mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ pʉrata amʉranʉ'nin kasa iye'to' pe.</li>
      <li>“I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; serɨ non po ɨ'rɨ rɨ auronsa' auya'nokon a'tai, Epʉn po kanan Papa uya auromʉ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ serɨ non po ɨ'rɨ rɨ eukasa' auya'nokon a'tai, Papa uya kanan euka Epʉn po.</li>
      <li>“Se kanan ekama uya etatɨ': Asa'rɨ tekonekai' serɨ non po ɨ'rɨ rɨ ɨnekama'ponʉ kon pɨ', ukʉipʉnʉ, Epʉn pon uya rɨ amaimu kon eikʉ.</li>
      <li>Asa'ron kon, osorʉwawon kon nʉ'kwɨ rɨ amʉrasa' a'tai, uyese' yau, to' piyau rɨ esi,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Pi'ta uyee'pʉ Sises piya' ekama'pose'na, “Uyepuru, ɨ'rɨ kaisa rɨ ite'kwa utonpa e'makoimasa' upɨ' pɨ' usentu'ma? 7 kaisa rɨ ite'kwa pe'?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya Pi'ta eikʉ'pʉ, “7 kaisa rɨ ite'kwa pen e'tane, 70 kaisa rɨ 7 ite'kwa kuru,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya panton ekama'pʉ Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe eseru pɨ'. “Se na'ne' kasa Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe eseru esi: Kin esi'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' tʉpʉrataai ko'manʉ'pɨ'nin nan winɨ tʉpʉrataai amʉranʉkʉ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Iyepiya'tɨ koro'tau, ipoitorʉ uya eke kuru rɨ ipʉrataai ko'manʉ'pɨ'nin nʉ'pʉ nee'pʉ ipiya'.</li>
      <li>Ipʉrataai pʉra iyesi'pʉ tepuru e'mato' iya ike. Kin uya ta'pʉ, ‘Ikʉrʉpo'pomatɨ', ino'pʉ, imunkɨ amʉ' pokon pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ itimamin ton nɨ, mɨrɨpan epe'pʉ uya inko'manʉ'pɨtʉ'pʉ e'mato' pe,’ ta'pʉ kin uya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨpan poitorʉ uta'mo'ka'pʉ irau tese'mu po tenai', ‘Apʉne parɨ, ɨye'ma uya rɨ mɨrɨ tanporo,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ wenai, kin usentu'ma'pʉ ipɨ', iye'womasa' rʉ'pʉ rɨ nin si tʉkukai', ennoko'pʉ iya mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“E'tane pʉse rɨ utɨ'pʉ aiko rʉ'kwɨ rɨ nin tʉpʉrataai ko'manʉ'pɨ'nin piya', mɨrɨpan uya ta'sii' i'mʉ pɨ', i'mʉ kʉtʉtʉ'ka'pʉ. ‘Inke pʉra upʉrataai itʉkɨ!’ tai'ma.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan nʉ'kwɨ sa'ne uta'mo'ka'pʉ irau temʉ' po, ‘Apʉne sa'ne, ɨye'ma uya rɨ mɨrɨ,’ tai'ma.</li>
      <li>E'tane, ewai' ta iya pʉra iyesi'pʉ, a'si'pʉ iya pariki'si ta' tʉnko'manʉkʉ'pʉ e'ma iya pʉ'kʉ pona.</li>
      <li>Tʉron kon ipoitorʉ ton uya ensa' a'tai, inkupʉnʉ tense ipan pe to' upokoita'pʉ. Mɨrɨ a'tai, to' utɨ'pʉ tepuru kon pɨ' ekamase'na tanporo inkupʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan epuru uya ikɨ'ma'pʉ, ‘Ɨmɨrɨ ɨri rɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'. ‘Tɨwɨ rɨ si nesii, ta'pʉ uya ɨpɨ', apʉne pʉra ipan pe rɨ auta'kwarʉka pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Ɨsentu'mapai pʉra pe' ɨwesi mɨ ɨtonpa pɨ', usentu'mataine' kasa ɨpɨ'?’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Tʉusakorotai' itepuru uya itʉrʉ'pʉ pʉresiman amʉ' ena' to' uya a'sito' pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipanta'mapɨ'to' pe to' uya, tanporo tʉpʉrataai na'po iya pona rɨ.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ na'ne' kasa kuru Epʉn pon, ukʉipʉnʉ uya ɨmɨrɨ'nokon, ɨtonpa kon pɨ' ɨyewan kon yau tʉusentu'masan pen, ku'to' oton,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Serɨ ton ta tʉuya e'nonkasa' a'tai, Sises uya Kiyarari nɨmɨ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ Isutiya nono, Isotan tuna ratoi pona.</li>
      <li>Tu'kan kon anpisin utɨ'pʉ ipɨkɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan kon epi'tɨ'pʉ iya mɨrɨ yau.</li>
      <li>Pari'si amʉ' tonpa ton uyee'pʉ i'tupɨ'se'na. To' uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Main awɨrɨ rɨ e'nɨ pe rɨ pe' iyesi ka'pon uya tʉno'pʉ nonkato' ɨ'rɨ rɨ wenai?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Ene auya'nokon pʉra pe' ne'pɨ'an kareta yau?” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'. “Pena iyepiya'tɨ a'tai, ‘Ka'nin uya warawo' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ uri'san nɨrɨ koneka'pʉ.’</li>
      <li>Ta'pʉ iya, ‘Mɨrɨ wenai, warawo' uya tʉkʉipʉnʉ, tʉsan nɨrɨ nɨnto' pe iyesi, mɨrɨpan uta'sikʉ tʉno'pʉ ya', mɨrɨpan asa'ron kon ena tikin nɨ ipun.’</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa, asa'rɨ to' esi pen, e'tane tikin nɨ. Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', Papa na'sikʉ'san ɨsipona, mo'ka ka'pon uya kʉse'nin,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>To' uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ pe ken si iyesi pɨ' e'nonkan nɨto' karetaai tʉmenukai' ɨno'pʉ inonkakɨ tasa' Mosi' uya?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' eikʉ'pʉ, “Mosi' uya ɨno'pʉ kon amʉ' inonkatɨ' tasa', sa'man pe rɨ ɨyewan kon esi wenai, mɨrɨpan pen nin pena iyepiya'tɨ'pʉ si'kɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉno'pʉ nonkayai'ne', iyekumasa' pen nɨ e'tane, mɨrɨpan uya tʉron nɨ uri'san mari'ma, iyekuma pe iyesi mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ipoitorʉ ton uya ta'pʉ, “Mɨrɨ na'ne' kasa iyesi yau, tɨwɨ uri'san mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ warawo' emari'ma e'pai pʉra rɨ nin si man,” ta'pʉ to' uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' eikʉ'pʉ, “Tanporon kon pɨ' ta pen nɨ mɨrɨ, e'tane kamo rɨken anʉnnin nʉ'san nɨ.</li>
      <li>Tʉron kon entusa' temari'masen ye' pe pʉra rɨ, tʉron kon konekasa' ka'pon amʉ' uya temari'masen ye' pe pʉra rɨ, tʉron kon nɨrɨ e'ku'sa' tiwano' kon pe temari'masen ye' pe pʉra te'to' kon pe, Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe uriya'. Ɨnʉ' rɨ kʉrɨ tikin sarɨ e'paino e'to' pe rɨ iyesi,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, mʉre amʉ' nee'pʉ to' uya Sises piya' temiyatʉ tʉto' pe iya to' pona mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ iyɨpʉremato' pe to' pona, e'tane ipoitorʉ ton uya kamoro to' ne'nin nʉ'san eseremekʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Tɨwɨ mʉre amʉ' nʉyepʉi upiya'; to' kʉsereutanʉ'tʉu, apʉne pʉra pʉsamoro waraino kon kuru iwano' mɨrɨ Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Temiyatʉ tʉrʉ tʉpo to' pona, itɨ'pʉ mɨrɨ apai.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan a'tai, ka'pon uyee'pʉ Sises piya' ekama'pose'na, “Ti'sa, ɨ'rɨ wakʉ ku'to' uya pe iyesi tɨwɨrɨ rɨ uko'manto' epoto' pe uya?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Ɨ'rɨ pe iyesi pɨ' wakʉ pɨ' uyekama'po auya? Mɨrɨ yau iyesi mɨrɨ tikin nan nɨ wakʉ. Uko'man nɨto' ya' epa'kapai ɨwesi yau, Mosi' nʉmenuka'pʉ ton awɨrɨ e'kɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Nai ton?” tukai'. Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Ɨnʉ' rɨ kʉ'wɨnɨi, iyemari'masa' uri'san kʉsekumankai, ama' pe kesii, kasi pe ka'pon pɨ' kasaurokʉi,</li>
      <li>ɨkʉipʉnʉ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ asan nɨrɨ inamakɨ, ɨtonpa ti'nʉnkai' e'kɨ, mɨsi'nʉnkayai'ne' kasa,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Tanporo mɨrɨ ton ku'sa' uya man. Ɨ'rɨ kuru ken e'ku'sa' nai?” ta'pʉ moineri'pɨ uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Wakʉ pe e'pai ɨwesi yau, itɨkɨ ɨimamin kʉrʉpo'pomase'na, mɨrɨ tʉpo entu'manin nan mʉrepai' itepe'pʉ pʉrata ke. Mɨrɨ a'tai, Epʉn po imaminke' pe ɨwesi mɨrɨ. Mɨrɨ ku'sa' auya tʉpo, upɨkɨrɨ si ɨsi'kɨ,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Moineri'pɨ uya serɨ etasa' a'tai, pokoi pe rɨ esii'ma itɨ'pʉ, apʉne pʉra eke pe kuru itimamin esi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya ta'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ', “I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; sa'man pe kuru iyesi imaminke' epa'ka poken pʉra Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe ya'.</li>
      <li>Ekamakapʉ uya kanan; sa'man pe pʉra rɨ kiyamerʉ epa'ka akusa enu euta awɨrɨ, imaminke' epa'ka Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe ya' entai.”</li>
      <li>Ipoitorʉ ton uya serɨ etasa' a'tai, to' usewansiuka'pʉ ipan pe. To' uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨnʉ' kuru ken si epika'tɨ?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>To' enei'ma, Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Ka'pon pona sa'man pe iyesi, e'tane Papa pona tanporo sa'man pe pʉra iyesi,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Pi'ta uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Tanporon nɨ nɨnsa' ina uya man ɨpɨkɨrɨ tʉutɨto' kon pe. Ɨ'rɨ ken si e'to' oton ina iwano' pe?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; Papa uya emenna' pe tanporon nɨ koneka a'tai, Ka'pon, Papa winon ereuta a'tai a'kwa tapon po, ɨmɨrɨ'nokon upɨkɨrɨ iye'sa' kon nɨrɨ ereutato' oton 12 kaisaron apono' po 12 kaisaron kon Esuwerʉ pon kon eseru aimenka pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tanporon kon kamoro tiwʉ' kon, takon kon nɨ, tʉparusi kon nɨ, tʉkʉipʉnʉ kon nɨ, tʉsan kon nɨ, tʉmunkɨ kon nɨ, tʉmainarʉ kon nɨ nɨnnin nʉ'san urɨ wenai uya 100 kaisa rɨ'ne ite'kwa epoto' oton, mɨrɨpan kon uya tɨwɨrɨ rɨ uko'man nɨto' epoto' oton.</li>
      <li>E'tane tu'kan kon wapiyaro' kon nʉ'san e'to' oton ite'ma'pʉ pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tu'kan kon iu'matʉ pe iye'sa' kon e'to' oton wapiyaro' pe,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>“Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe esi non esa' kasa. Awanakʉi' itɨ'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' anʉnse'na tʉmainarʉ yau te'tʉrawasoma ton kon.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, to' pokon pe iyekoneka'pʉ to' e'mato' pe tʉuya tikin nɨ wʉi e'tʉrawasoman epe' pʉrata pun ke, mɨrɨpan kon ennoko'pʉ iya tʉmainarʉ ya'.</li>
      <li>“Awanakʉi', 9 a'kʉra' a'tai, itɨ'pʉ kʉrʉpo'po pɨ' e'nɨto' pata'se' ya'. Mɨrɨ yau, ka'pon amʉ' e'soto'pɨ'sa' ene'pʉ iya, ɨ'rɨ kupʉ pɨ' pʉra rɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, to' auro'ka'pʉ iya, ‘Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon nɨ marɨ, itɨtɨ' umainarʉ ya' e'tʉrawasomai'. Ɨye'ma uya 'nokon mɨrɨ iye'to' awɨrɨ rɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon utɨ'pʉ umɨ ya' e'tʉrawasomase'na. “Non esa' kanan utɨkaa'pʉ kʉrʉpo'po pɨ' e'nɨto' pata'se' ya' 12 a'kʉra' a'tai, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ 3 a'kʉra' kanan ka'pon amʉ' anʉnse'na to' e'tʉrawasomato' pe tʉmainarʉ yau.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ tʉpo, non esa' utɨ'pʉ kʉrʉpo'po pɨ' e'nɨto' pata'se' ya' ko'mamʉ pe 5 a'kʉra' a'tai. Mɨrɨ yau, ka'pon amʉ' e'soto'pɨ'sa' ene'pʉ iya. To' ekama'po'pʉ iya, ‘Ɨ'rɨ pe iyesi pɨ' ɨye'soto'pɨ'sa' kon te'tʉrawasomai' pʉra rɨ?’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“‘Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ ina anʉnsa' pʉra iyesi,’ ta'pʉ to' uya. “Ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', ‘Itɨtɨ' e'tʉrawasomatantɨ' umainarʉ ya',’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Ko'mamʉ pe, umɨ esa' uya ta'pʉ to' epuru pɨ', ‘Tʉrawaso amʉ' ikɨ'makɨ to' e'ma pa to' epe'pʉ ke,’ ta'pʉ iya. ‘Iu'matʉ pe anʉnsa' kon tʉrawaso pe me'mai' wapiya, iyepiya'tɨ pe anʉnsa' kon e'ma pa iu'matʉ pe,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Tʉrawaso amʉ' iye'sara'tɨsa' kon e'tʉrawasoman pɨ' 5 a'kʉra' a'tai uyee'pʉ tʉpʉrataai kon ipun si epose'na.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' wapiya iye'sara'tɨsa' kon tʉrawaso pe uyee'pʉ tepe'pʉ kon epose'na. To' e'kupʉ'pʉ eke pe parɨ pʉrata eporo tʉuya'nokon tukai', e'tane to' uya tikin nɨ rɨ marɨ pʉrata pun eporo'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Pʉrata eporo tʉuya'nokon a'tai, to' entarumʉ'pʉ non esa' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>‘Pʉsamoro ka'pon amʉ' iye'tʉrawasomasa' kon aka'ne' pe rɨ e'masa' auya'nokon, ina kaisarɨ rɨ marɨ, sa'man pe rɨ ina e'tʉrawasomasa' e'tane a'ne' rɨ wʉi yau,’ ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“E'tane tikin nan to' tonpa eikʉ'pʉ iya, ‘Utonpa, wakʉ pe rɨ iyesi serɨ pɨ' e'tʉrawasoma rɨ, tikin nan nɨ pʉrata pun pɨ', ta'pʉ auya.</li>
      <li>Ɨyepe'pʉ anʉnkɨ, itɨkɨ. E'kupʉ'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' e'mato' pe uya iu'matʉ pe unanʉmʉ'san kɨnye'mayai'ne' kasa rɨ.</li>
      <li>Upʉrataai ke pe' i'se e'to' rɨ kupʉ uya pen? Upɨ' rɨ katɨ ɨyɨkɨnta amʉre'mʉra esi pɨ'?’ ta'pʉ iya,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya tʉpantomʉ i'ma'ka'pʉ se kasa: “Mɨrɨ kasa iu'matʉ pe iye'sa' kon e'to' oton iyepiya'tɨ pe; kamoro iyepiya'tɨ pe iye'sa' kon e'to' oton iu'matʉ pe,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Sises utɨ koro'tau Surusiran pona, 12 kaisaron kon tʉpoitorʉ ton pantaka'pʉ iya mɨ airɨ. Ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ',</li>
      <li>“Surusiran pona utɨ'nokon serɨ, Ka'pon, Papa winon eparankato' oton use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main pɨ' enupanin nan ena', to' uya eno'mato' oton ima'tato' ya',</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan tʉto' oton to' uya Esuwerʉ amʉ' pen ena' to' uya isapemato' pe, ari'po'pɨ'to' pe, ipokapɨ'to' pe kurusu' pona. Itosorʉwano wʉi a'tai, iye'mʉ'sa'kato' oton uko'man nɨto' ya',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sepiti munkɨ amʉ' san uyee'pʉ Sises piya' tʉmunkɨ amʉ' pokon pe, mɨrɨpan e'sekunkasa' uya ekama'po'pʉ, wakʉ ku'to' pe iya tiwano' pe.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ i'se me'an?” ta'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨpan eikʉ'pʉ iya, “Pʉsamoro asa'ron kon umunkɨ amʉ' iku'kɨ to' ereutato' pe ɨyenwo'netʉ winɨ, tʉron nɨ akamisi winɨ esa' wannɨ pe ɨwe'to' yau,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“I'tu auya'nokon pʉra iyesi mekama'poyatʉi'ne',” ta'pʉ Sises uya to' pɨ'. “Ɨyekota'ma kon poken ken pe' nai ekota'mato' oton na'ne' kasa?” ta'pʉ Sises uya to' pɨ'. “Ewai',” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“I'napairɨ rɨ ɨyekota'ma kon urɨ ekota'mato' oton kasa rɨ, e'tane umeruntɨrʉ pʉra man iku'to' pe uya, ɨnʉ' ereutato' pe uyenwo'netʉ winɨ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ukamisi winɨ nɨrɨ. Serɨ pata ton esi mɨrɨ kamoro ukʉipʉnʉ uya to' pata pe ikonekasa' na'ne' iwano' pe iyesi,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>10 kaisaron kon uya asa'ron kon tʉtonpa kon maimu etasa' a'tai, to' usakorota'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Sises uya tanporo to' tʉkɨ'mai' to' amʉranʉkʉ'pʉ. Ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “I'tu auya'nokon Esuwerʉ amʉ' pen epuru ton esi to' esa' pe, mɨrɨpan eke ton uya tʉmeruntɨrʉ kon apurɨ to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa ɨwesi kon pen. E'tane ru'ku, ɨnʉ' rɨ esi yau eke pe enapai ɨ'koro'tau'nokon e'to' pe iyesi ɨpoitorʉ kon pe,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨnʉ' rɨ esi yau wapiyaro' e' pe e'pai, tɨwɨ nesii ɨpoitorʉ kon pe.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon, Papa winon uye'sa' na'ne' kasa rɨ tapiyo' pe e'nɨto' pe pen, e'tane iyapiyo' pe e'se, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉuko'manto' tʉse'na, tu'kan kon ka'pon amʉ' epe' pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipoitorʉ ton uya Iseri'ko nɨmɨ koro'tau, anpisin ka'pon amʉ' utɨ'pʉ ipɨkɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Asa'ron kon tenku'na' nan ka'pon amʉ' ereutasa' esi'pʉ asanta ka'ta po. Sises utɨ etasa' tʉuya'nokon a'tai, to' ukɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨtʉ'pʉ, “Ina epuru, Tepi' pa rʉ'pʉ, ina pɨ' ɨsentu'makɨ!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Tu'kan kon ka'pon amʉ' uya to' eseremekʉ'pʉ, “E'pana e'tɨ'!” ta'pʉ to' uya, e'tane rɨ eke pe parɨ to' ukɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨtʉ'pʉ, “Ina epuru, Tepi' pa rʉ'pʉ, ina pɨ' ɨsentu'makɨ!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' etasa' a'tai, te'takʉ'kai' to' kɨ'ma'pʉ iya. To' ekama'po'pʉ iya, “Ɨ'rɨ kupʉ uya i'se me'atʉu ɨiwano' kon pe?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>To' uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Ina epuru, ennin pe e'pai ina esi,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises usentu'ma'pʉ to' pɨ'. To' enu a'pɨtʉ'pʉ iya. Inke pʉra rɨ, ennin pe to' ena'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon e'sara'tɨ'pʉ ipɨkɨrɨ.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>To' uya Surusiran eporo koro'tau, Pe'pake ya' si to' uye'kaa'pʉ Are' Wʉpʉ pon. Sises uya asa'ron kon tʉpoitorʉ ton ennoko'pʉ,</li>
      <li>tai'ma to' pɨ', “Entantɨ' ɨyentau'nokon na'ne' eke iwa pata ya'. Mɨrɨ yau, inke pʉra rɨ isa'ka'si ewa'tɨsa' eporo auya'nokon mɨrɨ, imʉre ipiyau, mɨrɨpan kon teukai', to' mʉne'tʉi' upiya'.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ ɨ'rɨ rɨ ta yau ɨpɨ'nokon, ‘Itepuru esi to' i'se,’ mʉkatʉi'. Mɨrɨ a'tai nin si, to' uya to' ennoko mɨrɨ inke pʉra rɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ si pu'kena' amʉ' awɨrɨ isetasa' rʉ'pʉ uta'ku'tɨ:</li>
      <li>“Surusiran pon kon ka'pon amʉ' pɨ' ekamatɨ', ‘Kin, ɨiwano' kon uye'nɨ pɨ' man, mɨ pe te'ku'se rɨ iyepʉ pen, iyepʉ isa'ka'si mʉre po,’” tawon.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, ipoitorʉ ton utɨ'pʉ Sises uya ta'pʉ awɨrɨ rɨ iku'se'na.</li>
      <li>To' uya isa'ka'si mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ imʉre ne'kaa'pʉ. To' uya tʉpon kon tʉpɨtʉ'pʉ to' pona, mɨrɨpan po Sises ereuta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Anpisin ton kuru ka'pon amʉ' uya tʉpon kon ta'nʉkʉ'pʉ asanta tawɨrɨ Sises utɨto' pe ipo. Tʉron kon uya yʉi panta ton a'tɨpɨtʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan ta'nʉkʉ'pʉ to' uya asanta tawɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Anpisin ton ka'pon amʉ' irawɨrɨ tʉutɨsan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipɨkɨrɨ te'san ukɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨtʉ'pʉ, “Usana! Kin Tepi' pa rʉ'pʉ apurɨpɨtʉ serɨ!” “Pori' pe kʉrɨ esi mɨrɨ Itepuru ese' yau nʉye'ai'ne'!” “Usana ka' entawon yau!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Surusiran pona Sises epa'kasa' a'tai, ka'pon amʉ' eke pata pon kon e'tʉrʉnka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya, “Ɨnʉ' pʉse rɨ?” ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Anpisin ton uya to' maimu eikʉ'pʉ, “Sises pʉse rɨ, pu'kena' Nasare' winon, Kiyarari pon!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises ewomʉ'pʉ Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' pʉ'kʉ ta', mɨrɨ yau te'san ka'pon amʉ' usennan pɨ', kʉrʉpo'po pɨ' te'san enpa'ka'pʉ iya. Pʉrata ensimanin nan tepʉrʉʉi mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ wako'wa amʉ' kʉrʉpo'pomanin nan apon ton nɨ rawoipɨtʉ'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “Iye'menukasa', ‘Uiwʉ' e'to' oton ɨpʉreman iwʉ',’ tukai' e'tane ‘ama' amʉ' en pe rɨ’ mʉku'atʉi'!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Tenku'na' nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ise'mesa' kon uyee'pʉ ipiya' Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' ta', mɨrɨpan kon epi'tɨpɨtʉ'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton, Main pɨ' enupanin nan uya wakʉ kupʉ iya ensa' a'tai, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ mʉre amʉ' ukɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨtʉ, “Usana! Kin Tepi' pa rʉ'pʉ apurɨpɨtʉ serɨ!” tawon etasa' a'tai, Esuwerʉ amʉ' epuru ton usakorota'pʉ ipan pe mɨrɨ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>“To' maimu pe' metayan?” ta'pʉ to' uya Sises pɨ'. “Ewai',” ta'pʉ Sises uya. “Iye'menukasa' pe' ene auya'nokon pʉra nai: “‘Apurɨpɨ'nin pe eke ton nʉ'kwɨ mʉre amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ mana' pokon kon mʉre amʉ' ku'sa',’ tawon?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ tʉpo si, Sises uya to' nɨmɨ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ Pe'tani pona. Mɨrɨ yau, pata tʉrʉ'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Awanakʉi' kuru, iyenna'po koro'tau eke pata pona, iwan pe iyesi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Asanta piyau tʉna'sen ye', pi' tukai' tesa'sen ene tʉuya pɨ', itekare pɨ' itɨ'pʉ, e'tane ɨ'rɨ eporo'pʉ iya pen nɨ ipo, iyare ton nɨken, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Tɨwɨ si tepetasen pe pʉra e'kɨ!” ta'pʉ iya. Inke pʉra rɨ yʉi useketa'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Ipoitorʉ ton uya serɨ ensa' a'tai, to' usewansiuka'pʉ, to' uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Nai kasa si pi' e' useketa inke pʉra rɨ?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“I'napairon ekama uya serɨ ɨpɨ'nokon,” ta'pʉ Sises uya. “Apurɨto' auya'nokon esi a'tai, tʉkasimai' pʉra, mɨrɨ pi' e' pɨ' iku'sa' na'ne' rɨken kupʉ auya'nokon pen e'tane, ‘Ata'mo'kakɨ tuna ka',’ ta auya'nokon a'tai wʉ' pɨ', mɨrɨpan nɨ e'kupʉ.</li>
      <li>Apurɨ auya pe iyesi yau, eporo auya rɨ ɨnekama'po'pʉ ɨwɨpʉremato' yau,” ta'pʉ Sises uya tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises ewomʉ'pʉ Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' pʉ'kʉ ta'. Mɨrɨ yau, to' enupa pɨ' iyesi koro'tau, Papa ena' use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon amʉ' epuru ton pokon uyee'pʉ ipiya'. “Ɨ'rɨ meruntɨrʉ winɨ serɨ ton kupʉ auya? Ɨnʉ' uya serɨ meruntɨ ke ɨrepa'pʉ?” tukai' to' uya ekama'po'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Sises uya entakanoma'pʉ, “Tikin nan pɨ' rɨ marɨ ɨyekama'po uya 'nokon nɨ nɨrɨ mɨrɨ. Umaimu ei'sa' auya'nokon a'tai, ekama uya rɨ nɨrɨ mɨrɨ ɨpɨ'nokon, ɨnʉ' uya umeruntɨrʉ'tɨsa' serɨ ton ku'to' pe uya tukai'.</li>
      <li>Isaan uya pa'taisiman nɨto'—nai winɨ iye'sa'? Epʉn winɨ pe', mɨrɨ pe pʉra ka'pon amʉ' winɨ katɨ?” ta'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨpan kon usaurokʉ'pʉ tiwano' kon pe, “‘Epʉn winɨ’ ta pe iyesi yau, uyekama'po iya 'nokon, ‘Ɨ'rɨ pe ken iyesi pɨ' Isaan apurɨ auya'nokon pʉra iyesi'pʉ?’ tukai'.</li>
      <li>E'tane ‘ka'pon amʉ' winɨ’ ta yau, ka'pon amʉ' uya enari'pan, apʉne pʉra Isaan esi pu'kena' tukai' to' uya apurɨ'pʉ,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises nin si eikʉ'pʉ to' uya mɨrɨ, “Ina uya i'tu pʉra man,” ta'pʉ to' uya. Mɨrɨ a'tai, ta'pʉ iya, “Ekamasa' auya'nokon pʉra iyesi ke, ekama uya nɨrɨ pen nɨ serɨ mɨrɨ meruntɨrʉ winɨ serɨ ton kupʉ uya tukai',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ tukai' se pɨ' mɨsenuminkayatʉu? Ka'pon esi'pʉ asa'ron kon imunkɨ amʉ'. Wapiyaro' tʉmu piya' itɨ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya, ‘Mooi, e'tʉrawasomai' enta kʉre' itese' kiyari e'kwa na',’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“E'tane imu uya, ‘Kane,’ tukai' imaimu eikʉ'pʉ. Mɨrɨ ta tʉpo, teseru ensima'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ rɨ marɨ tase'na ikʉipʉnʉ utɨ'pʉ tʉmu, isakon pɨ'. ‘Mooi, serɨ pe e'tʉrawasomata kʉre' kiyari e'kwa na',’ ta'pʉ iya. ‘Ewai', utɨ rɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya, e'tane itɨ'pʉ pen.</li>
      <li>“Nai kʉrɨ rupɨ uya tʉkʉipʉnʉ e'to' i'se kupʉ'pʉ tukai', mi'tuyatʉu?” ta'pʉ iya. “Wapiyaro' uya kuru,” tukai' to' uya imaimu eikʉ'pʉ. Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya ta'pʉ, “I'napairon ekama uya serɨ ɨpɨ'nokon; pʉsamoro pʉrata amʉranʉ'nin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ uri'sami'si amʉ' ɨri pe iteseru iko'mansa' rʉ'san uya Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe epoto' oton arawɨrɨ'nokon.</li>
      <li>Wakʉ pe e'nɨ eseru enpoikase'na Isaan uyee'pʉ ɨpiya'nokon e'tane, apurɨ auya'nokon pʉra iyesi'pʉ, pʉrata amʉranʉ'nin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ uri'sami'si amʉ' ɨri pe iteseru iko'mansa' kon nʉ'pʉ uya rɨken apurɨ'pʉ. Mɨrɨ rɨ si ene tʉpo amakooi kon apai ɨyera'tɨ kon pʉra rɨ iyesi, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ apurɨ auya'nokon pʉra iyesi,” ta'pʉ Sises uya to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Tʉron nɨ kanan panton etatɨ': Moro non esa' ka'pon esi'pʉ kiyari ye' si'na' pe te'sen patama'pʉ iya. Iwoi iwa'kʉtʉi pe iwekupiri'tɨ'pʉ iya. Non aka'pʉ iya tʉmainarʉ yau ikasu'kato' yai, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipa'simato' ponsi'kɨ ka'tawon soto'pan ɨutɨ amɨ'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨpan uya umɨ pɨ' te'san ena' tʉmainarʉ tʉrʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ ɨnnon pata ya'.</li>
      <li>“Kiyari akʉ'pʉsa' weyu e'seposa' a'tai, tʉpoitorʉ ton ennoko'pʉ iya umɨ tʉrʉ'pʉ tʉuya itena' ton piya' tiwano' oton epose'na.</li>
      <li>Umɨ esanon uya ipoitorʉ ton a'si'pʉ. Tikin nan panta'ma'pʉ to' uya, tʉron nɨ wɨnɨ'pʉ to' uya, to' osorʉwano wɨpɨtʉ'pʉ to' uya tɨ' ke.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai tʉron kon nʉ'san tʉpoitorʉ ton ennoko'pʉ iya wapiyaro' ennoko'pʉ tʉuya entai, umɨ esanon uya mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ to' kupʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Tanporon kon u'matʉ pe, tʉmu nin si ennoko'pʉ iya to' piya'. ‘To' uya kuru umu nama mɨrɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya,</li>
      <li>e'tane imu ensa' tʉuya'nokon a'tai, ta'pʉ to' uya tʉtonpa kon pɨ', ‘Pʉse rɨ kuru pʉse rɨ kiyari pata'se' anʉnton. Apʉne, iwɨpai'nokon, inanʉmʉnʉ anʉnto' kon pe,’ ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan tanʉnse to' uya eno'ma'pʉ kiyari e'kwa yapai, mɨrɨpan wɨnɨ'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', kiyari e'kwa esa' uye'sa' a'tai, ɨ'rɨ ken si kupʉ iya itena' tʉnonka'san pɨ'?” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>“To' ma'tanʉkʉ'pʉ iya, kamoro ɨri ton, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉron kon nʉ'san ena' nin si kiyari e'kwa tʉrʉ iya tʉrepanin nan nin si ena', umɨ winɨ tʉneporonʉ kon yapai,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Iye'menukasa' itekare yau ennin nan pen pe' ɨmɨrɨ'nokon: “‘Tɨ', ɨutɨ amɨnin nan neno'ma'pʉ enasa' itekun airon tɨ' pe; serɨ ku'sa' Itepuru uya, mɨrɨpan esi wakʉ pe kuru uyenu kon yau,’ tawon?</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pɨ' Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe emo'kato' oton ɨpiyapai'nokon, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ wakʉ pe epetanʉ'nin nan ena' iye'tʉto' oton.</li>
      <li>Kʉrɨ serɨ tɨ' pona nʉta'mo'kayai'ne' utakiti'kwa mɨrɨ, e'tane kʉrɨ tɨ' nʉta'mo'kayai'ne' ipona uta'si'kɨrɨ mɨrɨ ipʉra rɨ nin,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Papa ena' use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pari'si amʉ' uya Sises pantomʉ to'ka'nʉ'sa' a'tai tʉpɨ'nokon isaurokʉ tukai',</li>
      <li>a'sito' ipɨkɨrɨ warinpa pɨ' to' esi'pʉ, e'tane anpisin ka'pon amʉ' pɨ' to' enari'nʉmʉ'pʉ, apʉne pʉra ka'pon amʉ' uya apurɨ pɨ' pu'kena' pe iyesi tukai'.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Sises uya kanan to' auro'kakaa'pʉ panton yai. Ta'pʉ iya:</li>
      <li>“Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe esi kin, tʉmu emari'ma i'kiyari konekanin nʉ'pʉ kasa,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan uya tʉpoitorʉ ton ennoko'pʉ tʉnkɨ'ma'san pana'tɨse'na to' uye'to' pe, e'tane ɨsi'pai pʉra to' esi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“Serɨ rɨken pe tʉpoitorʉ ton ennoko'pʉ iya, ‘Apʉne enkɨ! Tanporon nɨ ekonekaka'sa' man. Paka amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ eka'nʉ'sa' ton paka munkɨ amʉ' wɨka'sa' ekonekasa' man. Ɨsi'tɨ' si emari'man i'kiyari pɨ' enta'nai'!’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane tetai' pʉra to' utɨpɨtʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan tikin nan utɨ'pʉ tʉmainarʉ ya', tʉron nɨ tʉnkupʉnʉ rɨ ku'se'na.</li>
      <li>Tʉron kon uya ipoitorʉ ton a'si'pʉ, ipan pe rɨ to' kota'ma'pʉ to' uya, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ to' wɨnɨ'pʉ rɨ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Kin usakorota'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya tʉsoisaai amʉ' ennoko'pʉ kamoro to' wɨnin nʉ'san ma'tanʉ'se'na, to' pata'se' rɨ po'tɨpɨ'se'na.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ', ‘Emari'man i'kiyari rɨ e'nonkasa' man e'tane, kamoro unkɨ'ma'san uye'to' pe pʉra rɨ kenʉ' iyesi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Entantɨ' asanta ka'ta pona rɨ, ɨneporo'pʉ kon nɨ mʉkɨ'matʉi',’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pɨ' ipoitorʉ ton utɨ'pʉ asanta ka'ta pona ka'pon amʉ' tʉneporonʉ kon nɨ amʉranʉ'se'na, asa'rɨ rɨ, wakʉ ton, ɨri ton nɨ, mɨrɨpan emari'man nɨto' itau ɨutɨ epe'tɨ'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' ke.</li>
      <li>“E'tane kin uye'sa' a'tai to' ense'na, ene'pʉ iya moro ka'pon emari'man pon pe pʉra ipon.</li>
      <li>‘Utonpa, nai kasa ɨuye'sa' emari'man pon yau pʉra rɨ?’ tukai' ekama'po'pʉ iya. Isauro'to' pʉra iyesi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, kin uya ta'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ', ‘Auronpɨ'tɨ', itemiyatʉ pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ i'ta pɨ' eno'ma kon pa pʉroroi pona ewarupɨ ya'. Mɨrɨ yau ikaranto' pe, tʉyɨ kɨtɨtɨi'mato' pe iya,’ ta'pʉ kin uya.</li>
      <li>“Tu'kan kon nɨ kɨ'ma e'tane, tu'ke pʉra to' anʉmʉ,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pɨ' Pari'si amʉ' utɨ'pʉ nai kasa ipoken pʉra isauro'to' pe ikupʉ'nokon ka'se'na.</li>
      <li>To' uya tʉpoitorʉ kon ennoko'pʉ Sises piya'. Kin pe te'sen, Era' pɨkɨron kon pokon pe rɨ, mɨrɨpan kon uya ta'pʉ Sises pɨ', “Ti'sa, ina i'tupɨ' man i'napairon ye' pe ɨwesi tukai', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Papa eseru pɨ' enupan auya i'napairon awɨrɨ. Ka'pon amʉ' rɨ nensimanʉ pe pʉra ɨyeseru esi, apʉne pʉra ɨnʉ' pe rɨ to' esi pɨ' te'namasen pe pʉra ɨwesi.</li>
      <li>Ina pɨ' ekamakɨ; ɨ'rɨ ta auya se pɨ'; ipoken pe' iyesi Sisa ena' pʉrata tʉtʉsen e'ma a'tai, kane katɨ?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>E'tane, ɨri kupʉ pɨ' to' e'ku'to' i'tu tʉuya ke Sises uya ta'pʉ. “Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon wakʉ pe te'ku'san, ɨ'rɨ pe iyesi pɨ' usa'mapai ɨwesi kon?</li>
      <li>Apʉne, use'man nɨto' ike enpoikatɨ' uyena',” ta'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨpan kon uya pata esa' apon pʉrata pun nee'pʉ itena'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya to' ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨnʉ' nai ipɨ', ɨnʉ' ese' nai ipɨ'?” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Sisa,” tukai' to' uya imaimu eikʉ'pʉ. Mɨrɨ a'tai, ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “Sisa iwano' itʉtɨ' itena' rɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Papa iwano' rɨ itʉtɨ' Papa ena' rɨ,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ tawon eta tʉuya'nokon a'tai, to' usewansiuka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon utɨ'pʉ ipiyapai.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ wʉi yau rɨ, Satu'si amʉ', eri'nɨ tʉpo e'mʉ'sa'kan pʉra iyesi tawon nan uyee'pʉ Sises piya' ekama'pose'na.</li>
      <li>Ta'pʉ to' uya, “Ti'sa, Mosi' uya tasa' upɨ'nokon, tʉumu'tai' pʉra ka'pon eri'sa' yau, iyakon nʉ'pʉ uya ino'pʉ rʉ'pʉ mari'mato' pe iyesi imu'tanʉ'to' pe tʉuya itiwano' pe.</li>
      <li>Moro 7 kaisaron kon ɨsirunan esi'pʉ ina koro'tau. Wapiyaro' emari'ma'pʉ, mɨrɨpan erikʉ'pʉ, tʉmunkɨ ke pʉra tʉno'pʉ tʉnonkai', mɨrɨpan no'pʉ rʉ'pʉ e'nonka'pʉ iyakon ena'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ, iyakon nʉ'pʉ erikʉ'pʉ imʉre pʉra rɨ. To' osorʉwano esi'pʉ mɨrɨ kasa rɨ. Tanporo 7 pe te'to' kon kaisa rɨ.</li>
      <li>Kamoro eri'pɨtʉ'pʉ pata'pʉ pe, to' no'pʉ rʉ'pʉ erikʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Eri'nɨ tʉpo, e'mʉ'sa'kan a'tai, ɨnʉ' kuru no'pʉ pe ken si iyesi, 7 kaisaron kon koro'tapai, apʉne pʉra 7 kaisaron kon uya imari'masa' pɨ'?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' maimu eikʉ'pʉ, “Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon esi ipoken pʉra, apʉne pʉra iye'menukasa' itekare mɨrɨ pe pʉra Papa meruntɨrʉ i'tu auya'nokon pʉra iyesi pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Eri'nɨ tʉpo e'mʉ'sa'kan a'tai, ka'pon amʉ' emari'mato' oton pen nɨ, mɨrɨ pe pʉra to' e'tʉrʉ pen nɨ emari'man nɨto' yau; inserʉ amʉ', Epʉn pon kon kasa rɨ to' e'to' oton.</li>
      <li>E'tane eri'nɨ tʉpo e'mʉ'sa'kan nɨto' ensa' auya'nokon pʉra pe' nai Papa uya ayauro'ka'pʉ kon ipɨ'?</li>
      <li>‘Papa urɨ, Epʉra'an, Aisi', Seko' e'to' itese' ipɨ',’ tawon. Papa, iyeri'sa' kon e'to' itese' pɨ' pen e'tane nurɨnan kon,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ tawon eta tʉuya'nokon a'tai, to' usewansiuka'pʉ tenupato' iya 'nokon pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya Satu'si amʉ' maimu'kasa' tense, Pari'si amʉ' amʉra'pʉ.</li>
      <li>To' tonpa, ipan pe Main i'tunin uya Sises ekama'po'pʉ i'tupɨtʉ pe,</li>
      <li>“Ti'sa, nai kuru esi eke pe iyawɨrɨ e'nɨto' pe Main, Mosi' winon yau?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “‘Papa i'nʉnkakɨ tanporo ɨyewan pokon pe, aya'kwarʉ pokon pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨusenuminkato' pokon pe.’</li>
      <li>Serɨ serɨ wapiyaro', eke kuru iyawɨrɨ e'nɨto'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipɨkɨron esi iwaraino rɨ marɨ: ‘Ɨtonpa i'nʉnkakɨ mɨsi'nʉnkayai'ne' kasa,’ tawon.</li>
      <li>Serɨ si asa'ron iyawɨrɨ e'nɨto' po, tanporo Main mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pu'kena' amʉ' esi mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Pari'si amʉ' amʉrasa' koro'tau, Sises uya to' ekama'popɨtʉ'pʉ,</li>
      <li>“Ɨnʉ' pe rɨ Kʉrai esi tukai' mi'tuyatʉu? Ɨnʉ' pa rʉ'pʉ pe iyesi?” ta'pʉ iya. “Tepi' pa rʉ'pʉ tukai',” to' uya eikʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “Ɨ'rɨ pe ken iyesi pɨ' Tepi' usaurokʉ Iya'kwarʉ yau uya esakʉ, ‘Uyepuru,’ tukai'? Apʉne pʉra ta iya,</li>
      <li>“‘Itepuru uya ta'pʉ uyepuru pɨ': “Uyenwo'netʉ winɨ ereutakɨ, ɨyeyaton non tʉrʉ uya pʉkʉ pona a'ta o'koi',”’ tasa'.</li>
      <li>Tepi' uya, ‘Uyepuru,’ tukai' esakʉ pe iyesi yau, nai kasa nɨrɨ ipa rʉ'pʉ pe nesii'no?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ imaimu entakanoma poken pʉra iyesi'pʉ, mɨrɨ wʉi awonsi'kɨ ɨnʉ' rɨ esi'pʉ mɨrɨ enta' ɨnekama'popɨ'pai pʉra.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya ta'pʉ iyamʉrasa' kon pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ':</li>
      <li>“Main pɨ' enupanin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pari'si amʉ' esi mɨrɨ Mosi' pata'pʉ akan pe.</li>
      <li>To' maimu awɨrɨ me'tʉi', ɨ'rɨ rɨ tasa' to' uya na'ne' ɨpɨ'nokon mʉku'tʉi', e'tane to' nʉkupʉnʉ kʉ'ku'tʉu, apʉne pʉra tʉusauro'to' kon ku'nin nan pen kamoro.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' ekama'po to' uya itekare ku'to' pe to' uya sa'man pe rɨ te'sen, e'tane ɨ'rɨ rɨ kupʉ to' uya pʉra rɨ iyesi tʉnauro'kapʉ kon pika'tɨnin pe.</li>
      <li>“Tanporon nɨ to' nʉkupʉ'pʉ pe na'ne' esi mɨrɨ ka'pon amʉ' uya tento' kon ipɨ' pe: tʉwɨpʉremato' kon yen konepɨtʉ to' uya eke ton pe ika'ta, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉpon kon sousowʉ pe te'sen kanan ɨnkapɨtʉ to' uya kusan ton pe.</li>
      <li>Eke ton ereutato' pata'se' yau kuru ereutapaino kon enta'nan a'tai'ne mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' usenupato' iwʉ' tau.</li>
      <li>Anpisin ka'pon amʉ' kʉrʉpo'po pata'se' iyawon kon uya, ‘Miyarɨ,’ ta i'se te'san tʉnama kon pe, ka'pon amʉ' uya, ‘Rapai,’ ta i'se kuru to' esi tʉpɨ'nokon.</li>
      <li>“E'tane ɨusesa'to' kon pʉra iyesi ‘Ti'sa’ tukai', apʉne pʉra tikin nan nɨ esi ɨyepuru kon pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨsitonpa pe rɨ nin ɨwesi kon.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan ɨnʉ' rɨ kʉsesa'tʉu, ‘Ukʉipʉnʉ,’ tukai' serɨ non po, apʉne pʉra tikin nan nɨ ɨkʉipʉnʉ kon esi, Epʉn pon.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' rɨ esa'to' pʉra rɨ iyesi, ‘Ti'sa,’ tukai', apʉne pʉra tikin nan nɨ kʉrɨ rɨ Ti'sa; Kʉrai.</li>
      <li>Eke pe na'ne' ɨ'koro'tau'nokon esi mɨrɨ ayapiyo' kon pe rɨ.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' rɨ eke pe te'ku'sen ena mɨrɨ se pe rɨ; mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ se pe rɨ te'ku'sen ena mɨrɨ eke pe,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsɨ sɨ, Main pɨ' enupanin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pari'si amʉ', ɨmɨrɨ'nokon wakʉ pe te'ku'san! Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ ya' rɨ ɨtɨpaino kon wa'kʉ'sa' auya'nokon man. Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon pe rɨ epa'kapai pʉra ɨwesi kon, mɨrɨ pe pʉra epa'kapai na'ne' nan epa'kato' pe ikupʉ auya'nokon pʉra iyesi.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsɨ sɨ, Main pɨ' enupanin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pari'si amʉ', ɨmɨrɨ'nokon wakʉ pe te'ku'san! Itaan'pʉ iyeri'sa' kon nʉ'san iwʉ' ma'tanʉkʉ auya'nokon, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨwɨpʉrema kon kusan pe, ‘Wakʉ ton,’ tato' pe ɨpɨ'nokon. Mɨrɨ wenai, ipan pe rɨ Papa uya ɨkota'mato' oton kon.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsɨ sɨ, Main pɨ' enupanin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pari'si amʉ', ɨmɨrɨ'nokon wakʉ pe te'ku'san! Siya rɨ tʉutɨsan ɨmɨrɨ'nokon non poro, parau kau rɨ, tikin nan nɨ konekai'. Ɨtonpa pe ikonekasa' auya'nokon a'tai, ikupʉ auya'nokon asa' ite'kwa iye'to' airɨ akasa'nokon, iyeri'sa' kon utɨto' ya' ekota'mai' itɨto' pe.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsɨ sɨ, tenku'ne esii'ma ka'pon esanon! Ta auya'nokon, ‘Ɨnʉ' rɨ usauro'sa' yau, iku'to' pe uya tukai' Papa ena' use'man nɨto', ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' tesa'pɨ'se uya iku'to' kuru pe pʉra rɨ iyesi, e'tane ɨnʉ' rɨ usauro'sa' pe iyesi yau, iku'to' pe tʉuya tukai', korʉ tesa'pɨ'se Papa ena' use'man nɨto', ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' tawon uya kuru nin si iku'to' pe iyesi,’ ta auya'nokon.</li>
      <li>Tenu a'kwarʉkena' nan pen! Nai esi eke pe kuru: korʉ, Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' katɨ---korʉ ku'nin wakʉ pe?</li>
      <li>Ta auya'nokon kanan, ‘Ɨnʉ' rɨ usauro'sa' yau, iku'to' pe uya tukai' Papa ena' use'man nɨto' apon tesa'pɨ'se uya iku'to' pe kuru pʉra rɨ iyesi, e'tane ɨnʉ' rɨ usauro'sa' pe iyesi yau, iku'to' pe tʉuya tukai' tʉntʉrʉnʉ Papa ena' use'man nɨto' apon tesa'pɨ'se ikupʉ uya tukai', tʉusaurokʉ'pʉ ku'to' iya pe kuru rɨ iyesi,’ ta auya'nokon.</li>
      <li>Itenu pʉnon! Nai esi eke pe kuru: tʉtʉsen, use'man nɨto' apon katɨ---tʉtʉsen ku'nin wakʉ pe?</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ wenai, tʉusauro'sa' rʉ'pʉ kupʉ iya pe iyesi Papa ena' use'man nɨto' apon tesa'pɨ'se, mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ iyesi ta tʉuya pe iyesi yau, tʉusauro'sa' iku'to' pe uya ta tʉuya a'tai, tanporon nɨ Papa ena' use'man nɨto' apon tesa'pɨ'se.</li>
      <li>Kʉrɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' tesa'pɨ'se ikupʉ uya tukai', Papa, itau na'ne' ese' yau isauro'sa' na'ne', Papa uya wakʉ nonkato' tʉmunkɨ amʉ' pona iwʉ', mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ iyesi tʉusauro'sa' kupʉ iya pe iyesi yau, Papa ese' tesa'pɨ'se Papa ena' use'man nɨto', ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' tawon.</li>
      <li>Kʉrɨ Epʉn tesa'pɨ'se iku'to' pe uya tukai' tʉusauro'sen, usaurokʉ mɨrɨ Papa apon tesa'pɨ'se mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipo te'sen.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsɨ sɨ, Main pɨ' enupanin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pari'si amʉ', ɨmɨrɨ'nokon wakʉ pe te'ku'san! 1 10 e'to' airɨ kiyari kɨ'nʉnpanin—min, tirʉ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kumin tato' tʉnin. E'tane eke ton pe kuru te'sen Main yau—ɨsi'kaisa rɨ ka'pon ku'to', ɨsentu'ke' pe e'nɨto' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ usauro'nɨ'pʉ awɨrɨ e'nɨto'. Emen iwa pe na'ne' kupʉ pɨ' ɨwesi'pʉ kon nesii'no, iwapiyaro' teno'mai' pʉra.</li>
      <li>Tenku'ne esii'ma ka'pon esanon! Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon esi weruwe eisikai'ma ɨuku kon apai, ɨikʉn kon eke rɨ kiyamerʉ tato' enko'mai'ma.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsɨ sɨ, Main pɨ' enupanin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pari'si amʉ', ɨmɨrɨ'nokon wakʉ pe te'ku'san! Iya'poi pɨ' a'sawʉ kon, aparapii kon korʉka auya'nokon, e'tane eke pe rɨ iyau mentai e'nɨto' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ amʉre' pe e'nɨto' esi.</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon tenku'na' nan, Pari'si amʉ'! Wapiya kuru iyau a'sawʉ kon, aparapii kon ikorʉkaka'tɨ'. Mɨrɨ a'tai, iya'poi esi mɨrɨ wakʉ pe rɨ nɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsɨ sɨ, Main pɨ' enupanin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pari'si amʉ', ɨmɨrɨ'nokon wakʉ pe te'ku'san! Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon esi aimu'ne ikorʉkasa' tɨ' akasa' uruwai' pe kasa, wakʉ pe tʉusensen kɨpo'po, e'tane eke pe rɨ iyeri'pɨ'sa' kon ɨ'pʉ rʉ'san esi iyau, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨri ton nɨ esi.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ, ɨusene kon ipokena' pe tʉron kon pona, e'tane ɨyewan kon yau makoi pe ɨwesi kon wakʉ pe ɨye'kupʉ kon.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsɨ sɨ, Main pɨ' enupanin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pari'si amʉ', ɨmɨrɨ'nokon wakʉ pe te'ku'san! Pu'kena' amʉ' uruwasii oton tɨ' akapɨtʉ'pʉ auya'nokon mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipokena' ton uruwasii ipʉrʉ'tɨpɨtʉ auya'nokon.</li>
      <li>‘Pena ina tamokori ton a'tai, ina uko'mamʉ pe iyesi yau, to' pika'tɨ'pʉ nesii'no pen nɨ pu'kena' amʉ' tʉ'ka pɨ',’ ta auya'nokon.</li>
      <li>E'tane ɨiwano' kon pe ɨusekama kon kamoro pu'kena' amʉ' tʉ'kanin nʉ'san payan nʉ'san pe.</li>
      <li>Iku'tɨ' rɨ si atamokori kon amʉ' nʉsara'tɨ'pʉ, Papa uya ɨkota'mato' kon pe iwenai!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya kanan ta'pʉ, “Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon, ɨkʉi amʉ' kasa te'san, ayainʉmʉ kon pe' Papa uya ɨkota'mato' kon ta'mu kenan pen nɨ ekota'man nɨto' yapai?</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', ɨ'koro'ta'nokon pu'kena' amʉ', ta'kwarʉkena' nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ti'sa amʉ' ennoko uya to' tonpa ton tʉ'kato' auya'nokon oton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉron kon pokapɨ'to' auya'nokon kurusu' pona mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉron kon nɨ ari'po'pɨ'to' auya'nokon oton ɨusenupato' kon iwʉ' tau, mɨrɨpan kon nɨ e'ma'pʉkapɨ'to' auya'nokon oton tʉron nɨ pata yapai'ne tʉron nɨ pata ya'ne.</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon pona serɨ e'moronkato' oton ipokena' ton mʉnʉ enno'sa' auya'nokon wenai serɨ non po, ipokena' Eperʉ mʉnʉ awonsi'kɨ, Sakaraya, Pere'kaya mu pe te'sen mʉnʉ pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ, ɨnwɨnɨ'pʉ kon ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ use'man nɨto' apon ka'sanau.</li>
      <li>I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; tanporo serɨ e'moronka mɨrɨ serɨ a'taino kon pona,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>“Aiko sɨ! Surusiran pon kon, Surusiran pon kon! Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon pu'kena' amʉ' tʉ'kanin nʉ'san, tɨ' ke ɨpiya'nokon enno'sa' kon wɨpɨ'nin nʉ'san. Inke rɨ ɨmunkɨ amʉ' amʉranʉkʉ i'se esi'pʉ, kɨrɨtɨkɨ uya tʉmunkɨ amʉ' amʉranʉkʉ kasa tapiri o'koi', e'tane mɨrɨ kupʉ uya i'se pʉra ɨwesi'pʉ kon.</li>
      <li>Entɨ' si! Ɨiwʉ' kon e'nonkasa' ɨyena'nokon iyarʉ pʉra!</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; uyento' auya'nokon oton pen nɨ kanan serɨ enta', ‘Pori' pe rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ nʉye'ai'ne' Itepuru ese' yau esi,’ ta auya'nokon pʉ'kʉ pona,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Sises utɨ esi'pʉ Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' tawonsi'kɨ, ipoitorʉ ton iya'kɨron kon uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Apʉne enkɨ, wakʉ pe rɨ amɨsa' ɨutɨ,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Tanporo rɨ pe' serɨ ton menyatʉu? I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, tikin nɨ rɨ tɨ' e'nonkato' oton pen nɨ mɨrɨ ɨsipʉro'po; tanporon nɨ uta'po'to' oton,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises ereutasa' koro'tau Are' Wʉpʉ po, ipoitorʉ ton uyee'pʉ ipiya' ama'ai ekama'pose'na, “Ina pɨ' ekama' ɨ'rɨ a'tai serɨ e'ku'to' oton, ɨ'rɨ e'to' oton ɨuyepʉ ento' ipɨ' pe, pata weyu u'matʉ ekamanin pe?” tukai'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Tenu ke e'tɨ' ɨnʉ' uya rɨ ɨyenku'tɨ kon namai'.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra tu'kan kon nɨ uye'to' oton uyese' yau, ‘Kʉrai urɨ,’ tukai', mɨrɨpan kon uya tu'kan kon nɨ enku'tɨto' oton.</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon uya etato' oton tʉusewa'nomasan, usewa'noman man tawon nɨ, e'tane serɨ ton pɨ' rɨ ketʉipɨ'tʉu. Serɨ warai'nan nɨ e'ku'to' pe iyesi, e'tane apʉne rɨ pata weyu u'ma'to' uye'tane rɨ iyesi.</li>
      <li>Tʉpataron kon uya tʉpataron kon nɨ nɨrɨ ewa'nomato' oton, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ esa' wannɨ pe te'san esa' wannɨ pe te'san nɨ nɨrɨ ewa'nomato' oton. Iwankan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉrʉ'pʉnʉ e'to' oton pata ton yau'ne.</li>
      <li>Tanporo serɨ ton esi mɨrɨ e'tinkan entun nɨto' pe kasa.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ a'tai ɨtʉto' oton kon ɨkota'mato' kon pe mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ uma'tan nɨto' ya'. Tanporo tʉpataron kon uya ɨyewaruma'tɨto' oton kon urɨ uriya'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai si, tu'kan kon nɨ ka'pon amʉ' uyapurɨ pɨ' te'san e'nonkato' oton, tu'kan kon nɨ ka'pon amʉ' uya tʉtonpa kon eparankato' oton, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ to' ewaruma'tɨto' oton.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau si, tu'ke rɨ enku'tɨnin nan pu'kena' amʉ' usenpoikato' oton, mɨrɨpan kon uya tu'kan kon nɨ enku'tɨto' oton.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra eke pe rɨ ɨri epamʉ uriya', tu'kan kon nɨ usi'nʉnkato' e'nɨ'panto' oton.</li>
      <li>E'tane kʉrɨ rɨ pana' pe te'sen tʉnapurɨnʉ yau iu'matʉ pʉ'kʉ pona, kʉrɨ rɨ si epika'tɨto' oton.</li>
      <li>Serɨ Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe ekareei usekamato' oton pata emʉ' kaisa rɨ, ennin nʉ'san uya ekama tanporo ka'pon amʉ' pɨ', mɨrɨ a'tai kuru nin si, iu'matʉ e'seporo mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“‘Ɨri Kuru Nuirapanin Uma'tan Emapu'tɨnin’ e'soto'kasa' wakʉ pata yau ene auya'nokon a'tai si, pu'kena' Taniyerʉ nekama'pʉ rʉ'pʉ — tɨwɨ serɨ ennin nʉto'ka'nʉkʉi —</li>
      <li>tɨwɨ si kamoro Isutiya pon kon nainʉmʉi wʉ' ton pona'ne.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' rɨ tiwʉ' nakapu po te'sen kʉu'tɨnin ɨ'rɨ rɨ anʉnse'na tiwʉ' tapai.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉmainarʉ yau te'sen kʉ'tɨnin tiwʉ' ta' tʉpon epose'na.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ wʉi a'tai'ne, ɨsɨ pe kuru rɨ uri'sami'si amʉ', mono' pe te'san pona iye'to' oton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ mana' pokon kon imunkɨ pona!</li>
      <li>Ɨpʉrematɨ' ɨutɨto' kon esi namai' komi' pata weyu a'tai, mɨrɨ pe pʉra Sapa' a'tai.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra mɨrɨ a'tai eke rɨ usewankaman e'to' oton pena pata epiya'tɨ'pʉ si'kɨrɨ iye'ku'sa' rʉ'pʉ kasa pʉra rɨ serɨ pʉ'kʉ pona, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ mɨrɨ kasa iye'to' oton pen nɨ kanan serɨ enta'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ weyu u'tɨsa' pʉra iyesi yau inke pʉra, ɨnʉ' ne'nonkai'no pen nɨ moro, e'tane kamoro, Papa nanʉmʉ'san pɨkɨrɨ iweyu to'kena'mato' iya oton.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai ɨnʉ' uya rɨ ta pe iyesi yau ɨpɨ'nokon, ‘Kʉrai man serɨ yau,’ mɨrɨ pe pʉra, ‘Mɨrɨ yau man,’ ta a'tai ɨpɨ'nokon, kʉsapurɨtʉu.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra enku'tɨnin nan kʉrai amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ enku'tɨnin nan pu'kena' amʉ' usenpoikato' oton, eke ton nɨ i'tuto' ipɨ' ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ eke Papa tʉrawasooi ton ku'to' oton to' uya, Papa nanʉmʉ'san enku'tɨnin pe—ikupʉ tʉuya'nokon pe iyesi yau.</li>
      <li>Entɨ' ayauro'ka uya 'nokon serɨ ton pɨ' iweyu wapiya.</li>
      <li>“Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ ta pe iyesi yau, ‘Mɨrɨ yau man, rɨmono' tau,’ ta a'tai, kʉtɨtʉu; mɨrɨ pe pʉra, ‘Serɨ yau man, ɨutɨ a'mu yau,’ ta a'tai, kʉsapurɨtʉu.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra kamiri' nʉye'ai'ne' wʉi enu uyepʉ winɨ nʉsenyai'ne' wʉi enu utɨto' pona rɨ kasa, mɨrɨ kasa kuru Ka'pon, Papa winon uyepʉ e'to' oton mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Eke' airɨ rɨ anwana amʉ' amʉrato' oton,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Inke pʉra rɨ, usewankaman pata'pʉ pe, “‘Wʉi enu ewarumanto' oton, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kapʉi e'wei'tɨto' oton pen; Sirikɨ amʉ' uta'po'to' oton ka' apai, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka' po te'sen ton nɨ e'tʉkʉukato' oton.’</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ a'tai, Ka'pon, Papa winon uyepʉ i'tuto' ipɨ' usenpoikato' oton ka' yau, mɨrɨpan tanporon kon non pon kon ukaranto' oton tʉuta'kwarʉkai'. To' uya Ka'pon, Papa winon uyepʉ kapuru' po, ka' yau ento' oton, tʉmeruntɨrʉ ke mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ eke a'kwa yau.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya tinserʉʉi ton enno'to' oton eke wai tʉronpi' turunpa pe, mɨrɨpan kon uya mɨ a'setun uye'to' yawɨron kon nɨ inanʉmʉ'san amʉranʉ'to' oton, ka' pʉ'kʉ awɨron kon nɨ.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsenupatɨ' serɨ pi' e' pɨ': Emenna' pe ipanta ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ iyare a'ta a'tai, i'tu auya'nokon wʉi uye'kapʉ a'ko pe tukai'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ tanporo serɨ ton e'kupʉ ene auya'nokon a'tai, i'tu auya'nokon a'ko pe iyesi, mʉra'ta nau rɨ.</li>
      <li>I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, serɨ a'taino kon kuru rɨ pʉra iyenato' oton pen nɨ tanporo serɨ ton e'kupʉ pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ.</li>
      <li>Epʉn mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ non pʉra iyenato' oton, e'tane umaimu mɨrɨ tereuta ton pen nɨ.</li>
      <li>“Ɨnʉ' uya mɨrɨ wʉi mɨrɨ pe pʉra iwekusi i'tu pʉra rɨ iyesi; inserʉ amʉ' Epʉn pon kon uya rɨ, mɨrɨ pe pʉra imu uya rɨ e'tane ikʉipʉnʉ uya rɨken serɨ i'tu.</li>
      <li>Nowa a'tai iyesi'pʉ na'ne' kasa, mɨrɨ kasa iye'to' oton Ka'pon, Papa winon uyepʉ a'tai.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra wʉi ton i'mʉnpʉ rawɨron yau, ka'pon amʉ' esi'pʉ uta're'tɨn pɨ', emari'man pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ e'tʉrʉn pɨ' emari'man nɨto' yau, Nowa ewomʉ a' ya' weyu pona rɨ.</li>
      <li>Ɨ'rɨ rɨ te'ku'ton i'tu to' uya pʉra rɨ iyesi'pʉ i'mʉnpʉ uyepʉ pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ, mɨrɨpan kon arɨ'pʉ iya tanporo rɨ. Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ iye'to' oton, Ka'pon, Papa winon uyepʉ a'tai.</li>
      <li>Asa'ron kon ka'pon amʉ' e'to' oton umɨ yau; tikin nɨ itanʉnto' oton, isakon e'nɨnto' oton.</li>
      <li>Asa'ron kon uri'sami'si amʉ' e'to' oton a'nai' e'pa pɨ'; tikin nɨ itanʉnto' oton, isakon e'nɨnto' oton.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', enei'ma e'tɨ', apʉne pʉra i'tu auya'nokon kasa pʉra ɨ'rɨ a'tai ɨyepuru kon uyepʉ tukai'.</li>
      <li>E'tane se ito'ka'nʉ'tɨ': Ɨutɨ esa' uya mɨrɨ a'tai kuru ewarupɨ nau ama' uyepʉ tukai' i'tusa' yau, tenu ke iyesi'pʉ nesii'no, mɨrɨpan tiwʉ' ta' ewon nɨ kuu'pʉ iya nesii'no pen.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', ɨmɨrɨ'nokon kanan tekonekai' me'tʉi', apʉne pʉra Ka'pon, Papa winon uye'to' oton itenupɨkɨrɨ pʉra rɨ ɨwe'tane'nokon,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Ɨnʉ' ken usauro'nɨ'pʉ awɨron mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ emiya'pokena' ipoitorʉ pe nai itesa' nʉnonka'pʉ tiwʉ' tawon kon tʉpoitorʉ ton esa' pe to' i'kiyari ke to' repanin pe itʉto' weyu a'tai?</li>
      <li>Wakʉ pe rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ ipoitorʉ e'to' oton itepuru neporonʉ ikupʉ pɨ' tenna'posa' a'tai.</li>
      <li>I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; itepuru uya tanporon nɨ tapuruui esa' pe iku'to' oton.</li>
      <li>E'tane si, a'tai pʉra kʉrɨ rɨ ipoitorʉ esi ɨri pe, mɨrɨpan uya, ‘Uyepuru uko'mamʉ serɨ sunwa inke rɨ,’ ta,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan e'sara'tɨ tʉron kon ipoitorʉ ton panta'ma pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ enta'nan pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ e'taripan pɨ' te'taripasan pokon pe.</li>
      <li>Kʉrɨ rɨ ipoitorʉ epuru uye'to' oton wʉi a'tai itenupɨkɨrɨ iye'tane pʉra, mɨrɨ a'kʉra' iyepʉ ta tane iya pʉra rɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya ipɨrʉkato' oton, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ inonkato' iya oton wakʉ pe te'ku'san pata'se' ya'. Mɨrɨ yau nin si, ipan pe ukaran nɨ pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉyɨ ton kɨtɨtɨi'ma pɨ' iye'to' oton,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Miyarɨ rɨ Sises uya tʉpoitorʉ ton auro'ka'pʉ. “Mɨrɨ a'tai si, Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe e'to' oton mɨrɨ se kasa; moine warawo' emari'ma ense'na 10 kaisaron kon uri'sami'si amʉ' utɨ'pʉ tʉraan'puui ke'ne.</li>
      <li>5 kaisaron kon uri'sami'si amʉ' esi'pʉ ita'kwarʉ pʉra, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ 5 kaisaron kon kanan esi'pʉ ta'kwarʉ ke.</li>
      <li>Ita'kwarʉ pʉ' nan uya tʉraan'puui kon arɨ'pʉ, e'tane iparu u'ma'sa' a'taino arɨ'pʉ to' uya pen nɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane ta'kwarʉkena' nan uya tʉraan'puui kon arɨ'pʉ iparu u'ma'sa' a'taino a'kɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Inke rɨ to' enurikʉ'pʉ kʉrɨ rɨ temari'masen uyepʉ i'se, mɨrɨpan kon ena'pʉ e'moronʉ' pe, mɨrɨpan kon nin si e'nʉmʉ'pʉ mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“Anomʉra' a'tai nin si, ka'pon uya eke pe ekama'pʉ mɨrɨ, ‘Temari'masen si uye'nɨ pɨ' man! Entanʉ'tɨ' si!’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Kamoro si uri'sami'si amʉ' usenpaka'pʉ mɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan kon e'mʉ'sa'ka'pʉ tʉraan'puui kon po'tɨse'na.</li>
      <li>Iya'kwarʉ pʉ' nan uya ta'kwarʉkena' nan pɨ', ‘Ina raan'puui paru oton ke ina irepatɨ', ina raan'puui usenkʉ'nʉ' nɨ pɨ' man,’ ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“E'tane kamoro uya, ‘Kane, eke pe pʉra rʉ'kwɨ iparu man; ukaisarɨ'nokon pʉra man,’ ta'pʉ to' uya. ‘E'tane ru'ku, siya'pu ta' araan'puui kon paru ɨne'matantɨ' ɨiwano' kon pe,’ ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Utɨn pɨ' rɨ nin si to' e'tane tʉraan'puui kon paru ennai', temari'masen uye'kaa'pʉ mɨrɨ. Kamoro nin si iyekonekasa' kon uri'sami'si amʉ' ewomʉ'pʉ mɨrɨ temari'masen a'kɨrɨ ata're'tɨse'na. Mʉra'ta nin si uta'koro'pʉ mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“Emennʉ'pʉ rɨ kamoro nin si uyee'pʉ mɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan kon uya ta'pʉ, ‘Ina epuru, mʉra'ta a'kokakɨ ina iwano' pe!’ ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“E'tane to' eikʉ'pʉ iya, ‘I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, ɨi'tu uya 'nokon pʉra man,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', enei'ma e'tɨ'; apʉne pʉra iweyu mɨrɨ pe pʉra iwekusi i'tu auya'nokon pʉra iyesi pɨ',” ta'pʉ Sises uya tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kanan, ka'pon tʉutɨsen kasa iye'to' oton, tʉpoitorʉ ton kɨ'manin mɨrɨpan kon ena' timamin tʉnin.</li>
      <li>Tikin nan ena' 5 kaisa rɨ ipaikii pʉrata tʉrʉ'pʉ iya, tʉron nɨ ena' asa'rɨ ipaikii tʉrʉ'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan kon tonpa ena' tikin nɨ ipaikii pʉrata tʉrʉ'pʉ iya. To' repa'pʉ iya mɨrɨ to' uya ikupʉ poken iyesi ti'tui', mɨrɨpan nin si utɨ'pʉ tʉutɨto' ya'.</li>
      <li>Kʉrɨ rɨ si 5 kaisaron paiki pʉrata eponin nʉ'pʉ utɨ'pʉ inke pʉra rɨ mɨrɨ pʉrata e'tonpa'tɨto' pe itʉrawasomase'na, emennʉ'pʉ tʉpoi'ne rɨ nin si, 5 kaisarɨ rɨ marɨ iye'tonpa'tɨsa' esi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ, asa'rɨ ipaikii eponin nʉ'pʉ utɨ'pʉ inke pʉra rɨ mɨrɨ pʉrata e'tonpa'tɨto' pe itʉrawasomase'na, mɨrɨpan uya asa'rɨ rɨ marɨ paikii tonpa'tɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>E'tane nin si, kʉrɨ tikin nɨ paiki eponin nʉ'pʉ utɨ'pʉ, non aka'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan uya tepuru pʉrataai onamʉ'pʉ iya'.</li>
      <li>“Inke rɨ tʉuko'mamʉ tʉpo, to' epuru enna'po'pʉ to' piya', mɨrɨpan uya to' pokon pe tʉpʉrataai eseru koneka'pʉ.</li>
      <li>5 kaisa rɨ eponin nʉ'pʉ uya 5 kaisarɨ rɨ marɨ ipona tʉneporo'pʉ tʉrʉ'pʉ itena'. ‘Uyepuru, 5 kaisa rɨ ipaikii urepa'pʉ auya, mɨrɨpan tonpa'tɨsa' uya man mɨrɨ rɨ tʉtʉrawasomai', 5 kaisarɨ rɨ marɨ ipona,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“‘Wakʉ kuru rɨ ku'sa' auya man, upoitorʉ, wakʉ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ usauro'nɨsa' awɨron! Tu'kan pen nʉ'kwɨ rɨ pɨ' yawɨrɨ ɨwe'sa' man. Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', tu'kan nɨ esa' pe ɨnonka uya. Ɨsi'kɨ upiya' pori' pe e'tanʉ'kɨ ɨyepuru pokon pe!’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Asa'rɨ ipaikii pʉrata eponin nʉ'pʉ uyee'pʉ tepuru piya', ‘Uyepuru, asa'rɨ ipaikii pʉrata urepataine' tonpa'tɨsa' uya man mɨrɨ rɨ tʉtʉrawasomai', asa'rɨ rɨ marɨ ipaikii ipona,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Itepuru uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', ‘Wakʉ kuru rɨ ku'sa' auya man, upoitorʉ, wakʉ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ usauro'nɨsa' awɨron! Tu'kan pen nʉ'kwɨ rɨ pɨ' yawɨrɨ ɨwe'sa' man. Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', tu'kan nɨ esa' pe ɨnonka uya. Ɨsi'kɨ, pori' pe ɨyepuru esi pokon pe e'tanʉ'kɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Kʉrɨ rɨ si tikin nɨ pʉrata paikii eponin nʉ'pʉ uyee'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ tepuru pɨ', ‘Uyepuru, ɨi'tu uya, sa'man pe rɨ te'sen pe ɨwesi. Ɨnpɨmɨ'pʉ pen nɨ anʉnnin pe ɨwesi, ite' ɨntʉrʉ'pɨtʉ'pʉ pen nɨ amʉranʉ'nin pe ɨwesi.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pɨ', enari'nʉmʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan pɨ' ɨpʉrataai onanse'na utɨ'pʉ non ya'. Se si ɨiwano' pe te'sen,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨpan pɨ' ta'pʉ itepuru uya, ‘Ɨmɨrɨ, emiya'ne' rɨ ipoitorʉ! I'tu auya si unpɨmɨ'pʉ pen nɨ anʉnnin pe esi, ite' untʉrʉ'pɨtʉ'pʉ pen nɨ amʉranʉ'nin pe esi?</li>
      <li>Upʉrataai rɨ sa'ne mʉtʉrʉi'no pʉrata e'tonpa'tɨto' iwʉ' ta'; enna'posa' a'tai, iye'tonpa'tɨsa' simo'kai'no,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“‘Mɨrɨ pʉrata paikii imo'katɨ' itenapai, mɨrɨpan itʉtɨ' kʉrɨ 10 kaisaron pʉrata paikii esa' ena'.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra tanporon kon itesa' pe na'ne' nan nɨ repa, miyarɨ ipona rɨ, mɨrɨpan esa' pe iye'to' oton eke pe rɨ. Ɨnʉ' rɨ kʉrɨ itesa' pe pʉra na'ne' enapai, itenau rʉ'kwɨ rɨ na'ne' emo'ka mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan ɨri rɨ poitorʉ eno'ma pʉroroi pona, ewarupɨ ya'. Mɨrɨ yau, ukaran nɨ pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉyɨ kɨtɨtɨi'ka pɨ' iye'to' pe,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Ka'pon, Papa winon uyepʉ a'tai tʉmeruntɨrʉ yau, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tinserʉʉi amʉ' pokon pe, iyereutato' oton tapon po.</li>
      <li>Tanporo rɨ tʉpataron kon amʉrato' oton irau, mɨrɨpan uya ka'pon amʉ' menka, karimeru amʉ' pa'simanin uya karimeru amʉ' menka kasa kapirita amʉ' piyapai.</li>
      <li>Karimeru amʉ' tʉrʉ iya mɨrɨ tenwo'netʉ winɨkʉi', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kapirita amʉ' tʉkamisi winɨkʉi'.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ a'tai si, ta iya mɨrɨ tenwo'netʉ winɨ te'san pɨ', ‘Ɨsi'tɨ' ɨmɨrɨ'nokon ukʉipʉnʉ nʉpʉrema'san. Ananʉmʉnʉ kon anʉntɨ', serɨ si ɨyesa' kon pe e'nɨto' yau iyekonekasa' rʉ'pʉ pata e'kaa'pʉ si'kɨrɨ rɨ,</li>
      <li>apʉne pʉra iwan pe esi a'tai, urepa'pʉ auya'nokon ui'kiyari ke; tuna'kiri' ke esi a'tai, uwo'pa'pʉ auya'nokon; ka'kʉran pe rɨ e'tane, ukɨ'ma'pʉ auya'nokon ɨiwʉ' kon ta'.</li>
      <li>Ipon pʉra esi a'tai, urepa'pʉ auya'nokon upon ke; takuru'ke esi a'tai, umainanpa pɨ' ɨwesi'pʉ kon; pariki'si tau esi a'tai, uka'kʉranpase'na ɨutɨ'pʉ kon,’ tato' iya oton.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ a'tai si, ipokena' ton uya ta mɨrɨ ipɨ', ‘Uyepuru, ɨ'rɨ a'tai si iwan pe ina uya ɨyene'pʉ, mɨrɨpan ina uya ɨyewekʉ'pʉ; mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tuna'kiri' ke, mɨrɨpan o'pa'pʉ ina uya?</li>
      <li>Ɨ'rɨ a'tai ka'kʉran pe ina uya ɨyene'pʉ, mɨrɨpan ɨkɨ'ma'pʉ ina uya tiwʉ' kon ta'? Ɨ'rɨ a'tai ipon pʉra ina uya ɨyene'pʉ, mɨrɨpan ɨpontɨ'pʉ ina uya?</li>
      <li>Ɨ'rɨ a'tai rɨ takuru'ke mɨrɨ pe pʉra pariki'si tau ɨwe'tane, ina utɨ'pʉ aka'kʉranpai'?’ tato' oton to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ a'tai nin si, kin uya ta mɨrɨ to' pɨ', ‘I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, ɨ'rɨ rɨ ku'sa' auya'nokon na'ne' pʉsamoro sepa' nan nʉ'kwɨ kuru utonpa ton pe te'san pɨ', urɨ pɨ' iku'sa' auya'nokon pe iyesi,’ tato' iya oton.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ a'tai ta iya mɨrɨ, tʉkamisi winon kon pɨ', ‘Atamatɨ' upiyapai, ɨmɨrɨ'nokon Papa nʉpa'nʉkʉ'san! Entantɨ' apo' ya', Papa nʉkoneka'pʉ makoi mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ itinserʉʉi ton iwano' pe!</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra iwan pe e'tane, urepasa' auya'nokon pʉra iyesi ui'kiyari ke; tuna'kiri' ke e'tane, uwo'pa'pʉ auya'nokon pʉra iyesi;</li>
      <li>ka'kʉran pe e'tane, ɨiwʉ' kon ta' ukɨ'masa' auya'nokon pʉra iyesi; upon i'se e'tane, upon ke urepasa' auya'nokon pʉra iyesi; takuru'ke e'tane, umainanpasa' auya'nokon pʉra iyesi; pariki'si tau e'tane, uka'kʉranpai' ɨutɨsa' kon pʉra iyesi,’ tato' iya oton to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ a'tai, to' uya rɨ marɨ ei'to' oton, ‘Ina epuru, ɨ'rɨ a'tai rɨ si ina uya ɨyene'pʉ iwan pe, tuna'kiri' ke, mɨrɨ pe pʉra ka'kʉran pe, mɨrɨpan ina uya asanomasa' pʉra iyesi? Ɨ'rɨ a'tai rɨ si ɨpon i'se, takuru'ke mɨrɨ pe pʉra pariki'si tau ɨwe'tane, ina uya ɨpika'tɨsa' pʉra iyesi?’ tato' oton.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ a'tai si, to' eikʉ iya mɨrɨ, ‘I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, ɨ'rɨ rɨ ku'sa' auya'nokon pʉra na'ne', pʉsamoro sepa' nan nʉ'kwɨ kuru utonpa ton pe te'san pɨ', urɨ pɨ' iku'sa' auya'nokon pe pʉra rɨ iyesi.’</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨpan kon utɨto' oton tɨwɨrɨ rɨ ekota'man nɨto' ya', e'tane ipokena' ton pe iye'sa' kon utɨto' oton tɨwɨrɨ rɨ uko'man nɨto' ya',” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Tanporo si serɨ ton ekama tʉuya tʉpo, Sises uya ta'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ',</li>
      <li>“Mi'tuyatʉi'ne' kasa rɨ To' Epoi Itɨ'pʉ Weyu Rʉ'pʉ esi awanapai rɨ ema'sa' yau. Ka'pon, Papa winon tʉto' oton ipokapɨ'to' pe kurusu' pona,” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ tʉpo si, use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' epuru ton amʉra'pʉ. To' e'seporo'pʉ Kaya'pas pata'se' yau, use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru eke pe kuru te'sen.</li>
      <li>To' e'kama'pʉ ama'ai Sises a'si pɨ' iwɨto' pe tʉuya'nokon.</li>
      <li>“E'tane iweyu rʉ'pʉ a'tai pen. Mɨrɨ ku'sa' pe iyesi yau, ka'pon amʉ' uya nin urɨ'nokon ewa'noma mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises esi koro'tau Pe'tani po, Saiman, erekʉ'pan tukai' ti'tusen iwʉ' tau,</li>
      <li>uri'san uyee'pʉ po'toro arapasta yawon po'piyun epe'kena' kuru rɨ esa' pe, mɨrɨpan uya a'koka'pʉ Sises i'pai pona ima'pʉ iya, tʉteire' po tenai' tepʉrʉ piyau iyesi koro'tau.</li>
      <li>Ipoitorʉ ton uya serɨ ensa' a'tai, to' usakorota'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya, “Ɨ'rɨto' pe ima'tanʉkʉ iya?” ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“Serɨ po'piyun kʉrʉpo'pomai'no sa'ne epe'kena' pe, mɨrɨpan epe'pʉ tʉrʉi'no entu'manin nan ena'!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' i'tusa' esi'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Ɨ'rɨ to' pe pʉse rɨ uri'san a'pɨ'pɨtʉ auya'nokon? Wakʉ rɨ ku'sa' iya mɨrɨ upɨ'.</li>
      <li>Tɨwɨrɨ rɨ entu'manin nan esi ɨpiyau'nokon, e'tane tɨwɨrɨ rɨ urɨ esi pʉra iyesi ɨpiyau'nokon.</li>
      <li>Serɨ po'piyun masa' iya upona iku'sa' iya mɨrɨ upun koneka pe uwu'na'tɨ e'ma ta'.</li>
      <li>I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, itekare nʉsekamayai'ne' airɨ rɨ pata emʉ' kaisa rɨ inkupʉ'pʉ rʉ'pʉ rɨ marɨ usekama mɨrɨ, en yau ikupʉ pe rɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>12 kaisaron kon ipoitorʉ ton tonpa, Isutas Eskariya' tato' ipɨ', utɨ'pʉ use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru piya'.</li>
      <li>“Ɨ'rɨ ke uye'ma auya'nokon ɨyena'nokon itʉsa' uya yau?” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', mɨrɨpan kon uya 30 kaisa rɨ sirʉpa pʉrata pun i'tu'pʉ itiwano' pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ si'kɨrɨ Isutas esi'pʉ itʉto' tʉuya weyu eporo i'se.</li>
      <li>A'sarutanʉ'sa' Pen Pʉreti Pɨ' Enta'nan Weyu e'sara'tɨ a'tai, Sises poitorʉ ton uyee'pʉ ipiya' ekama'pose'na, “Nai yau kuru ina uya To' Epoi Itɨ'pʉ Weyu Rʉ'pʉ pɨ' ɨyenta'nato' koneka ina uya i'se me'an?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>To' eikʉ'pʉ iya, “Entantɨ' eke pata Surusiran pona ka'pon piya', mɨrɨpan pɨ', ‘Ti'sa uya tasa' man, “Papa nʉkoneka'pʉ uweyu e'seposa' man, a'ko pe. Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', urɨ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ upoitorʉ ton pokon pe To' Epoi Itɨ'pʉ Weyu Rʉ'pʉ kupʉ uya ɨiwʉ' tau,” tukai',’ mekamatʉi' ipɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ipoitorʉ ton uya mɨrɨ kasa rɨ nin si To' Epoi Itɨ'pʉ Weyu Rʉ'pʉ pɨ' te'to' kon koneka'pʉ, ta'pʉ iya na'ne' awɨrɨ rɨ.</li>
      <li>Pata uko'mansa' a'tai, Sises esi'pʉ tʉteire' po tenai' 12 kaisaron kon pokon pe tepʉrʉ piyau.</li>
      <li>To' enta'na koro'tau, ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; ɨtonpa kon uya uyeparankato' oton,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon upokoita'pʉ, to' uya tʉkaisarɨ'nokon, “I'napai rɨ, uyepuru, urɨ pen kuru rɨ nin!” ta'pʉ Sises pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Kʉrɨ tʉyu ki'ai'ne' pʉsau ya' upokon pe uya uyeparankato' oton.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon, Papa winon utɨto' oton tʉpɨ' imenukasa' na'ne' kasa rɨ, e'tane ɨsɨ yau rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ ka'pon esi Ka'pon, Papa winon eparankanin. Wakʉ pe nesii'no iyentusa' pʉra iyesi yau,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan Isutas, eparankanin oton uya nin si ta'pʉ, “Rapai, i'napai rɨ, urɨ pen kuru rɨ nin,” ta'pʉ iya. “Ewai', ɨmɨrɨ rɨ,” tukai' Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>To' enta'na koro'tau rɨ, Sises uya pʉreti anʉmʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya tenki ta'pʉ Papa pɨ'. I'kwɨ'pɨtʉ'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan ekamʉ'pʉ iya tʉpoitorʉ ton ena', tai'ma to' pɨ', “Anʉntɨ', mɨrɨpan ɨ'tɨ'. Serɨ serɨ upun,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya ko', waain yen anʉmʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya tenki ta'pʉ Papa pɨ'. To' ena' itʉrʉ'pʉ iya, tai'ma to' pɨ', “Se yawon ensitɨ', ɨmɨrɨ'nokon.</li>
      <li>Serɨ serɨ emenna' ekonekan nɨto' iwano' umʉnʉ, tu'kan kon iwano' pe rɨ iye'kwansa' makoi ton pɨ' usentu'man nɨto' pe.</li>
      <li>Ekama uya serɨ enta' iteperu euku ensito' uya oton pen ɨpokon pe 'nokon ukʉipʉnʉ e'to' esa' wannɨ pe yau emenna' pe ensi uya pʉ'kʉ pona,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Eren pɨ' tʉuserenka kon tʉpo, to' utɨ'pʉ Are' Wʉpʉ pona.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya to' pana'tɨ'pʉ, “Serɨ ewarupɨɨi tau kuru, tanporo rɨ unɨmɨ auya'nokon mɨrɨ, te'ku'sen upɨ' wenai, apʉne pʉra iye'menukasa', “‘Karimeru amʉ' pa'simanin wɨnɨ uya mɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan karimeru amʉ' e'ta'nʉ'to' oton tamʉ' ke te'to' kon apai,’ tukai'.</li>
      <li>E'tane e'mʉ'sa'kasa' tʉpo, utɨ mɨrɨ arawɨrɨ'nokon Kiyarari pona,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Pi'ta uya, “Tanporon kon uya ɨnɨntane te'ku'sen ɨpɨ' wenai, urɨ uya nin ɨnonka pen mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ Sises pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya imaimu eikʉ'pʉ, “I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ', serɨ ewarupɨɨi tau kuru, kɨrɨtɨkɨ uturumʉ rawɨrɨ, osorʉwau ite'kwa unonkato' auya oton,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane rɨ Pi'ta uya, “Uma'tato' pe rɨ aya'kɨrɨ, ɨnonka uya pen nɨ mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ. Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ itonpa ton uya ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises utɨ'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton pokon pe Ke'semani tukai' tesa'sen pata ya', mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Se airɨ ereutatɨ', mɨ airɨ ɨpʉremai' utɨ tane,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ta'kɨrɨ Pi'ta mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ asa'rɨ Sepiti munkɨ amʉ' arɨ'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan ena'pʉ pokoi pe mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ika'nɨ' pʉra rɨ.</li>
      <li>“Uyewan man ika'nɨ' pʉra rɨ, e'tape'ne' pe rɨ iyesi uma'tanʉkʉ iya rɨ. Serɨ yau e'tɨ', uya'kɨrɨ tenu ke e'tɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Itɨ'pʉ miyarɨ parɨ ɨnnɨ iwa to' piyapai, mɨrɨpan uta'mo'ka'pʉ non pona temʉ' po, mɨrɨpan ɨpʉrema'pʉ, “Ukʉipʉnʉ, iye'kupʉ pe iyesi yau tɨwɨ upiyapai ko' nʉtamai, e'tane uyeseru awɨrɨ pen, e'tane ɨyeseru awɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan enna'po'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton piya', mɨrɨpan uya to' e'nʉmʉ eporo'pʉ. Pi'ta ekama'po'pʉ iya, “Uya'kɨrɨ pe' ɨmɨrɨ'nokon warawoti'si amʉ' esi poken pʉra iyesi tenu ke mara rʉ'kwɨ rɨ?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Tenu ke esii'ma ɨpʉrematɨ', i'tupɨ'nɨto' ya' auta'mo'ka kon namai'. Iya'kwarʉ esi ɨnku'pai, e'tane ipun esi ɨ'sɨ'mʉra,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises enna'pokaa'pʉ iyakon ite'kwa pe ɨpʉremase'na. “Ukʉipʉnʉ, iye'kupʉ poken pʉra rɨ iyesi yau, serɨ ko' utama poken pʉra upiyapai ensi uya a'tai rɨken, tɨwɨ ɨyeseru ne'kupʉi,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Iyenna'posa' a'tai kanan, to' rɨ marɨ e'nʉnpɨ'sa' eporo'pʉ iya, apʉne pʉra e'tape'ne' pe'ne to' enu pi'pɨ ton esi ke,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan kon piyapai ɨpʉremaka'se'na kanan itɨ'pʉ itosorʉwano ite'kwa pe, wapiya tʉwɨpʉrema'pʉ kasa rɨ marɨ iyepʉrema'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan enna'po'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton piya', mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Mɨrɨ si e'nʉn nɨ pɨ' rɨ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ umoronka'nɨ pɨ' rɨ ɨwesi kon? Apʉne entɨ'! Iweyu e'seposa' man! Ka'pon, Papa winon eparankasa' man tʉmakooikena' nan ena'!</li>
      <li>E'mʉ'sa'katɨ'! Utɨnpai'nokon! Uyeparankanin si uye'ka'nɨ pɨ' man!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Usauro'nɨ pɨ' rɨ marɨ iyesi koro'tau, Isutas, 12 kaisaron kon tonpa pe te'sen uyee'pʉ. Ipokon pe anpisin kuru rɨ usepai'tɨpɨ'sa' supara ke mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ wa'tana ke esi'pʉ, use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon amʉ' epuru ton nennoko'san.</li>
      <li>Eparankanin uya tʉnku'ton ekamasa' esi'pʉ to' pɨ': “Kʉrɨ sa'su'kayai'ne' si kʉrɨ rɨ; ma'sitʉi',” tasa' esi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Isutas utɨ'pʉ Sises piya' to'sarɨ rɨ, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Miyarɨ, Rapai!” mɨrɨpan a'su'ka'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Utonpa, iku'se ɨuye'sa' na'ne' rɨ iku'kɨ,” ta'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨ a'tai, ka'pon amʉ' utɨ'pʉ Sises winɨkʉi' mɨrɨpan kon uya a'si'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pɨ' tikin nan nɨ Sises tonpa ton tonpa uya tʉsuparaai mo'ka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru poitorʉ pana a'tɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Sises uya nin si ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Ɨsuparaai ina'poka'kɨ si ipata'pʉ ya'! Kamoro supara apurɨnin nʉ'san nɨ eri'to' oton esi mɨrɨ supara ke rɨ.</li>
      <li>I'tu auya'nokon pʉra rɨ iyesi mɨrɨ, ukʉipʉnʉ pɨ' ɨpʉremato', mɨrɨ a'tai upiya' 12 kaisa rɨ ite'kwa anpisin ton kuru rɨ inserʉ amʉ' enno'to' iya upika'tɨnin nan pe.</li>
      <li>E'tane mɨrɨ ku'sa' uya pe iyesi yau, itekare uya ekamasa' na'ne' uta'ku'tɨ pʉra rɨ iyesi, mɨrɨ e'ku'to' oton tasa' iya na'ne',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya ta'pʉ anpisin pɨ', “Main awɨron kon pen pe' esa' pe esi serɨ, ɨuye'sa' kon na'ne' supara amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ wa'tana amʉ' esa' pe uya'sise'na? Wʉi kaisarɨ rɨ e'tai ko use'man nɨto', ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' pʉ'kʉ tau tereutai' ka'pon amʉ' enupa pɨ', uya'si auya'nokon pʉra rɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane tanporo rɨ serɨ e'ku'sa' pu'kena' amʉ' nʉmenuka'pʉ uta'ku'tɨto' pe,” ta'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨ a'tai si, tanporo ipoitorʉ ton uya inonka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon ainʉmʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Kamoro, Sises a'sinin nʉ'san uya arɨ'pʉ Kaya'pas, use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru piya', Main pɨ' enupanin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' epuru ton amʉrasa' airɨ.</li>
