      <li>E'tane Pi'ta uya e'ma'pʉka'pʉ ɨnnonsi'kɨ rɨ, use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru iwʉ' pʉrorooi pona, mɨrɨpan ewomʉ'pʉ, iyereuta'pʉ erasu ton piya' te'ku'sen ense'na.</li>
      <li>Use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tanporon kon nɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' Konsʉrʉʉi ton esi'pʉ kasi pe rɨ Sises eseru'tɨto' warinpa pɨ', iyeri'to' ya' itʉto' pe tʉuya'nokon.</li>
      <li>E'tane to' uya ɨ'rɨ rɨ iteseru eporo'pʉ pen nɨ mɨrɨ rɨ e'tane tu'ke rɨ kasi ye' pe tʉusauro'san esi'pʉ. Emennʉ'pʉ tʉpo rɨ, asa'ron kon ka'pon amʉ' uyee'pʉ,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan kon uya si ekama'pʉ, “Pʉse rɨ uya ta'pʉ, ‘Papa iwano' use'man nɨto', ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' ma'tanʉkʉ uya mɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan konekato' pe uya kanan osorʉwau wʉi yau,’ ta'pʉ iya,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai si, use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru e'soto'ka'pʉ Sises pɨ' tase'na, “Eikʉ auya pen nɨ pe' mɨrɨ? Ɨ'rɨ tukai' pʉsamoro ka'pon amʉ' usaurokʉ ɨpɨ'?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane Sises enkurumʉ'pʉ e'pana rɨ. Use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Ayapiyo'ma uya serɨ Papa tʉuko'mansen uya eta tane i'napairon pe ɨusekama pa ina pɨ'; Kʉrai pe pe' ɨwesi, Papa Mumu pe?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya imaimu eikʉ'pʉ, “Ewai', ta auya na'ne' kasa rɨ, e'tane tanporo ɨpɨ'nokon ta uya; Serɨ enta', Ka'pon, Papa winon ento' auya'nokon oton iyereutasa' Meruntɨ pe Te'sen enwo'netʉ winɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ iyepʉ Epʉn poi kapuru' yau,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru uya tʉpon karaka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ, “Papa sapema pe isaurokʉ! Ɨ'rɨto' pe miyarɨ rɨ ekamanin nan i'se e'nɨ? Entɨ', Papa sapema pe isaurokʉ etasa' auya'nokon.</li>
      <li>Ɨ'rɨ ken tukai' mɨsenuminkayatʉu?” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'. “Ima'tato' pe rɨ iyesi!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon eta'tapɨtʉ'pʉ itemʉ' pona, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ to' uya tʉmokorooi kon ke iwɨnɨ'pʉ. Tʉron kon uya rɨ inta'mopɨtʉ'pʉ,</li>
      <li>tai'ma, “Kʉrai, pu'kena' pe ekamakɨ ina pɨ'. Ɨnʉ' ɨwɨnɨi?” ta'pʉ to' uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Pi'ta ereutasa' esi'pʉ Papa ena' use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru iwʉ' pʉrorooi po, mɨrɨpan piya' to' poitorʉ, uri'san uyee'pʉ. “Ɨmɨrɨ sa'ne kʉrɨ rɨ ko Sises, Kiyarari pon a'kɨron nʉ'pʉ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane i'tunin pe pʉra iye'kuu'pʉ tanporo mɨrɨ yawon kon rau esii'ma. “I'tu uya pʉra rɨ man ɨ'rɨ pɨ' ausaurokʉ tukai',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ pʉroroi mʉra'taai pona. Mɨrɨ yau, tʉron nɨ uri'san uya kanan ene'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ka'pon amʉ' mɨrɨ yau te'san pɨ', “Pʉse rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ Sises, Nasare' pon a'kɨron nʉ'pʉ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>I'tunin pe pʉra kanan iye'ku'kaa'pʉ, Papa kuru tesa'pɨ'se: “Kʉrɨ rɨ i'tu uya pʉra man!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mara rɨ iyesi'pʉ tʉpo kamoro mɨrɨ yau te'soto'pɨ'se te'san utɨ'pʉ Pi'ta piya', tase'na ipɨ', “I'napai rɨ kuru rɨ ɨmɨrɨ kʉrɨ rɨ to' tonpa, ausaurokʉ eseru uya ɨyekama,” ta'pʉ to' uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai si, Pi'ta e'pa'nʉkʉ'pʉ tiwano' pe rɨ, mɨrɨpan uya, “Tɨwɨ Papa ukota'mai kasi pe usaurokʉ pɨ'. Kʉrɨ rɨ i'tu uya pʉra man!” ta'pʉ. Mɨrɨ ta iya a'tai rɨ, kɨrɨtɨkɨ uturumʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai si, Pi'ta uya Sises maimu rʉ'pʉ nee'pʉ tenu ya', “Osorʉwau ite'kwa, ‘I'tu uya pʉra man,’ tato' auya oton, kɨrɨtɨkɨ uturumʉ rawɨrɨ!” tawon. Mɨrɨpan epa'ka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan ukaramʉ'pʉ ipan pe rɨ.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Awanakʉi' kuru, tanporo use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' epuru ton ekoneka'pʉ Sises uma'tato' pe iku'to' tʉuya'nokon pɨ'.</li>
      <li>To' uya auronpɨtʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan arɨ'pʉ to' uya Paire', kopʉna ena'.</li>
      <li>Sises eparankanin nʉ'pʉ, Isutas uya si ensa' esi'pʉ mɨrɨ, to' uya ikonekasa' Sises uma'tato' pe, ipan pe rɨ ipokoita'pʉ Sises eparankasa' tʉuya pɨ', mɨrɨpan uya 30 kaisaron sirʉpa pun na'po'pʉ use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' epuru ton ena'.</li>
      <li>“Umakoitasa' man, imakooi pʉn nɨ mʉnʉ teparankai',” ta'pʉ iya. “Ɨ'rɨ pe ken si mɨrɨ uya ina kupʉ? Ɨiwano' sa'ne mɨrɨ ko!” ta'pʉ to' uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ wenai, Isutas uya pʉrata pun eno'ma'pʉ use'man nɨto', ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' pʉ'kʉ ta', mɨrɨpan enna'po'pʉ tiwano' pe rɨ e'sa'mase'na.</li>
      <li>Use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton uya pʉrata pun amuku'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya ta'pʉ, “Main, Mosi' winon nɨ pʉremekʉ pe iyesi mɨrɨ inonkasa' a'tai pʉrata yen ya', apʉne pʉra mʉn epe'pʉ pe iyesi ke,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon ekoneka'pʉ mɨrɨ pʉrata ke ɨinɨ ka'nin pata'se' e'mato' pe tukai'. Mɨrɨ si kupʉ'pʉ to' uya ka'kʉran amʉ' pe te'san eri'sa' u'na'tɨto' yau pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ wenai, ka'pon amʉ' uya mɨrɨ pata esakʉ Mʉn Pata'se' tukai' serɨ pʉ'kʉ pona.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ si pu'kena' Iseremaya nekama'pʉ rʉ'pʉ pena rɨ uta'ku'tɨ'pʉ se tawon: “To' uya si 30 kaisa rɨ sirʉpa pun anʉmʉ'pʉ, Esuwerʉ amʉ' nʉkupʉ'pʉ itepe' pe,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan kon uya mɨrɨ pʉrata ke ɨinɨ ka'nin nan pata'se' e'ma'pʉ, uyepuru uya uyapiyo'ma'pʉ awɨrɨ rɨ,” tawon.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ koro'tau rɨ Sises e'soto'kasa' esi'pʉ kopʉna Paire' piya', mɨrɨpan ekama'po'pʉ Paire' uya, “Esuwerʉ amʉ' kin pe' ɨmɨrɨ?” ta'pʉ iya. Sises uya imaimu eikʉ'pʉ, “Ewai', mʉkayai'ne' kasa rɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' epuru ton uya ɨri pe, kasi pe rɨ teseru'tɨ a'tai eikʉ'pʉ iya pen.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Paire' uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Eta auya pʉra pe' iyesi ɨri pe to' usaurokʉ ɨpɨ'?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane Sises uya tikin nan pɨ' rɨ to' eikʉ'pʉ pen nɨ, ɨri pe to' uya tʉku'to' pɨ', kopʉna tewansiukai'.</li>
      <li>Kopʉna eseru esi'pʉ ka'pon nonkato' pariki'si tapai to' enta'nato' weyu a'tai anpisin ton nanʉmʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, tese ke te'sen a'sisa' pariki'si ta' esi'pʉ, Parapas tukai' tesa'sen.</li>
      <li>Tu'kan kon amʉrasa' a'tai, Paire' uya to' ekama'po'pʉ, “Nai kʉrɨ rupɨ enpa'ka uya i'se me'atʉu ɨiwano' kon pe? Parapas, mɨrɨ pe pʉra Sises, Kʉrai tato' katɨ?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra tɨkɨnta kon pɨ' to' uya itʉsa' tena' tukai' i'tu tʉuya pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Eseru aimenkato' apon po Paire' ereutasa' koro'tau rɨ, ino'pʉ uya se main enno'sa' esi'pʉ ipiya': “Ɨ'rɨ pe kʉrɨ rɨ, ɨ'rɨ ku'nin nʉ'pʉ pen nɨ ka'pon kʉ'kupʉi. Ɨri pe serɨ pe tekota'mapɨ'se e'ne'pɨ'sa' man kʉrɨ rɨ uriya',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' epuru ton uya ka'pon amʉ' pori'ma'pʉ to' uya Parapas ekama'poto' pe inonkato' pe iya, Sises ma'tanʉkʉi'ma.</li>
      <li>Kopʉna uya to' ekama'po'pʉ, “Nai kʉrɨ kuru nonka uya i'se me'atʉu ɨyena'nokon?” ta'pʉ iya. “Parapas,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Ɨ'rɨ pe ken si Sises, Kʉrai tato' ipɨ' kupʉ uya?” tukai' Paire' uya to' ekama'po'pʉ. Tanporon kon uya imaimu eikʉ'pʉ, “Kurusu' pona ipokapɨ'kɨ!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Ɨ'rɨto' pe? Ɨ'rɨ ɨri ku'sa' iya?” ta'pʉ Paire' uya. E'tane eke pe kuru to' ukɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨtʉ'pʉ, “Kurusu' pona ipokapɨ'kɨ!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Paire' uya ene'pʉ ɨ'rɨ pe iku'to' iya awɨrɨ pʉra rɨ, e'tane ɨsɨ pe rɨ to' ena esi'pʉ. Tuna anʉmʉ'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan isemiyakʉ'pʉ tu'kan kon rau esii'ma. “Tʉmakooi ke pʉra esi serɨ pʉse rɨ ka'pon mʉnʉ pɨ'. Ɨyenau'nokon nɨ iyesi mɨrɨ!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Tanporon kon uya imaimu eikʉ'pʉ, “Tɨwɨ ina mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ina munkɨ amʉ' iwano' pe imʉnʉ nesii!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya Parapas nonka'pʉ to' ena', e'tane ari'po'pɨ'to' pe Sises kupʉ'pʉ iya, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ itʉrʉ'pʉ iya kurusu' pona to' uya ipokapɨ'to' pe.</li>
      <li>Kopʉna soisaai amʉ' uya si Sises arɨ'pʉ kopʉna pe e'nɨ iwʉ' ta', mɨrɨpan kon uya tu'kan kon nɨ soisa amʉ' amʉranʉkʉ'pʉ Sises woi.</li>
      <li>To' uya iponka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan tʉtariren pon ke to' uya ipontɨ'pʉ,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan kon uya tikʉ ke te'sen e'mepɨtʉ'pʉ aro', kʉron pe, mɨrɨpan ke to' uya arʉko'tɨ'pʉ. To' uya iyɨɨi'tɨ'pʉ itenwo'netʉ winon itemiyatʉ ya', mɨrɨpan kon e'sekunkapɨtʉ'pʉ irau, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ to' uya isapema'pʉ. “Miyarɨ, Esuwerʉ amʉ' kin!” ta'pʉ to' uya Sises pɨ'.</li>
      <li>To' eta'tapɨtʉ'pʉ ipona; itɨɨi mo'ka'pʉ to' uya, mɨrɨ ke to' uya i'pai wɨpɨtʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Isapema tʉpo, to' uya iponka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan pontɨ'pʉ to' uya ipon ya', mɨrɨpan arɨ'pʉ to' uya kurusu' pona ipokapɨ'se'na.</li>
      <li>To' utɨ koro'tau, ka'pon Sairini winon, Saiman itese' eporo'pʉ to' uya, mɨrɨpan a'kwarʉka'pʉ to' uya kurusu' ato' pe iya.</li>
      <li>To' uyee'pʉ pata Korʉko'ta tato' ya' (Pu'pɨ Ɨ'pʉ Rʉ'pʉ Pata ta e'kwa pe).</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau, to' uya Sises o'pa'pʉ i'ne' ke waain tisumai'. Onpasa' tʉuya a'tai, ɨnensipai pʉra iyesi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Kurusu' pona ipokapɨ'sa' tʉuya'nokon a'tai, ipon nʉ'pʉ ta'nʉkʉ'pʉ to' uya te'wapiya'kapɨ'se,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan kon ereuta'pʉ enpɨ'se'na.</li>
      <li>Iwɨto' iwenai menukasa' poka'pʉ to' uya i'pai epoi; sises pʉse rɨ, esuwerʉ amʉ' kin, tawon.</li>
      <li>Asa'ron kon ama' rʉ'san pokapɨtʉ'pʉ to' uya ipokon pe; tikin nɨ itenwo'netʉ winɨ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ikamisi winɨ tikin nɨ.</li>
      <li>Kamoro ipiyawɨrɨ tʉutɨsan uya ɨri pe isapema'pʉ, ti'pai kon sʉkʉsʉkʉma'pʉ to' uya,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ta'pʉ to' uya, “Ɨmɨrɨ, use'man nɨto', ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' a'morʉkanin, mɨrɨpan amɨ auya osorʉwawon wʉi yau, epika'tɨ'! Ɨu'tɨkɨ kurusu' poi, Papa Mumu pe ɨwesi yau!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main pɨ' enupanin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' epuru ton uya rɨ isapema'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“Tʉron kon pika'tɨ'pʉ iya, e'tane tiwa rɨ iyepika'tɨ pʉra iyesi! Esuwerʉ amʉ' kin sa'ne si! Tɨwɨ si nʉu'tɨi kurusu' poi, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ urɨ'nokon uya apurɨto' pe.</li>
      <li>Papa apurɨnin kʉrɨ rɨ. Tɨwɨ Papa nʉpika'tɨi i'se tesi yau, ‘Papa Mumu urɨ,’ tasa' iya pɨ',” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ iya'kɨrɨ kurusu' pona ipokapɨ'sa' kon uya isapema'pʉ.</li>
      <li>12 a'kʉra' awonsi'kɨ 3 a'kʉra' pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ, tanporo rɨ pata ewarumamʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>3 a'kʉra' a'tai'ne rɨ, Sises ukɨ'pɨ'nʉmʉ'pʉ, “Iroi, Iroi, rama sapa'tani?” ta'pʉ iya, “Papa, Papa, ɨ'rɨto' pe unonkasa' auya?” ta e'kwa pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau si te'soto'pɨ'se te'san uya serɨ etasa' a'tai, “Iraisa kɨ'ma pɨ' man!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Inke pʉra, tikin nɨ to' tonpa pe te'sen si eka'tumʉ'pʉ mɨrɨ su'pa epose, waain maku'pɨ peneka ka' ikii'pʉ iya, yʉi pɨ' tepu'tɨi' Sises uya ensito' pe ikupʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>E'tane tʉron kon ka'pon amʉ' uya, “Tɨwɨ nesii. Apʉne, Iraisa uyepʉ enpai'nokon ipika'tɨi',” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises kanan ukɨ'pɨ'nʉnkaa'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ta'kwarʉ tʉrʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai rɨ si, Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' itau wapu pe te'sen ekaraka'pʉ inakapu ponsi'kɨ non pona a'sa'mʉyai. Tʉrʉ'pʉnʉ amʉ' esi'pʉ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tɨ' amʉ' uta'morʉpɨtʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Uruwai' amʉ' uta'kokapɨtʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan wakʉ ton ka'pon amʉ' iyeri'sa' kon e'mʉ'sa'ka'pʉ kanan.</li>
      <li>To' nin si epa'ka'pʉ mɨrɨ uruwai' yapai. Emennʉ'pʉ po, Sises e'mʉ'sa'kasa' a'tai nin si, to' utɨ'pʉ mɨrɨ Surusiran pona. Mɨrɨ yau, tu'kan kon nɨ ka'pon amʉ' uya to' ene'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Roman amʉ' soisaai ton epuru mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ita'kɨrɨ te'san itonpa ton Sises erasuntɨ pɨ' te'san uya tʉrʉ'pʉnʉ amʉ' utɨ i'tu'pʉ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tanporon nɨ te'ku'sen ene'pʉ, ipan pe rɨ to' etʉipɨtʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya, “I'napai rɨ kuru rɨ ka'si, pʉse rɨ esi'pʉ mɨrɨ wa Papa Mumu pe!” ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Tu'kan kon nɨ uri'sami'si amʉ' esi'pʉ enpɨtʉ pɨ' ɨnnonsi'kɨ. Sises e'ma'pʉkasa' to' uya esi'pʉ Kiyarari poi, ipika'tɨ pɨ' to' esi'pʉ i'se iye'to' ke.</li>
      <li>To' koro'tau Meri Mataren; Meri, Isens mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Isose' san; mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Sepiti munkɨ amʉ' san.</li>
      <li>Pata uko'mankapʉ koro'tau, imaminke' ka'pon, Arama'tiya winon uyee'pʉ. Itese' esi'pʉ Isose', Sises poitorʉ pe iyenasa' rʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Paire' piya' itɨ'pʉ Sises ekepu ekama'pose, ato' pe tʉuya. Paire' uya tʉsoisaai ton apiyo'ma'pʉ Sises ekepu tʉto' pe to' uya itena'.</li>
      <li>Isose' uya nin si itekepu arɨ'pʉ mɨrɨ. Iwontɨ'pʉ iya epe'kena' pon renen tato' atʉ ke,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan uya Sises ekepu nonka'pʉ tiwano' pe emenna' pe tɨ' akasa' uruwai' pe ya'. Eke rɨ tɨ' tʉtɨrinkai' imʉra'taai a'koro'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan nin si utɨ'pʉ mɨrɨ, mɨrɨ yapai.</li>
      <li>Meri Mataren mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉron nɨ Meri ereutasa' esi'pʉ tɨ' akasa' uruwai' pe ratoi pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ ema'sa' yau, Sapa' a'tai, Papa ena' use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton, Pari'si amʉ' utɨ'pʉ Paire' piya'.</li>
      <li>“Ina epuru, kʉrɨ Sises kasi ye' esi a'tai serɨ yau nurɨne isaurokʉ'pʉ esi ina enu yau, ‘Osorʉwau wʉi pata'pʉ pe e'mʉ'sa'kato' oton,’ tawon.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', ɨsoisaai ton apiyo'ma' iuruwasii erasuntɨto' pe to' uya serɨ awonsi'kɨ osorʉwau wʉi pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ ima'ta'pʉ awonsi'kɨ. Mɨrɨ pʉra nin iyesi yau, ipoitorʉ ton uyepʉ mɨrɨ itekepu onanse'na, mɨrɨpan a'tai nin si ka'pon amʉ' pɨ', ‘Sises e'mʉ'sa'kakaa'pʉ man,’ ta to' uya mɨrɨ. Serɨ nin si e'ku'sa' a'tai, wapiya iyesi'pʉ entai rɨ nin si ennakan nɨto' e'to' oton mɨrɨ ipan pe rɨ,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Aya'kɨrɨ'nokon si usoisaai ton atɨ',” ta'pʉ Paire' uya. “Entantɨ', wakʉ pe uruwai' erasuntɨtantɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon nin si utɨ'pʉ mɨrɨ uruwai' piya' erasuntɨse'na. To' uya a'si'pɨtʉ'pʉ wakʉ pe tɨ' pɨ'. Mɨrɨ tʉpo nin si, soisa amʉ' uya erasuntɨto' pe to' uya ikupʉ'pʉ mɨrɨ.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Awanakʉi' kuru rɨ nin si, suntaaka epiya'tɨ pe, Sapa' ema'sa' yau, Meri Mataren mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉron nɨ Meri utɨ'pʉ Sises uruwasii tɨ' akasa' ense'na.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, ɨsɨ pe tʉrʉ'pʉnʉ esi'pʉ, apʉne pʉra Itepuru inserʉʉi u'tɨ esi'pʉ Epʉn poi. Tɨ' akasa' uruwai' piya' itɨ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya tɨ' ama'pʉ imʉra'taai apai, mɨrɨpan po iyereuta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Sirɨn pe iyesi'pʉ kamiri' kasa. Ipon esi'pʉ ipan pe rɨ aimu'ne, sino kasa.</li>
      <li>Erasuntɨ pɨ' si te'san soisa amʉ' etʉipɨtʉ'pʉ ipɨ' ipan pe, mɨrɨpan kon e'tɨtɨtɨ'ka'pʉ to' uta'mo'ka'pʉ iyeri'sa' kon kasa.</li>
      <li>Uri'sami'si amʉ' pɨ' inserʉ uya, “Kenari'nʉntʉu! Sises, to' nʉpokapɨtʉ'pʉ kurusu' pona warinpa auya'nokon tukai' si'tuyai'.</li>
      <li>E'tane ipʉra man serɨ yau. Iye'mʉ'sa'ka'pʉ ta'pʉ tʉuya kasa rɨ. Apʉne, ipata'pʉ entanʉ'tɨ'.</li>
      <li>Inke pʉra ipoitorʉ ton ipana'tɨtantɨ': ‘Iye'mʉ'sa'kasa' man terikʉ'pʉ apai, mɨrɨpan utɨn pɨ' man arawɨrɨ'nokon Kiyarari pona. Mɨrɨ yau ene auya'nokon mɨrɨ.’ Apana'tɨsa' uya 'nokon si mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ inserʉ uya.</li>
      <li>Kamoro si uri'sami'si amʉ' enna'po'pʉ mɨrɨ uruwai' piyapai to' etʉipɨ'sa' esi'pʉ e'tane ipan pe rɨ kanan to' esi'pʉ pori' pe, mɨrɨpan kon utɨ'pʉ teka'tunse ipoitorʉ ton pana'tɨse'na.</li>
      <li>Ite'kwanau pʉra rɨ, Sises uya to' eporo'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya, “Miyarɨ'nokon!” ta'pʉ to' pɨ'. To' utɨ'pʉ ipiya' i'ta pɨ' tʉuta'sii', to' uya apurɨpɨtʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“Kenari'nʉntʉu!” ta'pʉ Sises uya to' pɨ'. “Utonpa ton pɨ' Kiyarari pona entantɨ' ka'tantɨ'; mɨrɨ yau nin si to' uya uyene mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Utɨn pɨ' rɨ uri'sami'si amʉ' e'tane, Sises uruwasii erasuntɨnin nan soisa amʉ' utɨ'pʉ Surusiran pona, mɨrɨpan kon uya tanporo rɨ iye'ku'sa' rʉ'pʉ ekama'pʉ Papa ena' use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Kamoro si Papa ena' use'ma nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru e'seposa' a'tai Esuwerʉ amʉ' epuru ton pokon pe, to' ekoneka'pʉ mɨrɨ ku'to' kon pe tukai'. Soisa amʉ' ena' eke pe rɨ pʉrata tʉrʉ'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Se mɨkatʉi', ‘Ina e'nʉntane, ewarupɨ nau, Sises poitorʉ ton uya itekepu arɨ'pʉ,’ mɨkatʉi'.</li>
      <li>Serɨ etasa' kopʉna uya yau, ɨkota'ma iya 'nokon namai' ina uya auro'ka mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ to' uya to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Soisa amʉ' uya nin si pʉrata a'si'pʉ mɨrɨ; kamoro uya mɨrɨ kasa me'tʉi' tasa' awɨrɨ rɨ to' uya ikupʉ'pʉ. Mɨrɨ uriya', siya rɨ serɨ panton utɨsa' mɨrɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' koro'tau rɨ serɨ pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pata'pʉ pe, 11 kaisaron kon ipoitorʉ ton utɨ'pʉ Kiyarari pona, wʉ' pona, Sises uya, “Mɨrɨ ya' entantɨ',” ta'pʉ rʉ'pʉ pona.</li>
      <li>To' uya ensa' a'tai, to' uya apurɨpɨtʉ'pʉ, e'tane tʉron kon uya ikasima'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Sises uyee'pʉ to' piya', mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Umeruntɨrʉ ke urepasa' man tanporon nɨ Epʉn mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ non poron kon nɨ esa' pe e'to' pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', siya rɨ entantɨ' tanporon kon ka'pon amʉ' ikonekatantɨ' upoitorʉ pe to' e'to' pe. To' ipa'taisimatantɨ' ikʉipʉnʉ, imu, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Wakʉ A'kwarʉ ese' yau.</li>
      <li>To' menupatʉi' tanporon nɨ ayauro'ka'pʉ uya 'nokon awɨron pe to' e'to' pe. I'napai rɨ kuru rɨ ɨpiyau'nokon esi iweyu u'matʉ pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ,” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
</ol>
